import { Toaster as Sonner } from '@/components/ui/sonner';
import { TooltipProvider } from '@/components/ui/tooltip';
import { QueryClient, QueryClientProvider } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { BrowserRouter, Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { useWorkspaceStore } from '@/store/workspaceStore';
import Layout from './components/layout/Layout';
import Dashboard from './pages/Dashboard';
import Projects from './pages/Projects';
import ProjectDetails from './pages/ProjectDetails';
import Team from './pages/Team';
import Auth from './pages/Auth';
import NotFound from './pages/NotFound';
import { Toaster } from 'sonner';

const queryClient = new QueryClient();

function ProtectedRoute({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  const { auth } = useWorkspaceStore();

  if (!auth.isAuthenticated) {
    return <Navigate to='/auth' replace />;
  }

  return <>{children}</>;
}

function AuthRoute({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  const { auth } = useWorkspaceStore();

  if (auth.isAuthenticated) {
    return <Navigate to='/' replace />;
  }

  return <>{children}</>;
}

const App = () => (
  <QueryClientProvider client={queryClient}>
    <TooltipProvider>
      <Toaster />
      <Sonner />
      <BrowserRouter>
        <Routes>
          <Route
            path='/auth'
            element={
              <AuthRoute>
                <Auth />
              </AuthRoute>
            }
          />
          <Route
            element={
              <ProtectedRoute>
                <Layout />
              </ProtectedRoute>
            }
          >
            <Route index element={<Dashboard />} />
            <Route path='projects' element={<Projects />} />
            <Route path='projects/:id' element={<ProjectDetails />} />
            <Route path='team' element={<Team />} />
          </Route>
          <Route path='*' element={<NotFound />} />
        </Routes>
      </BrowserRouter>
    </TooltipProvider>
  </QueryClientProvider>
);

export default App;

/**
 * Dependency Graph Visualization
 * Shows task dependencies as an interactive node-edge graph
 * Supports drag-to-create dependencies between nodes
 */

import { useState, useMemo, useCallback, useRef, useEffect } from 'react';
import { motion } from 'framer-motion';
import {
  ZoomIn,
  ZoomOut,
  Maximize2,
  Move,
  AlertCircle,
  CheckCircle2,
  Clock,
  X,
  Link2,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { useWorkspaceStore, type Task } from '@/store/workspaceStore';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import {
  Tooltip,
  TooltipContent,
  TooltipProvider,
  TooltipTrigger,
} from '@/components/ui/tooltip';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { toast } from 'sonner';

interface DependencyGraphProps {
  tasks: Task[];
  selectedTaskId?: string;
  onTaskClick?: (task: Task) => void;
  onClose?: () => void;
}

interface GraphNode {
  id: string;
  task: Task;
  x: number;
  y: number;
  level: number;
  column: number;
}

interface GraphEdge {
  id: string;
  from: string;
  to: string;
  fromNode: GraphNode;
  toNode: GraphNode;
  isBlocked: boolean;
}

interface DragConnection {
  fromNodeId: string;
  fromX: number;
  fromY: number;
  currentX: number;
  currentY: number;
}

const statusColors: Record<
  string,
  { bg: string; border: string; text: string }
> = {
  TODO: {
    bg: 'bg-muted',
    border: 'border-muted-foreground/50',
    text: 'text-muted-foreground',
  },
  IN_PROGRESS: {
    bg: 'bg-warning/20',
    border: 'border-warning',
    text: 'text-warning',
  },
  REVIEW: {
    bg: 'bg-primary/20',
    border: 'border-primary',
    text: 'text-primary',
  },
  DONE: { bg: 'bg-success/20', border: 'border-success', text: 'text-success' },
};

const priorityIndicators: Record<string, string> = {
  LOW: 'bg-muted-foreground/40',
  MEDIUM: 'bg-warning',
  HIGH: 'bg-destructive/70',
  URGENT: 'bg-destructive',
};

// Helper to detect circular dependencies
const wouldCreateCycle = (
  tasks: Task[],
  fromTaskId: string,
  toTaskId: string,
): boolean => {
  const taskMap = new Map(tasks.map((t) => [t.id, t]));
  const visited = new Set<string>();

  const hasPath = (currentId: string, targetId: string): boolean => {
    if (currentId === targetId) return true;
    if (visited.has(currentId)) return false;

    visited.add(currentId);
    const task = taskMap.get(currentId);
    if (!task) return false;

    // Check blocking relationships (tasks this one blocks)
    for (const blockingId of task.blocking || []) {
      if (hasPath(blockingId, targetId)) return true;
    }

    return false;
  };

  // Check if adding fromTask -> toTask would create a cycle
  // This means checking if there's already a path from toTask to fromTask
  return hasPath(toTaskId, fromTaskId);
};

export default function DependencyGraph({
  tasks,
  selectedTaskId,
  onTaskClick,
  onClose,
}: DependencyGraphProps) {
  const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const svgRef = useRef<SVGSVGElement>(null);
  const updateTask = useWorkspaceStore((state) => state.updateTask);

  const [zoom, setZoom] = useState(1);
  const [pan, setPan] = useState({ x: 0, y: 0 });
  const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);
  const [dragStart, setDragStart] = useState({ x: 0, y: 0 });
  const [hoveredNode, setHoveredNode] = useState<string | null>(null);

  // Drag-to-connect state
  const [dragConnection, setDragConnection] = useState<DragConnection | null>(
    null,
  );
  const [dropTarget, setDropTarget] = useState<string | null>(null);

  // Node dimensions
  const nodeWidth = 200;
  const nodeHeight = 80;
  const horizontalGap = 100;
  const verticalGap = 60;

  // Filter tasks that have dependencies
  const tasksWithDependencies = useMemo(() => {
    return tasks.filter(
      (t) => (t.blockedBy?.length || 0) > 0 || (t.blocking?.length || 0) > 0,
    );
  }, [tasks]);

  // Build the graph layout using topological sorting
  const { nodes, edges, graphWidth, graphHeight } = useMemo(() => {
    if (tasksWithDependencies.length === 0) {
      return { nodes: [], edges: [], graphWidth: 0, graphHeight: 0 };
    }

    const taskMap = new Map(tasks.map((t) => [t.id, t]));
    const nodeMap = new Map<string, GraphNode>();

    // Calculate levels (depth) for each task
    const levels = new Map<string, number>();
    const visited = new Set<string>();

    const calculateLevel = (taskId: string, currentLevel: number): number => {
      if (levels.has(taskId)) {
        return Math.max(levels.get(taskId)!, currentLevel);
      }

      const task = taskMap.get(taskId);
      if (!task) return currentLevel;

      visited.add(taskId);
      let maxLevel = currentLevel;

      // Tasks that block this one should be at a lower level
      task.blockedBy?.forEach((blockerId) => {
        if (!visited.has(blockerId)) {
          const blockerLevel = calculateLevel(blockerId, currentLevel - 1);
          maxLevel = Math.min(maxLevel, blockerLevel + 1);
        }
      });

      levels.set(taskId, maxLevel);
      return maxLevel;
    };

    // Start from tasks that are not blocked by anything (roots)
    const roots = tasksWithDependencies.filter(
      (t) => !t.blockedBy || t.blockedBy.length === 0,
    );

    // If no roots, start from all tasks
    const startTasks = roots.length > 0 ? roots : tasksWithDependencies;

    startTasks.forEach((task) => {
      calculateLevel(task.id, 0);
    });

    // Calculate remaining tasks
    tasksWithDependencies.forEach((task) => {
      if (!levels.has(task.id)) {
        calculateLevel(task.id, 0);
      }
    });

    // Normalize levels to start from 0
    const minLevel = Math.min(...Array.from(levels.values()));
    levels.forEach((level, taskId) => {
      levels.set(taskId, level - minLevel);
    });

    // Group tasks by level
    const levelGroups = new Map<number, Task[]>();
    tasksWithDependencies.forEach((task) => {
      const level = levels.get(task.id) || 0;
      if (!levelGroups.has(level)) {
        levelGroups.set(level, []);
      }
      levelGroups.get(level)!.push(task);
    });

    // Create nodes with positions
    const graphNodes: GraphNode[] = [];
    const maxNodesPerLevel = Math.max(
      ...Array.from(levelGroups.values()).map((g) => g.length),
    );

    levelGroups.forEach((tasksAtLevel, level) => {
      tasksAtLevel.forEach((task, index) => {
        const totalAtLevel = tasksAtLevel.length;
        const startY =
          ((maxNodesPerLevel - totalAtLevel) * (nodeHeight + verticalGap)) / 2;

        const node: GraphNode = {
          id: task.id,
          task,
          x: level * (nodeWidth + horizontalGap) + 50,
          y: startY + index * (nodeHeight + verticalGap) + 50,
          level,
          column: index,
        };

        graphNodes.push(node);
        nodeMap.set(task.id, node);
      });
    });

    // Create edges
    const graphEdges: GraphEdge[] = [];
    tasksWithDependencies.forEach((task) => {
      const toNode = nodeMap.get(task.id);
      if (!toNode) return;

      task.blockedBy?.forEach((blockerId) => {
        const fromNode = nodeMap.get(blockerId);
        if (fromNode) {
          const blockerTask = taskMap.get(blockerId);
          graphEdges.push({
            id: `${blockerId}-${task.id}`,
            from: blockerId,
            to: task.id,
            fromNode,
            toNode,
            isBlocked: task.status === 'TODO' && blockerTask?.status !== 'DONE',
          });
        }
      });
    });

    // Calculate graph dimensions
    const maxLevel = Math.max(...Array.from(levels.values()), 0);
    const width = (maxLevel + 1) * (nodeWidth + horizontalGap) + 100;
    const height = maxNodesPerLevel * (nodeHeight + verticalGap) + 100;

    return {
      nodes: graphNodes,
      edges: graphEdges,
      graphWidth: width,
      graphHeight: height,
    };
  }, [
    tasksWithDependencies,
    tasks,
    nodeWidth,
    nodeHeight,
    horizontalGap,
    verticalGap,
  ]);

  // Get connected nodes for highlighting
  const connectedNodes = useMemo(() => {
    if (!hoveredNode && !selectedTaskId) return new Set<string>();

    const targetId = hoveredNode || selectedTaskId;
    const connected = new Set<string>();

    if (targetId) {
      connected.add(targetId);
      edges.forEach((edge) => {
        if (edge.from === targetId || edge.to === targetId) {
          connected.add(edge.from);
          connected.add(edge.to);
        }
      });
    }

    return connected;
  }, [hoveredNode, selectedTaskId, edges]);

  // Pan handlers (only when not dragging a connection)
  const handleMouseDown = (e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    if (dragConnection) return; // Don't pan while creating connection
    if (
      e.target === containerRef.current ||
      (e.target as HTMLElement).tagName === 'svg'
    ) {
      setIsDragging(true);
      setDragStart({ x: e.clientX - pan.x, y: e.clientY - pan.y });
    }
  };

  const handleMouseMove = useCallback(
    (e: MouseEvent) => {
      if (dragConnection && svgRef.current) {
        // Update drag connection position
        const svgRect = svgRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
        const x = (e.clientX - svgRect.left - pan.x) / zoom;
        const y = (e.clientY - svgRect.top - pan.y) / zoom;
        setDragConnection((prev) =>
          prev ? { ...prev, currentX: x, currentY: y } : null,
        );
      } else if (isDragging) {
        setPan({
          x: e.clientX - dragStart.x,
          y: e.clientY - dragStart.y,
        });
      }
    },
    [isDragging, dragStart, dragConnection, pan, zoom],
  );

  const handleMouseUp = useCallback(() => {
    if (dragConnection && dropTarget) {
      // Create the dependency
      const fromTask = tasks.find((t) => t.id === dragConnection.fromNodeId);
      const toTask = tasks.find((t) => t.id === dropTarget);

      if (fromTask && toTask) {
        // Check if dependency already exists
        if (fromTask.blocking?.includes(dropTarget)) {
          toast.error('This dependency already exists');
        } else if (
          wouldCreateCycle(tasks, dragConnection.fromNodeId, dropTarget)
        ) {
          toast.error('Cannot create circular dependency');
        } else {
          // Create bidirectional relationship
          updateTask({
            ...fromTask,
            blocking: [...(fromTask.blocking || []), dropTarget],
          });
          updateTask({
            ...toTask,
            blockedBy: [...(toTask.blockedBy || []), dragConnection.fromNodeId],
          });
          toast.success('Dependency created', {
            description: `"${fromTask.title}" now blocks "${toTask.title}"`,
          });
        }
      }
    }

    setIsDragging(false);
    setDragConnection(null);
    setDropTarget(null);
  }, [dragConnection, dropTarget, tasks, updateTask]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (isDragging || dragConnection) {
      window.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
      window.addEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
      return () => {
        window.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
        window.removeEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
      };
    }
  }, [isDragging, dragConnection, handleMouseMove, handleMouseUp]);

  // Start dragging a connection from a node
  const handleNodeDragStart = (e: React.MouseEvent, node: GraphNode) => {
    e.stopPropagation();
    const startX = node.x + nodeWidth;
    const startY = node.y + nodeHeight / 2;
    setDragConnection({
      fromNodeId: node.id,
      fromX: startX,
      fromY: startY,
      currentX: startX,
      currentY: startY,
    });
  };

  // Zoom handlers
  const handleZoomIn = () => setZoom((z) => Math.min(z + 0.2, 2));
  const handleZoomOut = () => setZoom((z) => Math.max(z - 0.2, 0.3));
  const handleResetView = () => {
    setZoom(1);
    setPan({ x: 0, y: 0 });
  };

  // Generate edge path
  const getEdgePath = (edge: GraphEdge): string => {
    const fromX = edge.fromNode.x + nodeWidth;
    const fromY = edge.fromNode.y + nodeHeight / 2;
    const toX = edge.toNode.x;
    const toY = edge.toNode.y + nodeHeight / 2;

    const midX = (fromX + toX) / 2;

    // Use bezier curves for smooth connections
    return `M ${fromX} ${fromY} C ${midX} ${fromY}, ${midX} ${toY}, ${toX} ${toY}`;
  };

  if (tasksWithDependencies.length === 0) {
    return (
      <div className='flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-96 text-muted-foreground'>
        <AlertCircle className='w-12 h-12 mb-4 opacity-50' />
        <p className='text-lg font-medium'>No Dependencies Found</p>
        <p className='text-sm mt-1'>Tasks with dependencies will appear here</p>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className='relative w-full h-full min-h-[500px] bg-background rounded-lg border border-border overflow-hidden'>
      {/* Controls */}
      <div className='absolute top-4 left-4 z-20 flex items-center gap-2'>
        <div className='flex items-center gap-1 bg-card/95 backdrop-blur border border-border rounded-lg p-1 shadow-lg'>
          <TooltipProvider>
            <Tooltip>
              <TooltipTrigger asChild>
                <Button
                  variant='ghost'
                  size='icon'
                  className='h-8 w-8'
                  onClick={handleZoomIn}
                >
                  <ZoomIn className='w-4 h-4' />
                </Button>
              </TooltipTrigger>
              <TooltipContent>Zoom In</TooltipContent>
            </Tooltip>
          </TooltipProvider>

          <span className='text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground px-2 min-w-[3rem] text-center'>
            {Math.round(zoom * 100)}%
          </span>

          <TooltipProvider>
            <Tooltip>
              <TooltipTrigger asChild>
                <Button
                  variant='ghost'
                  size='icon'
                  className='h-8 w-8'
                  onClick={handleZoomOut}
                >
                  <ZoomOut className='w-4 h-4' />
                </Button>
              </TooltipTrigger>
              <TooltipContent>Zoom Out</TooltipContent>
            </Tooltip>
          </TooltipProvider>

          <div className='w-px h-6 bg-border' />

          <TooltipProvider>
            <Tooltip>
              <TooltipTrigger asChild>
                <Button
                  variant='ghost'
                  size='icon'
                  className='h-8 w-8'
                  onClick={handleResetView}
                >
                  <Maximize2 className='w-4 h-4' />
                </Button>
              </TooltipTrigger>
              <TooltipContent>Reset View</TooltipContent>
            </Tooltip>
          </TooltipProvider>
        </div>

        <div className='flex items-center gap-2 bg-card/95 backdrop-blur border border-border rounded-lg px-3 py-1.5 shadow-lg'>
          <Move className='w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground' />
          <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>Drag to pan</span>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Close button */}
      {onClose && (
        <Button
          variant='ghost'
          size='icon'
          className='absolute top-4 right-4 z-20 bg-card/95 backdrop-blur border border-border shadow-lg'
          onClick={onClose}
        >
          <X className='w-4 h-4' />
        </Button>
      )}

      {/* Legend */}
      <div className='absolute bottom-4 left-4 z-20 bg-card/95 backdrop-blur border border-border rounded-lg p-3 shadow-lg'>
        <p className='text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground mb-2'>Legend</p>
        <div className='space-y-1.5'>
          <div className='flex items-center gap-2'>
            <Link2 className='w-4 h-4 text-primary' />
            <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
              Drag from node edge to create dependency
            </span>
          </div>
          <div className='flex items-center gap-2'>
            <svg width='24' height='8' className='overflow-visible'>
              <line
                x1='0'
                y1='4'
                x2='18'
                y2='4'
                strokeWidth='2'
                className='stroke-primary'
              />
              <polygon points='18,0 24,4 18,8' className='fill-primary' />
            </svg>
            <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
              Dependency (completed)
            </span>
          </div>
          <div className='flex items-center gap-2'>
            <svg width='24' height='8' className='overflow-visible'>
              <line
                x1='0'
                y1='4'
                x2='18'
                y2='4'
                strokeWidth='2'
                strokeDasharray='4 2'
                className='stroke-destructive'
              />
              <polygon points='18,0 24,4 18,8' className='fill-destructive' />
            </svg>
            <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
              Blocking (waiting)
            </span>
          </div>
          {Object.entries(statusColors).map(([status, colors]) => (
            <div key={status} className='flex items-center gap-2'>
              <div
                className={cn(
                  'w-4 h-4 rounded border-2',
                  colors.bg,
                  colors.border,
                )}
              />
              <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                {status.replace('_', ' ')}
              </span>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Stats */}
      <div className='absolute top-4 right-16 z-20 bg-card/95 backdrop-blur border border-border rounded-lg px-3 py-2 shadow-lg'>
        <div className='flex items-center gap-4 text-xs'>
          <div>
            <span className='text-muted-foreground'>Tasks: </span>
            <span className='font-medium text-foreground'>{nodes.length}</span>
          </div>
          <div>
            <span className='text-muted-foreground'>Dependencies: </span>
            <span className='font-medium text-foreground'>{edges.length}</span>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Graph Canvas */}
      <div
        ref={containerRef}
        className={cn(
          'w-full h-full overflow-hidden',
          isDragging ? 'cursor-grabbing' : 'cursor-grab',
        )}
        onMouseDown={handleMouseDown}
      >
        <svg
          ref={svgRef}
          width={graphWidth * zoom + 200}
          height={graphHeight * zoom + 200}
          style={{
            transform: `translate(${pan.x}px, ${pan.y}px) scale(${zoom})`,
            transformOrigin: '0 0',
          }}
          className='transition-transform duration-100'
        >
          <defs>
            <marker
              id='arrow-normal'
              markerWidth='10'
              markerHeight='10'
              refX='8'
              refY='5'
              orient='auto'
            >
              <path d='M 0 0 L 10 5 L 0 10 L 3 5 Z' className='fill-primary' />
            </marker>
            <marker
              id='arrow-blocked'
              markerWidth='10'
              markerHeight='10'
              refX='8'
              refY='5'
              orient='auto'
            >
              <path
                d='M 0 0 L 10 5 L 0 10 L 3 5 Z'
                className='fill-destructive'
              />
            </marker>
            <marker
              id='arrow-dimmed'
              markerWidth='10'
              markerHeight='10'
              refX='8'
              refY='5'
              orient='auto'
            >
              <path
                d='M 0 0 L 10 5 L 0 10 L 3 5 Z'
                className='fill-muted-foreground/30'
              />
            </marker>
            <marker
              id='arrow-dragging'
              markerWidth='10'
              markerHeight='10'
              refX='8'
              refY='5'
              orient='auto'
            >
              <path d='M 0 0 L 10 5 L 0 10 L 3 5 Z' className='fill-primary' />
            </marker>
          </defs>

          {/* Edges */}
          <g>
            {edges.map((edge) => {
              const isHighlighted =
                connectedNodes.size === 0 ||
                (connectedNodes.has(edge.from) && connectedNodes.has(edge.to));
              const isDimmed = connectedNodes.size > 0 && !isHighlighted;

              return (
                <motion.path
                  key={edge.id}
                  initial={{ pathLength: 0, opacity: 0 }}
                  animate={{ pathLength: 1, opacity: isDimmed ? 0.2 : 1 }}
                  transition={{ duration: 0.5 }}
                  d={getEdgePath(edge)}
                  fill='none'
                  className={cn(
                    'transition-all duration-200',
                    isDimmed
                      ? 'stroke-muted-foreground/30'
                      : edge.isBlocked
                        ? 'stroke-destructive'
                        : 'stroke-primary',
                  )}
                  strokeWidth={isHighlighted && !isDimmed ? 2.5 : 2}
                  strokeDasharray={edge.isBlocked && !isDimmed ? '6 3' : 'none'}
                  markerEnd={`url(#${isDimmed ? 'arrow-dimmed' : edge.isBlocked ? 'arrow-blocked' : 'arrow-normal'})`}
                />
              );
            })}
          </g>

          {/* Dragging connection line */}
          {dragConnection && (
            <g>
              <motion.path
                initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
                animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
                d={`M ${dragConnection.fromX} ${dragConnection.fromY} 
                    C ${(dragConnection.fromX + dragConnection.currentX) / 2} ${dragConnection.fromY}, 
                      ${(dragConnection.fromX + dragConnection.currentX) / 2} ${dragConnection.currentY}, 
                      ${dragConnection.currentX} ${dragConnection.currentY}`}
                fill='none'
                className='stroke-primary'
                strokeWidth={2.5}
                strokeDasharray='6 3'
                markerEnd='url(#arrow-dragging)'
              />
              {/* Source indicator */}
              <circle
                cx={dragConnection.fromX}
                cy={dragConnection.fromY}
                r={6}
                className='fill-primary'
              />
            </g>
          )}

          {/* Nodes */}
          <g>
            {nodes.map((node) => {
              const isSelected = selectedTaskId === node.id;
              const isHovered = hoveredNode === node.id;
              const isHighlighted =
                connectedNodes.size === 0 || connectedNodes.has(node.id);
              const isDimmed = connectedNodes.size > 0 && !isHighlighted;
              const colors = statusColors[node.task.status];
              const isDropCandidate =
                dragConnection && dragConnection.fromNodeId !== node.id;
              const isActiveDropTarget = dropTarget === node.id;

              return (
                <g
                  key={node.id}
                  transform={`translate(${node.x}, ${node.y})`}
                  className='cursor-pointer'
                  onMouseEnter={() => {
                    setHoveredNode(node.id);
                    if (isDropCandidate) {
                      setDropTarget(node.id);
                    }
                  }}
                  onMouseLeave={() => {
                    setHoveredNode(null);
                    if (dropTarget === node.id) {
                      setDropTarget(null);
                    }
                  }}
                  onClick={() => onTaskClick?.(node.task)}
                >
                  {/* Drop target highlight */}
                  {isActiveDropTarget && (
                    <motion.rect
                      initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 1.05 }}
                      animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1.08 }}
                      transition={{ duration: 0.2 }}
                      x={-6}
                      y={-6}
                      width={nodeWidth + 12}
                      height={nodeHeight + 12}
                      rx={12}
                      className='fill-primary/20 stroke-primary'
                      strokeWidth={2}
                      strokeDasharray='4 2'
                    />
                  )}

                  {/* Node background */}
                  <motion.rect
                    initial={{ scale: 0, opacity: 0 }}
                    animate={{
                      scale: 1,
                      opacity: isDimmed ? 0.3 : 1,
                    }}
                    transition={{ duration: 0.3, delay: node.level * 0.1 }}
                    width={nodeWidth}
                    height={nodeHeight}
                    rx={8}
                    className={cn(
                      'transition-all duration-200',
                      colors.bg,
                      'stroke-2',
                      isSelected || isHovered
                        ? 'stroke-primary'
                        : colors.border,
                      isActiveDropTarget && 'stroke-primary',
                    )}
                    strokeWidth={
                      isSelected || isHovered || isActiveDropTarget ? 3 : 2
                    }
                    filter={
                      isSelected || isHovered
                        ? 'drop-shadow(0 4px 12px rgba(0,0,0,0.15))'
                        : 'none'
                    }
                  />

                  {/* Priority indicator */}
                  <rect
                    x={0}
                    y={0}
                    width={4}
                    height={nodeHeight}
                    rx={2}
                    className={priorityIndicators[node.task.priority]}
                  />

                  {/* Connection drag handle (right side) */}
                  <g
                    transform={`translate(${nodeWidth - 4}, ${nodeHeight / 2 - 12})`}
                    className='cursor-crosshair'
                    onMouseDown={(e) => handleNodeDragStart(e, node)}
                  >
                    <rect
                      x={0}
                      y={0}
                      width={12}
                      height={24}
                      rx={4}
                      className={cn(
                        'transition-all duration-200',
                        isHovered ? 'fill-primary' : 'fill-primary/50',
                      )}
                    />
                    <circle cx={6} cy={8} r={2} className='fill-background' />
                    <circle cx={6} cy={16} r={2} className='fill-background' />
                  </g>

                  {/* Connection target handle (left side) - shows during drag */}
                  {isDropCandidate && (
                    <g transform={`translate(-8, ${nodeHeight / 2 - 12})`}>
                      <motion.rect
                        initial={{ opacity: 0, x: 4 }}
                        animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
                        x={0}
                        y={0}
                        width={12}
                        height={24}
                        rx={4}
                        className={cn(
                          'transition-colors duration-200',
                          isActiveDropTarget
                            ? 'fill-primary'
                            : 'fill-primary/30',
                        )}
                      />
                      <circle
                        cx={6}
                        cy={12}
                        r={3}
                        className={cn(
                          'transition-colors duration-200',
                          isActiveDropTarget
                            ? 'fill-background'
                            : 'fill-background/70',
                        )}
                      />
                    </g>
                  )}

                  {/* Status icon */}
                  <g transform={`translate(${nodeWidth - 36}, 12)`}>
                    {node.task.status === 'DONE' ? (
                      <circle
                        r={10}
                        cx={10}
                        cy={10}
                        className='fill-success/20'
                      />
                    ) : node.task.status === 'IN_PROGRESS' ? (
                      <circle
                        r={10}
                        cx={10}
                        cy={10}
                        className='fill-warning/20'
                      />
                    ) : null}
                    <foreignObject x={2} y={2} width={16} height={16}>
                      {node.task.status === 'DONE' ? (
                        <CheckCircle2 className='w-4 h-4 text-success' />
                      ) : node.task.status === 'IN_PROGRESS' ? (
                        <Clock className='w-4 h-4 text-warning' />
                      ) : null}
                    </foreignObject>
                  </g>

                  {/* Task title */}
                  <foreignObject
                    x={12}
                    y={12}
                    width={nodeWidth - 58}
                    height={24}
                  >
                    <p
                      className={cn(
                        'text-sm font-medium truncate',
                        node.task.status === 'DONE'
                          ? 'line-through text-muted-foreground'
                          : 'text-foreground',
                      )}
                      title={node.task.title}
                    >
                      {node.task.title}
                    </p>
                  </foreignObject>

                  {/* Task metadata */}
                  <foreignObject
                    x={12}
                    y={40}
                    width={nodeWidth - 24}
                    height={30}
                  >
                    <div className='flex items-center gap-2'>
                      <span
                        className={cn(
                          'text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded font-medium',
                          colors.bg,
                          colors.text,
                        )}
                      >
                        {node.task.status.replace('_', ' ')}
                      </span>
                      <span className='text-[10px] text-muted-foreground'>
                        {node.task.assignee?.name}
                      </span>
                    </div>
                  </foreignObject>

                  {/* Dependency counts */}
                  <foreignObject
                    x={12}
                    y={nodeHeight - 22}
                    width={nodeWidth - 24}
                    height={18}
                  >
                    <div className='flex items-center gap-3 text-[10px] text-muted-foreground'>
                      {(node.task.blockedBy?.length || 0) > 0 && (
                        <span className='flex items-center gap-1'>
                          <AlertCircle className='w-3 h-3 text-destructive' />
                          {node.task.blockedBy?.length} blocker(s)
                        </span>
                      )}
                      {(node.task.blocking?.length || 0) > 0 && (
                        <span className='flex items-center gap-1'>
                          <span className='w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-primary' />
                          Blocks {node.task.blocking?.length}
                        </span>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </foreignObject>
                </g>
              );
            })}
          </g>
        </svg>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

/**
 * Dialog for choosing to edit a single occurrence or entire series
 */

import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import { Calendar, Repeat, X } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';

export type EditScope = 'single' | 'series';

interface EditOccurrenceDialogProps {
  open: boolean;
  onClose: () => void;
  onSelect: (scope: EditScope) => void;
  taskTitle: string;
  action: 'edit' | 'delete';
}

export function EditOccurrenceDialog({
  open,
  onClose,
  onSelect,
  taskTitle,
  action,
}: EditOccurrenceDialogProps) {
  const actionText = action === 'edit' ? 'Edit' : 'Delete';
  const actionTextLower = action === 'edit' ? 'edit' : 'delete';

  return (
    <AnimatePresence>
      {open && (
        <>
          {/* Backdrop */}
          <motion.div
            initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
            className='fixed inset-0 bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-sm z-50'
            onClick={onClose}
          />

          {/* Dialog */}
          <motion.div
            initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95, y: 20 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1, y: 0 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95, y: 20 }}
            className='fixed left-1/2 top-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 z-50 w-full max-w-md'
          >
            <div className='glass-card mx-4 p-6'>
              {/* Header */}
              <div className='flex items-center justify-between mb-4'>
                <div className='flex items-center gap-3'>
                  <div className='p-2 rounded-lg bg-primary/10'>
                    <Repeat className='w-5 h-5 text-primary' />
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    <h2 className='text-lg font-semibold text-foreground'>
                      {actionText} Recurring Task
                    </h2>
                    <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground truncate max-w-[200px]'>
                      {taskTitle}
                    </p>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <Button variant='ghost' size='icon' onClick={onClose}>
                  <X className='w-5 h-5' />
                </Button>
              </div>

              {/* Content */}
              <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-6'>
                This is a recurring task. Would you like to {actionTextLower}{' '}
                only this occurrence or the entire series?
              </p>

              {/* Options */}
              <div className='space-y-3'>
                <button
                  onClick={() => onSelect('single')}
                  className='w-full p-4 rounded-lg border border-border bg-secondary/30 hover:bg-secondary/50 transition-colors text-left group'
                >
                  <div className='flex items-center gap-3'>
                    <div className='p-2 rounded-lg bg-muted group-hover:bg-muted-foreground/10 transition-colors'>
                      <Calendar className='w-5 h-5 text-muted-foreground' />
                    </div>
                    <div>
                      <p className='font-medium text-foreground'>
                        {actionText} this occurrence only
                      </p>
                      <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>
                        Other occurrences will remain unchanged
                      </p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </button>

                <button
                  onClick={() => onSelect('series')}
                  className='w-full p-4 rounded-lg border border-border bg-secondary/30 hover:bg-secondary/50 transition-colors text-left group'
                >
                  <div className='flex items-center gap-3'>
                    <div className='p-2 rounded-lg bg-muted group-hover:bg-primary/10 transition-colors'>
                      <Repeat className='w-5 h-5 text-primary' />
                    </div>
                    <div>
                      <p className='font-medium text-foreground'>
                        {actionText} entire series
                      </p>
                      <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>
                        {action === 'edit'
                          ? 'Changes will apply to all occurrences'
                          : 'All occurrences will be deleted'}
                      </p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </button>
              </div>

              {/* Cancel */}
              <div className='mt-4 text-center'>
                <Button variant='ghost' size='sm' onClick={onClose}>
                  Cancel
                </Button>
              </div>
            </div>
          </motion.div>
        </>
      )}
    </AnimatePresence>
  );
}
