// Drag Overlay Task Component
function DragOverlayTask({ task }: { task: Task }) {
  const isOverdue =
    safeParseDate(task.due_date) &&
    isBefore(safeParseDate(task.due_date)!, new Date()) &&
    task.status !== 'DONE';

  return (
    <div
      className={cn(
        'px-3 py-2 rounded-lg border-l-2 transition-colors cursor-grabbing shadow-xl',
        'bg-secondary border border-border',
        priorityBorders[task.priority],
        task.status === 'DONE' && 'opacity-60',
        isOverdue && 'bg-destructive/10',
      )}
    >
      <div className='flex items-center gap-2'>
        <GripVertical className='w-3 h-3 text-muted-foreground' />
        <span
          className={cn(
            'w-2 h-2 rounded-full flex-shrink-0',
            statusColors[task.status],
          )}
        />
        <span
          className={cn(
            'font-medium text-sm text-foreground',
            task.status === 'DONE' && 'line-through',
          )}
        >
          {task.title}
        </span>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export default function TaskCalendar({
  tasks,
  onTaskClick,
  onCreateTask,
}: TaskCalendarProps) {
  const [currentDate, setCurrentDate] = useState(new Date());
  const [selectedDate, setSelectedDate] = useState<Date | null>(null);
  const [viewMode, setViewMode] = useState<ViewMode>('month');
  const [activeTask, setActiveTask] = useState<Task | null>(null);
  const [selectedTask, setSelectedTask] = useState<Task | null>(null);
  const [selectedTaskIndex, setSelectedTaskIndex] = useState<number>(-1);
  const [filters, setFilters] = useState<Filters>({
    priorities: [],
    statuses: [],
    assigneeIds: [],
  });
  const [filterOpen, setFilterOpen] = useState(false);
  const [presets, setPresets] = useState<FilterPreset[]>([]);
  const [newPresetName, setNewPresetName] = useState('');
  const [showSavePreset, setShowSavePreset] = useState(false);

  const updateTask = useWorkspaceStore((state) => state.updateTask);
  const deleteTask = useWorkspaceStore((state) => state.deleteTask);

  // Load presets from localStorage on mount
  useEffect(() => {
    try {
      const stored = localStorage.getItem(PRESETS_STORAGE_KEY);
      if (stored) {
        setPresets(JSON.parse(stored));
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.error('Failed to load filter presets:', e);
    }
  }, []);

  // Save presets to localStorage whenever they change
  useEffect(() => {
    try {
      localStorage.setItem(PRESETS_STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(presets));
    } catch (e) {
      console.error('Failed to save filter presets:', e);
    }
  }, [presets]);

  // Get unique assignees from tasks
  const uniqueAssignees = useMemo(() => {
    const assigneeMap = new Map<
      string,
      { id: string; name: string; image: string }
    >();
    tasks.forEach((task) => {
      if (task.assignee && !assigneeMap.has(task.assigneeId)) {
        assigneeMap.set(task.assigneeId, {
          id: task.assigneeId,
          name: task.assignee.name,
          image: task.assignee.image,
        });
      }
    });
    return Array.from(assigneeMap.values());
  }, [tasks]);

  // Filter tasks based on active filters
  const filteredTasks = useMemo(() => {
    return tasks.filter((task) => {
      const priorityMatch =
        filters.priorities.length === 0 ||
        filters.priorities.includes(task.priority);
      const statusMatch =
        filters.statuses.length === 0 || filters.statuses.includes(task.status);
      const assigneeMatch =
        filters.assigneeIds.length === 0 ||
        filters.assigneeIds.includes(task.assigneeId);
      return priorityMatch && statusMatch && assigneeMatch;
    });
  }, [tasks, filters]);

  const activeFiltersCount =
    filters.priorities.length +
    filters.statuses.length +
    filters.assigneeIds.length;

  const toggleFilter = (type: keyof Filters, value: string) => {
    setFilters((prev) => {
      const currentValues = prev[type] as string[];
      const newValues = currentValues.includes(value)
        ? currentValues.filter((v) => v !== value)
        : [...currentValues, value];
      return { ...prev, [type]: newValues };
    });
  };

  const clearFilters = () => {
    setFilters({ priorities: [], statuses: [], assigneeIds: [] });
  };

  const savePreset = () => {
    if (!newPresetName.trim() || activeFiltersCount === 0) return;

    const newPreset: FilterPreset = {
      id: crypto.randomUUID(),
      name: newPresetName.trim(),
      filters: { ...filters },
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    };

    setPresets((prev) => [...prev, newPreset]);
    setNewPresetName('');
    setShowSavePreset(false);
  };

  const loadPreset = (preset: FilterPreset) => {
    setFilters(preset.filters);
  };

  const deletePreset = (presetId: string) => {
    setPresets((prev) => prev.filter((p) => p.id !== presetId));
  };

  const getPresetDescription = (preset: FilterPreset) => {
    const parts: string[] = [];
    if (preset.filters.priorities.length > 0) {
      parts.push(`${preset.filters.priorities.length} priority`);
    }
    if (preset.filters.statuses.length > 0) {
      parts.push(`${preset.filters.statuses.length} status`);
    }
    if (preset.filters.assigneeIds.length > 0) {
      parts.push(`${preset.filters.assigneeIds.length} assignee`);
    }
    return parts.join(', ') || 'No filters';
  };

  const sensors = useSensors(
    useSensor(PointerSensor, {
      activationConstraint: {
        distance: 8,
      },
    }),
  );

  // Get calendar days based on view mode
  const calendarDays = useMemo(() => {
    if (viewMode === 'day') {
      return [currentDate];
    }
    if (viewMode === 'week') {
      const weekStart = startOfWeek(currentDate);
      const weekEnd = endOfWeek(currentDate);
      return eachDayOfInterval({ start: weekStart, end: weekEnd });
    }

    const monthStart = startOfMonth(currentDate);
    const monthEnd = endOfMonth(currentDate);
    const calendarStart = startOfWeek(monthStart);
    const calendarEnd = endOfWeek(monthEnd);

    return eachDayOfInterval({ start: calendarStart, end: calendarEnd });
  }, [currentDate, viewMode]);

  // Group tasks by date (using filtered tasks)
  const tasksByDate = useMemo(() => {
    const grouped: Record<string, Task[]> = {};

    filteredTasks.forEach((task) => {
      const dueDate = safeParseDate(task.due_date);
      if (dueDate) {
        const dateKey = format(dueDate, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
        if (!grouped[dateKey]) {
          grouped[dateKey] = [];
        }
        grouped[dateKey].push(task);
      }
    });

    return grouped;
  }, [filteredTasks]);

  // Get tasks for current day view, grouped by hour
  const dayViewTasks = useMemo(() => {
    const dateKey = format(currentDate, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    return tasksByDate[dateKey] || [];
  }, [currentDate, tasksByDate]);

  // Group tasks by hour for day view
  const tasksByHour = useMemo(() => {
    const grouped: Record<number, Task[]> = {};
    const unscheduled: Task[] = [];

    dayViewTasks.forEach((task) => {
      const taskHour = parseTimeToHour(task.due_time);
      if (taskHour !== null && taskHour >= 6 && taskHour <= 23) {
        if (!grouped[taskHour]) {
          grouped[taskHour] = [];
        }
        grouped[taskHour].push(task);
      } else {
        unscheduled.push(task);
      }
    });

    return { grouped, unscheduled };
  }, [dayViewTasks]);

  // Get tasks for selected date
  const selectedDateTasks = useMemo(() => {
    if (!selectedDate) return [];
    const dateKey = format(selectedDate, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    return tasksByDate[dateKey] || [];
  }, [selectedDate, tasksByDate]);

  const navigate = useCallback(
    (direction: 'prev' | 'next') => {
      if (viewMode === 'day') {
        setCurrentDate((prev) =>
          direction === 'prev' ? subDays(prev, 1) : addDays(prev, 1),
        );
      } else if (viewMode === 'week') {
        setCurrentDate((prev) =>
          direction === 'prev' ? subWeeks(prev, 1) : addWeeks(prev, 1),
        );
      } else if (viewMode === 'month') {
        setCurrentDate((prev) =>
          direction === 'prev' ? subMonths(prev, 1) : addMonths(prev, 1),
        );
      }
      // Gantt view handles its own navigation
    },
    [viewMode],
  );

  const goToToday = useCallback(() => {
    setCurrentDate(new Date());
    setSelectedDate(new Date());
  }, []);

  const handleViewChange = useCallback((view: ViewMode) => {
    setViewMode(view);
  }, []);

  const handleEditSelectedTask = useCallback(() => {
    if (selectedTask) {
      onTaskClick?.(selectedTask);
    }
  }, [selectedTask, onTaskClick]);

  const handleDeleteSelectedTask = useCallback(() => {
    if (selectedTask) {
      deleteTask([selectedTask.id]);
      setSelectedTask(null);
      setSelectedTaskIndex(-1);
    }
  }, [selectedTask, deleteTask]);

  const handleNavigateTaskUp = useCallback(() => {
    if (filteredTasks.length === 0) return;
    const newIndex =
      selectedTaskIndex <= 0 ? filteredTasks.length - 1 : selectedTaskIndex - 1;
    setSelectedTaskIndex(newIndex);
    setSelectedTask(filteredTasks[newIndex]);
  }, [filteredTasks, selectedTaskIndex]);

  const handleNavigateTaskDown = useCallback(() => {
    if (filteredTasks.length === 0) return;
    const newIndex =
      selectedTaskIndex >= filteredTasks.length - 1 ? 0 : selectedTaskIndex + 1;
    setSelectedTaskIndex(newIndex);
    setSelectedTask(filteredTasks[newIndex]);
  }, [filteredTasks, selectedTaskIndex]);

  const handleEscape = useCallback(() => {
    setSelectedTask(null);
    setSelectedTaskIndex(-1);
  }, []);

  const handleFocusFilters = useCallback(() => {
    setFilterOpen(true);
  }, []);

  // Keyboard shortcuts
  const { showHelpModal, setShowHelpModal } = useKeyboardShortcuts({
    onCreateTask,
    onEditTask: handleEditSelectedTask,
    onDeleteTask: handleDeleteSelectedTask,
    onNavigatePrev: () => navigate('prev'),
    onNavigateNext: () => navigate('next'),
    onGoToToday: goToToday,
    onViewChange: handleViewChange,
    onFocusFilters: handleFocusFilters,
    onEscape: handleEscape,
    onNavigateTaskUp: handleNavigateTaskUp,
    onNavigateTaskDown: handleNavigateTaskDown,
    enabled: viewMode !== 'gantt', // Let Gantt handle its own navigation
  });

  const getHeaderTitle = () => {
    if (viewMode === 'day') {
      return format(currentDate, 'EEEE, MMMM d, yyyy');
    }
    if (viewMode === 'week') {
      const weekStart = startOfWeek(currentDate);
      const weekEnd = endOfWeek(currentDate);
      return `${format(weekStart, 'MMM d')} - ${format(weekEnd, 'MMM d, yyyy')}`;
    }
    if (viewMode === 'gantt') {
      return 'Gantt Timeline';
    }
    return format(currentDate, 'MMMM yyyy');
  };

  const weekDays = ['Sun', 'Mon', 'Tue', 'Wed', 'Thu', 'Fri', 'Sat'];

  // Handle drag start
  const handleDragStart = (event: DragStartEvent) => {
    const task = event.active.data.current?.task as Task;
    if (task) {
      setActiveTask(task);
    }
  };

  // Handle drag end
  const handleDragEnd = (event: DragEndEvent) => {
    const { active, over } = event;
    setActiveTask(null);

    if (!over) return;

    const task = active.data.current?.task as Task;
    if (!task) return;

    const dropData = over.data.current;
    if (!dropData) return;

    let newDueDate = task.due_date;
    let newDueTime = task.due_time;

    if (dropData.type === 'date') {
      // Dropped on a date cell (month/week view)
      newDueDate = `${dropData.dateKey}T00:00:00.000Z`;
      // Keep existing time if any
    } else if (dropData.type === 'hour') {
      // Dropped on an hour slot (day view)
      newDueDate = `${dropData.dateKey}T00:00:00.000Z`;
      newDueTime = `${String(dropData.hour).padStart(2, '0')}:00`;
    } else if (dropData.type === 'unscheduled') {
      // Dropped on unscheduled section
      newDueDate = `${dropData.dateKey}T00:00:00.000Z`;
      newDueTime = undefined;
    }

    // Only update if something changed
    if (newDueDate !== task.due_date || newDueTime !== task.due_time) {
      const updatedTask: Task = {
        ...task,
        due_date: newDueDate,
        due_time: newDueTime,
        updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      };
      updateTask(updatedTask);
    }
  };

  // Render day view with hourly time slots
  const renderDayView = () => {
    const currentHour = getHours(new Date());
    const dateKey = format(currentDate, 'yyyy-MM-dd');

    return (
      <div className='glass-card p-6'>
        {/* Day header */}
        <div className='flex items-center justify-between mb-4 pb-4 border-b border-border'>
          <div className='flex items-center gap-3'>
            <div
              className={cn(
                'w-14 h-14 rounded-xl flex flex-col items-center justify-center',
                isToday(currentDate)
                  ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground'
                  : 'bg-secondary',
              )}
            >
              <span className='text-xs font-medium'>
                {format(currentDate, 'EEE')}
              </span>
              <span className='text-xl font-bold'>
                {format(currentDate, 'd')}
              </span>
            </div>
            <div>
              <h3 className='font-semibold text-foreground'>
                {format(currentDate, 'MMMM yyyy')}
              </h3>
              <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>
                {dayViewTasks.length} task{dayViewTasks.length !== 1 ? 's' : ''}{' '}
                scheduled
                <span className='text-xs ml-2 text-primary'>
                  (drag tasks to reschedule)
                </span>
              </p>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Unscheduled tasks (no time set) */}
        <DroppableUnscheduled
          dateKey={dateKey}
          className='mb-4 p-3 bg-secondary/30 rounded-lg border border-border min-h-[60px]'
        >
          <div className='flex items-center gap-2 mb-2'>
            <Clock className='w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground' />
            <span className='text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground'>
              All Day / No Time Set
            </span>
          </div>
          <div className='space-y-1.5'>
            {tasksByHour.unscheduled.map((task) => {
              const isOverdue =
                safeParseDate(task.due_date) &&
                isBefore(safeParseDate(task.due_date)!, new Date()) &&
                task.status !== 'DONE';

              return (
                <DraggableTask
                  key={task.id}
                  task={task}
                  onTaskClick={onTaskClick}
                  variant='unscheduled'
                  isOverdue={isOverdue}
                  isSelected={selectedTask?.id === task.id}
                />
              );
            })}
            {tasksByHour.unscheduled.length === 0 && (
              <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground italic'>
                Drop tasks here to remove time
              </p>
            )}
          </div>
        </DroppableUnscheduled>

        {/* Time slots */}
        <ScrollArea className='h-[600px]'>
          <div className='relative'>
            {HOURS.map((hour) => {
              const hourTime = setHours(currentDate, hour);
              const isCurrentHour =
                isToday(currentDate) && hour === currentHour;

              // Get tasks scheduled for this specific hour
              const hourTasks = tasksByHour.grouped[hour] || [];

              return (
                <DroppableHourSlot
                  key={hour}
                  dateKey={dateKey}
                  hour={hour}
                  className={cn(
                    'flex border-t border-border min-h-[60px]',
                    isCurrentHour && 'bg-primary/5',
                    hourTasks.length > 0 && 'min-h-[80px]',
                  )}
                >
                  {/* Time label */}
                  <div className='w-20 flex-shrink-0 py-2 pr-4 text-right'>
                    <span
                      className={cn(
                        'text-xs font-medium',
                        isCurrentHour
                          ? 'text-primary'
                          : 'text-muted-foreground',
                      )}
                    >
                      {format(hourTime, 'h a')}
                    </span>
                  </div>

                  {/* Time slot content */}
                  <div className='flex-1 py-1 pl-4 border-l border-border relative'>
                    {/* Current time indicator */}
                    {isCurrentHour && (
                      <div className='absolute left-0 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-full flex items-center z-10 pointer-events-none'>
                        <div className='w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-destructive -ml-1' />
                        <div className='flex-1 h-0.5 bg-destructive/50' />
                      </div>
                    )}

                    {/* Tasks at this hour */}
                    <div className='space-y-1.5'>
                      {hourTasks.map((task) => {
                        const isOverdue =
                          safeParseDate(task.due_date) &&
                          isBefore(safeParseDate(task.due_date)!, new Date()) &&
                          task.status !== 'DONE';

                        return (
                          <DraggableTask
                            key={task.id}
                            task={task}
                            onTaskClick={onTaskClick}
                            variant='day'
                            isOverdue={isOverdue}
                            isSelected={selectedTask?.id === task.id}
                          />
                        );
                      })}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </DroppableHourSlot>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        </ScrollArea>

        {/* Legend */}
        <div className='flex flex-wrap items-center gap-4 mt-6 pt-4 border-t border-border'>
          <div className='flex items-center gap-2 text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
            <span
              className={cn('w-2.5 h-2.5 rounded-full', statusColors.TODO)}
            />
            To Do
          </div>
          <div className='flex items-center gap-2 text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
            <span
              className={cn(
                'w-2.5 h-2.5 rounded-full',
                statusColors.IN_PROGRESS,
              )}
            />
            In Progress
          </div>
          <div className='flex items-center gap-2 text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
            <span
              className={cn('w-2.5 h-2.5 rounded-full', statusColors.REVIEW)}
            />
            Review
          </div>
          <div className='flex items-center gap-2 text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
            <span
              className={cn('w-2.5 h-2.5 rounded-full', statusColors.DONE)}
            />
            Done
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  };

  // Render month/week view
  const renderMonthWeekView = () => (
    <div className='glass-card p-6'>
      {/* Week day headers */}
      <div className='grid grid-cols-7 mb-3'>
        {weekDays.map((day) => (
          <div
            key={day}
            className='text-center text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground py-2 border-b border-border'
          >
            {day}
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Calendar days */}
      <div
        className={cn(
          'grid grid-cols-7 gap-1',
          viewMode === 'week' && 'min-h-[400px]',
        )}
      >
        {calendarDays.map((day, index) => {
          const dateKey = format(day, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
          const dayTasks = tasksByDate[dateKey] || [];
          const isCurrentMonth =
            viewMode === 'week' || isSameMonth(day, currentDate);
          const isSelected = selectedDate && isSameDay(day, selectedDate);
          const isDayToday = isToday(day);
          const hasOverdue = dayTasks.some((t) => {
            const dueDate = safeParseDate(t.due_date);
            return (
              dueDate && isBefore(dueDate, new Date()) && t.status !== 'DONE'
            );
          });

          // Week view shows more tasks
          const maxVisibleTasks = viewMode === 'week' ? 8 : 3;

          return (
            <DroppableDateCell
              key={index}
              dateKey={dateKey}
              className={cn(
                'relative p-2 rounded-lg transition-all cursor-pointer border',
                viewMode === 'week' ? 'min-h-[400px]' : 'min-h-[120px]',
                isCurrentMonth
                  ? 'bg-secondary/20 border-border/50'
                  : 'bg-secondary/5 border-transparent',
                isSelected &&
                  'ring-2 ring-primary bg-primary/5 border-primary/30',
                isDayToday &&
                  !isSelected &&
                  'ring-2 ring-primary/50 border-primary/20',
                'hover:bg-secondary/40',
              )}
            >
              <div
                onClick={() => setSelectedDate(day)}
                onDoubleClick={() => {
                  setCurrentDate(day);
                  setViewMode('day');
                }}
                className='h-full'
              >
                {/* Date header */}
                <div className='flex items-center justify-between mb-2'>
                  <div className='flex flex-col'>
                    <span
                      className={cn(
                        'text-sm font-medium w-7 h-7 flex items-center justify-center rounded-full',
                        !isCurrentMonth && 'text-muted-foreground/40',
                        isDayToday && 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground',
                        isSelected && !isDayToday && 'bg-foreground/10',
                      )}
                    >
                      {format(day, 'd')}
                    </span>
                    {viewMode === 'week' && (
                      <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1 ml-1'>
                        {format(day, 'EEE')}
                      </span>
                    )}
                  </div>

                  {/* Overdue indicator */}
                  {hasOverdue && (
                    <AlertTriangle className='w-4 h-4 text-destructive' />
                  )}
                </div>

                {/* Task list in cell */}
                <div
                  className={cn(
                    'space-y-1 overflow-hidden',
                    viewMode === 'week' && 'space-y-1.5',
                  )}
                >
                  {dayTasks.slice(0, maxVisibleTasks).map((task) => {
                    const isOverdue =
                      safeParseDate(task.due_date) &&
                      isBefore(safeParseDate(task.due_date)!, new Date()) &&
                      task.status !== 'DONE';

                    return (
                      <DraggableTask
                        key={task.id}
                        task={task}
                        onTaskClick={onTaskClick}
                        variant={viewMode as 'month' | 'week'}
                        isOverdue={isOverdue}
                        isSelected={selectedTask?.id === task.id}
                      />
                    );
                  })}
                  {dayTasks.length > maxVisibleTasks && (
                    <div className='text-[10px] text-muted-foreground px-2 font-medium'>
                      +{dayTasks.length - maxVisibleTasks} more
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>
            </DroppableDateCell>
          );
        })}
      </div>

      {/* Legend */}
      <div className='flex flex-wrap items-center gap-4 mt-6 pt-4 border-t border-border'>
        <div className='flex items-center gap-2 text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
          <span className={cn('w-2.5 h-2.5 rounded-full', statusColors.TODO)} />
          To Do
        </div>
        <div className='flex items-center gap-2 text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
          <span
            className={cn('w-2.5 h-2.5 rounded-full', statusColors.IN_PROGRESS)}
          />
          In Progress
        </div>
        <div className='flex items-center gap-2 text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
          <span
            className={cn('w-2.5 h-2.5 rounded-full', statusColors.REVIEW)}
          />
          Review
        </div>
        <div className='flex items-center gap-2 text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
          <span className={cn('w-2.5 h-2.5 rounded-full', statusColors.DONE)} />
          Done
        </div>
        <div className='ml-auto text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
          <GripVertical className='w-3 h-3 inline mr-1' />
          Drag tasks to reschedule
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );

  return (
    <TooltipProvider>
      <DndContext
        sensors={sensors}
        onDragStart={handleDragStart}
        onDragEnd={handleDragEnd}
      >
        <div className='space-y-6'>
          {/* Calendar Header */}
          <div className='flex items-center justify-between flex-wrap gap-4'>
            <div className='flex items-center gap-4'>
              <h2 className='text-xl font-semibold text-foreground'>
                {getHeaderTitle()}
              </h2>
              <Button variant='outline' size='sm' onClick={goToToday}>
                Today
              </Button>
            </div>
            <div className='flex items-center gap-2 flex-wrap'>
              {/* Export Menu */}
              <ExportMenu
                allTasks={tasks}
                filteredTasks={filteredTasks}
                selectedTask={selectedTask}
                hasActiveFilters={activeFiltersCount > 0}
              />

              {/* Keyboard Shortcuts Button */}
              <Tooltip>
                <TooltipTrigger asChild>
                  <Button
                    variant='outline'
                    size='sm'
                    onClick={() => setShowHelpModal(true)}
                    className='gap-2'
                  >
                    <Keyboard className='w-4 h-4' />
                    <span className='hidden sm:inline'>Shortcuts</span>
                    <kbd className='hidden sm:inline-flex h-5 select-none items-center gap-1 rounded border border-border bg-muted px-1.5 font-mono text-[10px] font-medium opacity-100'>
                      ?
                    </kbd>
                  </Button>
                </TooltipTrigger>
                <TooltipContent side='bottom'>
                  <p>View keyboard shortcuts</p>
                </TooltipContent>
              </Tooltip>

              {/* Filter Button */}
              <Popover open={filterOpen} onOpenChange={setFilterOpen}>
                <PopoverTrigger asChild>
                  <Button
                    variant='outline'
                    size='sm'
                    className={cn(
                      'gap-2',
                      activeFiltersCount > 0 && 'border-primary bg-primary/10',
                    )}
                  >
                    <Filter className='w-4 h-4' />
                    Filter
                    {activeFiltersCount > 0 && (
                      <Badge
                        variant='secondary'
                        className='ml-1 h-5 px-1.5 text-xs'
                      >
                        {activeFiltersCount}
                      </Badge>
                    )}
                  </Button>
                </PopoverTrigger>
                <PopoverContent
                  className='w-80 p-4 bg-popover border border-border shadow-lg'
                  align='end'
                >
                  <div className='space-y-4'>
                    <div className='flex items-center justify-between'>
                      <h4 className='font-medium text-foreground'>
                        Filter Tasks
                      </h4>
                      {activeFiltersCount > 0 && (
                        <Button
                          variant='ghost'
                          size='sm'
                          onClick={clearFilters}
                          className='h-auto p-1 text-xs text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground'
                        >
                          Clear all
                        </Button>
                      )}
                    </div>

                    {/* Priority Filter */}
                    <div className='space-y-2'>
                      <Label className='text-sm font-medium text-foreground'>
                        Priority
                      </Label>
                      <div className='grid grid-cols-2 gap-2'>
                        {(
                          [
                            'LOW',
                            'MEDIUM',
                            'HIGH',
                            'URGENT',
                          ] as Task['priority'][]
                        ).map((priority) => (
                          <div
                            key={priority}
                            className='flex items-center space-x-2'
                          >
                            <Checkbox
                              id={`priority-${priority}`}
                              checked={filters.priorities.includes(priority)}
                              onCheckedChange={() =>
                                toggleFilter('priorities', priority)
                              }
                            />
                            <Label
                              htmlFor={`priority-${priority}`}
                              className={cn(
                                'text-sm cursor-pointer',
                                priority === 'URGENT' && 'text-destructive',
                                priority === 'HIGH' && 'text-destructive/80',
                                priority === 'MEDIUM' && 'text-warning',
                                priority === 'LOW' && 'text-muted-foreground',
                              )}
                            >
                              {priority.charAt(0) +
                                priority.slice(1).toLowerCase()}
                            </Label>
                          </div>
                        ))}
                      </div>
                    </div>

                    {/* Status Filter */}
                    <div className='space-y-2'>
                      <Label className='text-sm font-medium text-foreground'>
                        Status
                      </Label>
                      <div className='grid grid-cols-2 gap-2'>
                        {(
                          [
                            'TODO',
                            'IN_PROGRESS',
                            'REVIEW',
                            'DONE',
                          ] as Task['status'][]
                        ).map((status) => (
                          <div
                            key={status}
                            className='flex items-center space-x-2'
                          >
                            <Checkbox
                              id={`status-${status}`}
                              checked={filters.statuses.includes(status)}
                              onCheckedChange={() =>
                                toggleFilter('statuses', status)
                              }
                            />
                            <Label
                              htmlFor={`status-${status}`}
                              className='text-sm cursor-pointer flex items-center gap-1.5'
                            >
                              <span
                                className={cn(
                                  'w-2 h-2 rounded-full',
                                  statusColors[status],
                                )}
                              />
                              {status.replace('_', ' ')}
                            </Label>
                          </div>
                        ))}
                      </div>
                    </div>

                    {/* Assignee Filter */}
                    {uniqueAssignees.length > 0 && (
                      <div className='space-y-2'>
                        <Label className='text-sm font-medium text-foreground'>
                          Assignee
                        </Label>
                        <div className='space-y-2 max-h-32 overflow-y-auto'>
                          {uniqueAssignees.map((assignee) => (
                            <div
                              key={assignee.id}
                              className='flex items-center space-x-2'
                            >
                              <Checkbox
                                id={`assignee-${assignee.id}`}
                                checked={filters.assigneeIds.includes(
                                  assignee.id,
                                )}
                                onCheckedChange={() =>
                                  toggleFilter('assigneeIds', assignee.id)
                                }
                              />
                              <Label
                                htmlFor={`assignee-${assignee.id}`}
                                className='text-sm cursor-pointer flex items-center gap-2'
                              >
                                <img
                                  src={assignee.image}
                                  alt={assignee.name}
                                  className='w-5 h-5 rounded-full'
                                />
                                {assignee.name}
                              </Label>
                            </div>
                          ))}
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    )}

                    {/* Presets Section */}
                    <Separator />

                    <div className='space-y-2'>
                      <div className='flex items-center justify-between'>
                        <Label className='text-sm font-medium text-foreground flex items-center gap-1.5'>
                          <Bookmark className='w-3.5 h-3.5' />
                          Saved Presets
                        </Label>
                        {activeFiltersCount > 0 && !showSavePreset && (
                          <Button
                            variant='ghost'
                            size='sm'
                            onClick={() => setShowSavePreset(true)}
                            className='h-auto p-1 text-xs text-primary hover:text-primary/80'
                          >
                            <Save className='w-3 h-3 mr-1' />
                            Save current
                          </Button>
                        )}
                      </div>

                      {/* Save New Preset Form */}
                      {showSavePreset && (
                        <div className='flex gap-2'>
                          <Input
                            placeholder='Preset name...'
                            value={newPresetName}
                            onChange={(e) => setNewPresetName(e.target.value)}
                            className='h-8 text-sm'
                            onKeyDown={(e) => {
                              if (e.key === 'Enter') savePreset();
                              if (e.key === 'Escape') {
                                setShowSavePreset(false);
                                setNewPresetName('');
                              }
                            }}
                            autoFocus
                          />
                          <Button
                            size='sm'
                            onClick={savePreset}
                            disabled={!newPresetName.trim()}
                            className='h-8 px-2'
                          >
                            <Save className='w-3.5 h-3.5' />
                          </Button>
                          <Button
                            variant='ghost'
                            size='sm'
                            onClick={() => {
                              setShowSavePreset(false);
                              setNewPresetName('');
                            }}
                            className='h-8 px-2'
                          >
                            <X className='w-3.5 h-3.5' />
                          </Button>
                        </div>
                      )}

                      {/* Preset List */}
                      {presets.length > 0 ? (
                        <div className='space-y-1 max-h-32 overflow-y-auto'>
                          {presets.map((preset) => (
                            <div
                              key={preset.id}
                              className='flex items-center justify-between p-2 rounded-md bg-secondary/50 hover:bg-secondary group cursor-pointer'
                              onClick={() => loadPreset(preset)}
                            >
                              <div className='flex-1 min-w-0'>
                                <p className='text-sm font-medium text-foreground truncate'>
                                  {preset.name}
                                </p>
                                <p className='text-[10px] text-muted-foreground truncate'>
                                  {getPresetDescription(preset)}
                                </p>
                              </div>
                              <Button
                                variant='ghost'
                                size='sm'
                                onClick={(e) => {
                                  e.stopPropagation();
                                  deletePreset(preset.id);
                                }}
                                className='h-6 w-6 p-0 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 text-destructive hover:text-destructive hover:bg-destructive/10'
                              >
                                <Trash2 className='w-3 h-3' />
                              </Button>
                            </div>
                          ))}
                        </div>
                      ) : (
                        <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground italic py-2'>
                          No saved presets. Apply filters and save them for
                          quick access.
                        </p>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </PopoverContent>
              </Popover>

              {/* Presets Quick Access Dropdown */}
              {presets.length > 0 && (
                <DropdownMenu>
                  <DropdownMenuTrigger asChild>
                    <Button variant='outline' size='sm' className='gap-1.5'>
                      <Bookmark className='w-4 h-4' />
                      Presets
                      <ChevronDown className='w-3 h-3' />
                    </Button>
                  </DropdownMenuTrigger>
                  <DropdownMenuContent
                    align='end'
                    className='w-48 bg-popover border border-border'
                  >
                    {presets.map((preset) => (
                      <DropdownMenuItem
                        key={preset.id}
                        onClick={() => loadPreset(preset)}
                        className='cursor-pointer'
                      >
                        <div className='flex-1 min-w-0'>
                          <p className='text-sm truncate'>{preset.name}</p>
                          <p className='text-[10px] text-muted-foreground truncate'>
                            {getPresetDescription(preset)}
                          </p>
                        </div>
                      </DropdownMenuItem>
                    ))}
                    <DropdownMenuSeparator />
                    <DropdownMenuItem
                      onClick={clearFilters}
                      className='cursor-pointer text-muted-foreground'
                    >
                      <X className='w-3.5 h-3.5 mr-2' />
                      Clear filters
                    </DropdownMenuItem>
                  </DropdownMenuContent>
                </DropdownMenu>
              )}

              {/* Active Filter Tags */}
              {activeFiltersCount > 0 && (
                <div className='flex items-center gap-1.5 flex-wrap'>
                  {filters.priorities.map((p) => (
                    <Badge
                      key={p}
                      variant='secondary'
                      className='gap-1 pr-1 cursor-pointer hover:bg-secondary/80'
                      onClick={() => toggleFilter('priorities', p)}
                    >
                      {p.charAt(0) + p.slice(1).toLowerCase()}
                      <X className='w-3 h-3' />
                    </Badge>
                  ))}
                  {filters.statuses.map((s) => (
                    <Badge
                      key={s}
                      variant='secondary'
                      className='gap-1 pr-1 cursor-pointer hover:bg-secondary/80'
                      onClick={() => toggleFilter('statuses', s)}
                    >
                      {s.replace('_', ' ')}
                      <X className='w-3 h-3' />
                    </Badge>
                  ))}
                  {filters.assigneeIds.map((id) => {
                    const assignee = uniqueAssignees.find((a) => a.id === id);
                    return (
                      assignee && (
                        <Badge
                          key={id}
                          variant='secondary'
                          className='gap-1 pr-1 cursor-pointer hover:bg-secondary/80'
                          onClick={() => toggleFilter('assigneeIds', id)}
                        >
                          {assignee.name}
                          <X className='w-3 h-3' />
                        </Badge>
                      )
                    );
                  })}
                </div>
              )}

              {/* View Mode Toggle */}
              <div className='flex items-center gap-1 bg-secondary/50 rounded-lg p-1'>
                <Tooltip>
                  <TooltipTrigger asChild>
                    <Button
                      variant={viewMode === 'month' ? 'secondary' : 'ghost'}
                      size='sm'
                      onClick={() => setViewMode('month')}
                      className='gap-1.5'
                    >
                      <CalendarIcon className='w-4 h-4' />
                      <span className='hidden sm:inline'>Month</span>
                    </Button>
                  </TooltipTrigger>
                  <TooltipContent side='bottom'>
                    <p>Month view</p>
                    <kbd className='ml-2 text-xs opacity-60'>1</kbd>
                  </TooltipContent>
                </Tooltip>
                <Tooltip>
                  <TooltipTrigger asChild>
                    <Button
                      variant={viewMode === 'week' ? 'secondary' : 'ghost'}
                      size='sm'
                      onClick={() => setViewMode('week')}
                      className='gap-1.5'
                    >
                      <CalendarDays className='w-4 h-4' />
                      <span className='hidden sm:inline'>Week</span>
                    </Button>
                  </TooltipTrigger>
                  <TooltipContent side='bottom'>
                    <p>Week view</p>
                    <kbd className='ml-2 text-xs opacity-60'>2</kbd>
                  </TooltipContent>
                </Tooltip>
                <Tooltip>
                  <TooltipTrigger asChild>
                    <Button
                      variant={viewMode === 'day' ? 'secondary' : 'ghost'}
                      size='sm'
                      onClick={() => setViewMode('day')}
                      className='gap-1.5'
                    >
                      <Clock className='w-4 h-4' />
                      <span className='hidden sm:inline'>Day</span>
                    </Button>
                  </TooltipTrigger>
                  <TooltipContent side='bottom'>
                    <p>Day view</p>
                    <kbd className='ml-2 text-xs opacity-60'>3</kbd>
                  </TooltipContent>
                </Tooltip>
                <Tooltip>
                  <TooltipTrigger asChild>
                    <Button
                      variant={viewMode === 'gantt' ? 'secondary' : 'ghost'}
                      size='sm'
                      onClick={() => setViewMode('gantt')}
                      className='gap-1.5'
                    >
                      <BarChart3 className='w-4 h-4' />
                      <span className='hidden sm:inline'>Gantt</span>
                    </Button>
                  </TooltipTrigger>
                  <TooltipContent side='bottom'>
                    <p>Gantt timeline</p>
                    <kbd className='ml-2 text-xs opacity-60'>4</kbd>
                  </TooltipContent>
                </Tooltip>
              </div>

              {viewMode !== 'gantt' && (
                <div className='flex items-center gap-2'>
                  <Tooltip>
                    <TooltipTrigger asChild>
                      <Button
                        variant='ghost'
                        size='icon'
                        onClick={() => navigate('prev')}
                      >
                        <ChevronLeft className='w-4 h-4' />
                      </Button>
                    </TooltipTrigger>
                    <TooltipContent side='bottom'>
                      <p>Previous</p>
                      <kbd className='ml-2 text-xs opacity-60'>←</kbd>
                    </TooltipContent>
                  </Tooltip>
                  <Tooltip>
                    <TooltipTrigger asChild>
                      <Button
                        variant='ghost'
                        size='icon'
                        onClick={() => navigate('next')}
                      >
                        <ChevronRight className='w-4 h-4' />
                      </Button>
                    </TooltipTrigger>
                    <TooltipContent side='bottom'>
                      <p>Next</p>
                      <kbd className='ml-2 text-xs opacity-60'>→</kbd>
                    </TooltipContent>
                  </Tooltip>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Render appropriate view */}
          {viewMode === 'gantt' ? (
            <GanttView tasks={filteredTasks} onTaskClick={onTaskClick} />
          ) : viewMode === 'day' ? (
            renderDayView()
          ) : (
            renderMonthWeekView()
          )}
        </div>

        {/* Drag Overlay */}
        <DragOverlay>
          {activeTask ? <DragOverlayTask task={activeTask} /> : null}
        </DragOverlay>
      </DndContext>

      {/* Keyboard Shortcuts Modal */}
      <KeyboardShortcutsModal
        open={showHelpModal}
        onClose={() => setShowHelpModal(false)}
      />
    </TooltipProvider>
  );
}


==============================
FILE: E:\My Projects\Project-Management\sprintly-frontend\src\components\command\CommandPalette.tsx
==============================

import { useEffect, useState, useMemo } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import {
  Search,
  FolderKanban,
  CheckSquare,
  Users,
  Plus,
  ArrowRight,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { useWorkspaceStore } from '@/store/workspaceStore';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';

interface CommandItem {
  id: string;
  type: 'project' | 'task' | 'member' | 'action';
  title: string;
  subtitle?: string;
  icon: typeof Search;
  action: () => void;
}

export default function CommandPalette() {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const { currentWorkspace } = useWorkspaceStore();
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false);
  const [search, setSearch] = useState('');
  const [selectedIndex, setSelectedIndex] = useState(0);

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleKeyDown = (e: KeyboardEvent) => {
      if ((e.metaKey || e.ctrlKey) && e.key === 'k') {
        e.preventDefault();
        setIsOpen(true);
        setSearch('');
        setSelectedIndex(0);
      }
      if (e.key === 'Escape') {
        setIsOpen(false);
      }
    };

    window.addEventListener('keydown', handleKeyDown);
    return () => window.removeEventListener('keydown', handleKeyDown);
  }, []);

  const items = useMemo(() => {
    const results: CommandItem[] = [];
    const query = search.toLowerCase();

    // Quick Actions
    if (!search || 'create'.includes(query) || 'new'.includes(query)) {
      results.push({
        id: 'action-new-project',
        type: 'action',
        title: 'Create New Project',
        subtitle: 'Start a new project',
        icon: Plus,
        action: () => {
          navigate('/projects');
          setIsOpen(false);
        },
      });
    }

    // Projects
    currentWorkspace?.projects.forEach((project) => {
      if (!search || project.name.toLowerCase().includes(query)) {
        results.push({
          id: `project-${project.id}`,
          type: 'project',
          title: project.name,
          subtitle: `${project.tasks.length} tasks`,
          icon: FolderKanban,
          action: () => {
            navigate(`/projects/${project.id}`);
            setIsOpen(false);
          },
        });
      }

      // Tasks within projects
      project.tasks.forEach((task) => {
        if (!search || task.title.toLowerCase().includes(query)) {
          results.push({
            id: `task-${task.id}`,
            type: 'task',
            title: task.title,
            subtitle: project.name,
            icon: CheckSquare,
            action: () => {
              navigate(`/projects/${project.id}`);
              setIsOpen(false);
            },
          });
        }
      });
    });

    // Members
    currentWorkspace?.members.forEach((member) => {
      if (!search || member.user.name.toLowerCase().includes(query)) {
        results.push({
          id: `member-${member.id}`,
          type: 'member',
          title: member.user.name,
          subtitle: member.user.email,
          icon: Users,
          action: () => {
            navigate('/team');
            setIsOpen(false);
          },
        });
      }
    });

    return results.slice(0, 10);
  }, [search, currentWorkspace, navigate]);

  useEffect(() => {
    setSelectedIndex(0);
  }, [search]);

  const handleKeyDown = (e: React.KeyboardEvent) => {
    if (e.key === 'ArrowDown') {
      e.preventDefault();
      setSelectedIndex((i) => Math.min(i + 1, items.length - 1));
    } else if (e.key === 'ArrowUp') {
      e.preventDefault();
      setSelectedIndex((i) => Math.max(i - 1, 0));
    } else if (e.key === 'Enter' && items[selectedIndex]) {
      items[selectedIndex].action();
    }
  };

  return (
    <AnimatePresence>
      {isOpen && (
        <>
          <motion.div
            initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
            className='fixed inset-0 bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-sm z-50'
            onClick={() => setIsOpen(false)}
          />
          <motion.div
            initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95, y: -20 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1, y: 0 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95, y: -20 }}
            className='fixed left-1/2 top-[20%] -translate-x-1/2 z-50 w-full max-w-xl mx-4'
          >
            <div className='glass-card overflow-hidden shadow-2xl'>
              {/* Search Input */}
              <div className='flex items-center gap-3 p-4 border-b border-border'>
                <Search className='w-5 h-5 text-muted-foreground' />
                <input
                  type='text'
                  value={search}
                  onChange={(e) => setSearch(e.target.value)}
                  onKeyDown={handleKeyDown}
                  placeholder='Search projects, tasks, members...'
                  className='flex-1 bg-transparent border-0 outline-none text-foreground placeholder:text-muted-foreground'
                  autoFocus
                />
                <kbd className='px-2 py-1 text-[10px] font-medium bg-secondary rounded text-muted-foreground'>
                  ESC
                </kbd>
              </div>

              {/* Results */}
              <div className='max-h-[400px] overflow-y-auto p-2'>
                {items.length === 0 ? (
                  <div className='p-8 text-center text-muted-foreground'>
                    No results found
                  </div>
                ) : (
                  items.map((item, index) => (
                    <button
                      key={item.id}
                      onClick={item.action}
                      className={cn(
                        'w-full flex items-center gap-3 p-3 rounded-lg transition-colors text-left',
                        index === selectedIndex
                          ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground'
                          : 'hover:bg-accent',
                      )}
                    >
                      <item.icon
                        className={cn(
                          'w-4 h-4',
                          index === selectedIndex
                            ? 'text-primary-foreground'
                            : 'text-muted-foreground',
                        )}
                      />
                      <div className='flex-1 min-w-0'>
                        <p
                          className={cn(
                            'font-medium text-sm truncate',
                            index === selectedIndex
                              ? 'text-primary-foreground'
                              : 'text-foreground',
                          )}
                        >
                          {item.title}
                        </p>
                        {item.subtitle && (
                          <p
                            className={cn(
                              'text-xs truncate',
                              index === selectedIndex
                                ? 'text-primary-foreground/70'
                                : 'text-muted-foreground',
                            )}
                          >
                            {item.subtitle}
                          </p>
                        )}
                      </div>
                      <ArrowRight
                        className={cn(
                          'w-4 h-4 opacity-0 transition-opacity',
                          index === selectedIndex && 'opacity-100',
                        )}
                      />
                    </button>
                  ))
                )}
              </div>

              {/* Footer */}
              <div className='p-3 border-t border-border flex items-center justify-between text-[10px] text-muted-foreground'>
                <div className='flex items-center gap-4'>
                  <span>
                    <kbd className='px-1.5 py-0.5 bg-secondary rounded'>↑↓</kbd>{' '}
                    Navigate
                  </span>
                  <span>
                    <kbd className='px-1.5 py-0.5 bg-secondary rounded'>↵</kbd>{' '}
                    Select
                  </span>
                </div>
                <span>
                  <kbd className='px-1.5 py-0.5 bg-secondary rounded'>⌘K</kbd>{' '}
                  Toggle
                </span>
              </div>
            </div>
          </motion.div>
        </>
      )}
    </AnimatePresence>
  );
}

FILE: E:\My Projects\Project-Management\sprintly-frontend\src\components\dashboard\ProjectsOverview.tsx

import { motion } from 'framer-motion';
import { ArrowRight, Calendar, Users } from 'lucide-react';
import { Link } from 'react-router-dom';
import { useWorkspaceStore } from '@/store/workspaceStore';
import { format } from 'date-fns';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';

const statusColors: Record<string, string> = {
  PLANNING: 'bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground',
  ACTIVE: 'bg-success/20 text-success',
  ON_HOLD: 'bg-warning/20 text-warning',
  COMPLETED: 'bg-primary/20 text-primary',
  CANCELLED: 'bg-destructive/20 text-destructive',
};

const priorityColors: Record<string, string> = {
  LOW: 'text-muted-foreground',
  MEDIUM: 'text-warning',
  HIGH: 'text-destructive',
};

export default function ProjectsOverview() {
  const { currentWorkspace } = useWorkspaceStore();
  const projects = currentWorkspace?.projects.slice(0, 3) || [];

  return (
    <div className='glass-card p-6'>
      <div className='flex items-center justify-between mb-6'>
        <h2 className='text-lg font-semibold text-foreground'>
          Recent Projects
        </h2>
        <Link
          to='/projects'
          className='flex items-center gap-1 text-sm text-primary hover:text-primary/80 transition-colors'
        >
          View all
          <ArrowRight className='w-4 h-4' />
        </Link>
      </div>

      <div className='space-y-4'>
        {projects.length === 0 ? (
          <p className='text-center text-muted-foreground py-8'>
            No projects yet
          </p>
        ) : (
          projects.map((project, index) => (
            <motion.div
              key={project.id}
              initial={{ opacity: 0, x: -20 }}
              animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
              transition={{ delay: index * 0.1 }}
            >
              <Link
                to={`/projects/${project.id}`}
                className='block p-4 rounded-xl bg-secondary/30 hover:bg-secondary/50 transition-all group'
              >
                <div className='flex items-start justify-between mb-3'>
                  <div className='flex-1'>
                    <h3 className='font-medium text-foreground group-hover:text-primary transition-colors'>
                      {project.name}
                    </h3>
                    <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground line-clamp-1 mt-1'>
                      {project.description}
                    </p>
                  </div>
                  <span
                    className={cn(
                      'px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-medium',
                      statusColors[project.status],
                    )}
                  >
                    {project.status.replace('_', ' ')}
                  </span>
                </div>

                <div className='flex items-center justify-between'>
                  <div className='flex items-center gap-4 text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                    <span className='flex items-center gap-1'>
                      <Calendar className='w-3.5 h-3.5' />
                      {project.end_date
                        ? format(new Date(project.end_date), 'MMM d')
                        : 'No deadline'}
                    </span>
                    <span className='flex items-center gap-1'>
                      <Users className='w-3.5 h-3.5' />
                      {project.members.length}
                    </span>
                    <span className={priorityColors[project.priority]}>
                      {project.priority}
                    </span>
                  </div>

                  {/* Progress Bar */}
                  <div className='flex items-center gap-2'>
                    <div className='w-20 h-1.5 bg-secondary rounded-full overflow-hidden'>
                      <div
                        className='h-full bg-primary rounded-full transition-all'
                        style={{ width: `${project.progress}%` }}
                      />
                    </div>
                    <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                      {project.progress}%
                    </span>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </Link>
            </motion.div>
          ))
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}


==============================
FILE: E:\My Projects\Project-Management\sprintly-frontend\src\components\dashboard\RecentActivity.tsx
==============================

import { motion } from 'framer-motion';
import { CheckCircle2, AlertCircle, Zap, ArrowUpRight } from 'lucide-react';
import { useWorkspaceStore } from '@/store/workspaceStore';
import { format, isBefore } from 'date-fns';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';

export default function RecentActivity() {
  const { currentWorkspace } = useWorkspaceStore();
  const projects = currentWorkspace?.projects || [];
  const allTasks = projects.flatMap((p) => p.tasks);

  const activities = allTasks
    .slice(0, 5)
    .map((task) => {
      const isOverdue =
        isBefore(new Date(task.due_date), new Date()) && task.status !== 'DONE';
      const isCompleted = task.status === 'DONE';

      const icon = isCompleted ? CheckCircle2 : isOverdue ? AlertCircle : Zap;
      const color = isCompleted
        ? 'text-success bg-success/10'
        : isOverdue
          ? 'text-destructive bg-destructive/10'
          : 'text-primary bg-primary/10';
      const message = isCompleted
        ? `Completed "${task.title}"`
        : isOverdue
          ? `Overdue: "${task.title}"`
          : `Task: "${task.title}"`;

      return {
        id: task.id,
        message,
        timestamp: new Date(task.updatedAt),
        icon,
        color,
      };
    })
    .sort((a, b) => b.timestamp.getTime() - a.timestamp.getTime());

  return (
    <div className='glass-card p-6'>
      <h2 className='text-lg font-semibold text-foreground mb-6'>
        Recent Activity
      </h2>

      <div className='space-y-4'>
        {activities.length === 0 ? (
          <p className='text-center text-muted-foreground py-8'>
            No recent activity
          </p>
        ) : (
          activities.map((activity, index) => (
            <motion.div
              key={activity.id}
              initial={{ opacity: 0, x: -20 }}
              animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
              transition={{ delay: index * 0.05 }}
              className='flex items-start gap-3'
            >
              <div
                className={cn('p-2 rounded-lg flex-shrink-0', activity.color)}
              >
                <activity.icon className='w-4 h-4' />
              </div>
              <div className='flex-1 min-w-0'>
                <p className='text-sm text-foreground truncate'>
                  {activity.message}
                </p>
                <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-0.5'>
                  {format(activity.timestamp, 'MMM d, yyyy')}
                </p>
              </div>
            </motion.div>
          ))
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}


==============================
FILE: E:\My Projects\Project-Management\sprintly-frontend\src\components\dashboard\StatsGrid.tsx
==============================

import { motion } from 'framer-motion';
import {
  FolderKanban,
  CheckCircle2,
  Clock,
  AlertTriangle,
  TrendingUp,
  Users,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { useWorkspaceStore } from '@/store/workspaceStore';
import { useMemo } from 'react';

const container = {
  hidden: { opacity: 0 },
  show: {
    opacity: 1,
    transition: { staggerChildren: 0.1 },
  },
};

const item = {
  hidden: { opacity: 0, y: 20 },
  show: { opacity: 1, y: 0 },
};

export default function StatsGrid() {
  const { currentWorkspace } = useWorkspaceStore();

  const stats = useMemo(() => {
    const projects = currentWorkspace?.projects || [];
    const allTasks = projects.flatMap((p) => p.tasks);
    const now = new Date();

    return {
      totalProjects: projects.length,
      activeProjects: projects.filter((p) => p.status === 'ACTIVE').length,
      completedTasks: allTasks.filter((t) => t.status === 'DONE').length,
      inProgressTasks: allTasks.filter((t) => t.status === 'IN_PROGRESS')
        .length,
      todoTasks: allTasks.filter((t) => t.status === 'TODO').length,
      overdueTasks: allTasks.filter(
        (t) => new Date(t.due_date) < now && t.status !== 'DONE',
      ).length,
      teamMembers: currentWorkspace?.members.length || 0,
    };
  }, [currentWorkspace]);

  const statsData = [
    {
      label: 'Total Projects',
      value: stats.totalProjects,
      icon: FolderKanban,
      color: 'from-primary to-cyan-400',
      bgColor: 'bg-primary/10',
      trend: `${stats.activeProjects} active`,
    },
    {
      label: 'Completed Tasks',
      value: stats.completedTasks,
      icon: CheckCircle2,
      color: 'from-success to-emerald-400',
      bgColor: 'bg-success/10',
      trend: 'All time',
    },
    {
      label: 'In Progress',
      value: stats.inProgressTasks,
      icon: Clock,
      color: 'from-warning to-amber-400',
      bgColor: 'bg-warning/10',
      trend: `${stats.todoTasks} pending`,
    },
    {
      label: 'Team Members',
      value: stats.teamMembers,
      icon: Users,
      color: 'from-violet-500 to-purple-400',
      bgColor: 'bg-violet-500/10',
      trend: 'Active',
    },
  ];

  return (
    <motion.div
      variants={container}
      initial='hidden'
      animate='show'
      className='grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-4 gap-4 mb-8'
    >
      {statsData.map((stat, index) => (
        <motion.div
          key={stat.label}
          variants={item}
          className='glass-card-hover p-5'
        >
          <div className='flex items-start justify-between'>
            <div className='space-y-2'>
              <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>{stat.label}</p>
              <p className='text-3xl font-bold text-foreground'>{stat.value}</p>
              <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground flex items-center gap-1'>
                <TrendingUp className='w-3 h-3' />
                {stat.trend}
              </p>
            </div>
            <div className={`p-3 rounded-xl ${stat.bgColor}`}>
              <stat.icon
                className={`w-5 h-5 bg-gradient-to-br ${stat.color} bg-clip-text text-transparent`}
                style={{ color: `hsl(var(--primary))` }}
              />
            </div>
          </div>
        </motion.div>
      ))}
    </motion.div>
  );
}


==============================
FILE: E:\My Projects\Project-Management\sprintly-frontend\src\components\dashboard\TasksSummary.tsx
==============================

import { motion } from 'framer-motion';
import { Calendar, ArrowRight } from 'lucide-react';
import { Link } from 'react-router-dom';
import { useWorkspaceStore } from '@/store/workspaceStore';
import { format, isBefore } from 'date-fns';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';

const priorityColors: Record<string, string> = {
  LOW: 'border-l-muted-foreground',
  MEDIUM: 'border-l-warning',
  HIGH: 'border-l-destructive',
};

const typeColors: Record<string, string> = {
  BUG: 'bg-destructive/10 text-destructive',
  FEATURE: 'bg-primary/10 text-primary',
  TASK: 'bg-success/10 text-success',
  IMPROVEMENT: 'bg-violet-500/10 text-violet-500',
  OTHER: 'bg-warning/10 text-warning',
};

export default function TasksSummary() {
  const { currentWorkspace } = useWorkspaceStore();
  const projects = currentWorkspace?.projects || [];
  const allTasks = projects.flatMap((p) => p.tasks);

  const pendingTasks = allTasks
    .filter((t) => t.status !== 'DONE')
    .sort(
      (a, b) => new Date(a.due_date).getTime() - new Date(b.due_date).getTime(),
    )
    .slice(0, 5);

  const now = new Date();

  return (
    <div className='glass-card p-6'>
      <div className='flex items-center justify-between mb-6'>
        <h2 className='text-lg font-semibold text-foreground'>
          Upcoming Tasks
        </h2>
        <Link
          to='/projects'
          className='flex items-center gap-1 text-sm text-primary hover:text-primary/80 transition-colors'
        >
          View all
          <ArrowRight className='w-4 h-4' />
        </Link>
      </div>

      <div className='space-y-3'>
        {pendingTasks.length === 0 ? (
          <p className='text-center text-muted-foreground py-8'>
            All caught up! 🎉
          </p>
        ) : (
          pendingTasks.map((task, index) => {
            const isOverdue = isBefore(new Date(task.due_date), now);
            const project = projects.find((p) => p.id === task.projectId);

            return (
              <motion.div
                key={task.id}
                initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
                animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                transition={{ delay: index * 0.05 }}
                className={cn(
                  'p-3 rounded-lg bg-secondary/30 border-l-2 transition-all hover:bg-secondary/50',
                  priorityColors[task.priority],
                )}
              >
                <div className='flex items-start justify-between gap-2 mb-2'>
                  <p className='text-sm font-medium text-foreground line-clamp-1'>
                    {task.title}
                  </p>
                  <span
                    className={cn(
                      'px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-[10px] font-medium flex-shrink-0',
                      typeColors[task.type],
                    )}
                  >
                    {task.type}
                  </span>
                </div>

                <div className='flex items-center justify-between text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                  <span className='truncate'>{project?.name}</span>
                  <span
                    className={cn(
                      'flex items-center gap-1',
                      isOverdue && 'text-destructive',
                    )}
                  >
                    <Calendar className='w-3 h-3' />
                    {format(new Date(task.due_date), 'MMM d')}
                  </span>
                </div>
              </motion.div>
            );
          })
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import { useState } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import { X, Calendar } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Label } from '@/components/ui/label';
import { Textarea } from '@/components/ui/textarea';
import { useWorkspaceStore, type Project } from '@/store/workspaceStore';
import { toast } from 'sonner';

interface CreateProjectDialogProps {
  open: boolean;
  onOpenChange: (open: boolean) => void;
}

export default function CreateProjectDialog({
  open,
  onOpenChange,
}: CreateProjectDialogProps) {
  const { addProject, currentWorkspace } = useWorkspaceStore();
  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({
    name: '',
    description: '',
    status: 'PLANNING' as Project['status'],
    priority: 'MEDIUM' as Project['priority'],
    start_date: '',
    end_date: '',
  });

  const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();

    if (!formData.name.trim()) {
      toast.error('Please enter a project name');
      return;
    }

    const newProject: Project = {
      id: `project_${Date.now()}`,
      ...formData,
      workspaceId: currentWorkspace?.id || '',
      team_lead: currentWorkspace?.ownerId || '',
      progress: 0,
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      tasks: [],
      members: [],
      kanbanColumns: [
        { id: 'col-1', status: 'TODO', title: 'To Do', order: 0 },
        { id: 'col-2', status: 'IN_PROGRESS', title: 'In Progress', order: 1 },
        { id: 'col-3', status: 'REVIEW', title: 'Review', order: 2 },
        { id: 'col-4', status: 'DONE', title: 'Done', order: 3 },
      ],
      taskTemplates: [],
    };

    addProject(newProject);
    toast.success('Project created successfully');
    onOpenChange(false);
    setFormData({
      name: '',
      description: '',
      status: 'PLANNING',
      priority: 'MEDIUM',
      start_date: '',
      end_date: '',
    });
  };

  return (
    <AnimatePresence>
      {open && (
        <>
          <motion.div
            initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
            className='fixed inset-0 bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-sm z-50'
            onClick={() => onOpenChange(false)}
          />

          <motion.div
            initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95, y: 20 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1, y: 0 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95, y: 20 }}
            className='fixed left-1/2 top-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 z-50 w-full max-w-lg'
          >
            <div className='glass-card p-6 mx-4'>
              <div className='flex items-center justify-between mb-6'>
                <h2 className='text-xl font-semibold text-foreground'>
                  Create New Project
                </h2>
                <button
                  onClick={() => onOpenChange(false)}
                  className='p-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-accent transition-colors'
                >
                  <X className='w-5 h-5' />
                </button>
              </div>

              <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className='space-y-4'>
                <div className='space-y-2'>
                  <Label htmlFor='name'>Project Name</Label>
                  <Input
                    id='name'
                    value={formData.name}
                    onChange={(e) =>
                      setFormData({ ...formData, name: e.target.value })
                    }
                    placeholder='Enter project name'
                    className='bg-secondary/50'
                  />
                </div>

                <div className='space-y-2'>
                  <Label htmlFor='description'>Description</Label>
                  <Textarea
                    id='description'
                    value={formData.description}
                    onChange={(e) =>
                      setFormData({ ...formData, description: e.target.value })
                    }
                    placeholder='Describe your project'
                    className='bg-secondary/50 min-h-[100px]'
                  />
                </div>

                <div className='grid grid-cols-2 gap-4'>
                  <div className='space-y-2'>
                    <Label htmlFor='status'>Status</Label>
                    <select
                      id='status'
                      value={formData.status}
                      onChange={(e) =>
                        setFormData({
                          ...formData,
                          status: e.target.value as Project['status'],
                        })
                      }
                      className='w-full px-3 py-2 rounded-lg bg-secondary/50 border border-border text-foreground text-sm'

                        setFormData({
                          ...formData,
                          priority: e.target.value as Project['priority'],
                        })
                      }
                      className='w-full px-3 py-2 rounded-lg bg-secondary/50 border border-border text-foreground text-sm'

FILE: E:\My Projects\Project-Management\sprintly-frontend\src\components\dialogs\CreateTaskDialog.tsx
