import { useState } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import { X, Repeat } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Label } from '@/components/ui/label';
import { Textarea } from '@/components/ui/textarea';
import { useWorkspaceStore, type Task } from '@/store/workspaceStore';
import { RecurrenceSelector } from '@/components/calendar/RecurrenceSelector';
import {
  generateSeriesId,
  getRecurrenceDescription,
  type RecurrenceRule,
} from '@/lib/recurrence';
import { toast } from 'sonner';

interface CreateTaskDialogProps {
  open: boolean;
  onOpenChange: (open: boolean) => void;
  projectId: string;
}

export default function CreateTaskDialog({
  open,
  onOpenChange,
  projectId,
}: CreateTaskDialogProps) {
  const { addTask, currentWorkspace } = useWorkspaceStore();
  const project = currentWorkspace?.projects.find((p) => p.id === projectId);
  const members = project?.members || [];

  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({
    title: '',
    description: '',
    status: 'TODO' as Task['status'],
    type: 'TASK' as Task['type'],
    priority: 'MEDIUM' as Task['priority'],
    assigneeId: '',
    due_date: '',
    due_time: '',
  });

  const [recurrenceRule, setRecurrenceRule] = useState<
    RecurrenceRule | undefined
  >(undefined);

  const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();

    if (!formData.title.trim()) {
      toast.error('Please enter a task title');
      return;
    }

    const assignee = members.find(
      (m) => m.userId === formData.assigneeId,
    )?.user;
    const taskId = `task_${Date.now()}`;
    const seriesId = recurrenceRule ? generateSeriesId() : undefined;

    // Store recurrence data as JSON in a custom field (simulated)
    const recurringData = recurrenceRule
      ? {
          isRecurring: true,
          recurrenceRule,
          seriesId,
          excludedDates: [],
          modifiedInstances: {},
        }
      : undefined;

    const newTask: Task = {
      id: taskId,
      projectId,
      ...formData,
      assignee: assignee || members[0]?.user,
      assigneeId: formData.assigneeId || members[0]?.userId || '',
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      comments: [],
      activities: [
        {
          id: `act-${Date.now()}`,
          taskId,
          type: 'created',
          user: assignee || members[0]?.user,
          newValue: recurrenceRule
            ? `Recurring task created (${getRecurrenceDescription(recurrenceRule)})`
            : 'Task created',
          createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        },
      ],
      subtasks: [],
      blockedBy: [],
      blocking: [],
      order: 0,
    };

    // In a real app, we'd store recurringData in the task or a separate store
    // For demo purposes, we'll store it in localStorage
    if (recurringData) {
      try {
        const existingRecurring = JSON.parse(
          localStorage.getItem('recurring-tasks') || '{}',
        );
        existingRecurring[taskId] = recurringData;
        localStorage.setItem(
          'recurring-tasks',
          JSON.stringify(existingRecurring),
        );
      } catch (e) {
        console.error('Failed to save recurrence data:', e);
      }
    }

    addTask(newTask);

    if (recurrenceRule) {
      toast.success('Recurring task created successfully', {
        description: getRecurrenceDescription(recurrenceRule),
      });
    } else {
      toast.success('Task created successfully');
    }

    onOpenChange(false);
    setFormData({
      title: '',
      description: '',
      status: 'TODO',
      type: 'TASK',
      priority: 'MEDIUM',
      assigneeId: '',
      due_date: '',
      due_time: '',
    });
    setRecurrenceRule(undefined);
  };

  return (
    <AnimatePresence>
      {open && (
        <>
          <motion.div
            initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
            className='fixed inset-0 bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-sm z-50'
            onClick={() => onOpenChange(false)}
          />

          <motion.div
            initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95, y: 20 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1, y: 0 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95, y: 20 }}
            className='fixed left-1/2 top-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 z-50 w-full max-w-lg max-h-[90vh] overflow-y-auto'
          >
            <div className='glass-card p-6 mx-4'>
              <div className='flex items-center justify-between mb-6'>
                <div>
                  <h2 className='text-xl font-semibold text-foreground'>
                    Create New Task
                  </h2>
                  <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-1'>
                    Adding to:{' '}
                    <span className='text-primary'>{project?.name}</span>
                  </p>
                </div>
                <button
                  onClick={() => onOpenChange(false)}
                  className='p-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-accent transition-colors'
                >
                  <X className='w-5 h-5' />
                </button>
              </div>

              <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className='space-y-4'>
                <div className='space-y-2'>
                  <Label htmlFor='title'>Task Title</Label>
                  <Input
                    id='title'
                    value={formData.title}
                    onChange={(e) =>
                      setFormData({ ...formData, title: e.target.value })
                    }
                    placeholder='Enter task title'
                    className='bg-secondary/50'
                  />
                </div>

                <div className='space-y-2'>
                  <Label htmlFor='description'>Description</Label>
                  <Textarea
                    id='description'
                    value={formData.description}
                    onChange={(e) =>
                      setFormData({ ...formData, description: e.target.value })
                    }
                    placeholder='Describe the task'
                    className='bg-secondary/50 min-h-[80px]'
                  />
                </div>

                <div className='grid grid-cols-2 gap-4'>
                  <div className='space-y-2'>
                    <Label htmlFor='type'>Type</Label>
                    <select
                      id='type'
                      value={formData.type}
                      onChange={(e) =>
                        setFormData({
                          ...formData,
                          type: e.target.value as Task['type'],
                        })
                      }
                      className='w-full px-3 py-2 rounded-lg bg-secondary/50 border border-border text-foreground text-sm'
                    >
                      <option value='TASK'>Task</option>
                      <option value='BUG'>Bug</option>
                      <option value='FEATURE'>Feature</option>
                      <option value='IMPROVEMENT'>Improvement</option>
                      <option value='OTHER'>Other</option>
                    </select>
                  </div>

                  <div className='space-y-2'>
                    <Label htmlFor='priority'>Priority</Label>
                    <select
                      id='priority'
                      value={formData.priority}
                      onChange={(e) =>
                        setFormData({
                          ...formData,
                          priority: e.target.value as Task['priority'],
                        })
                      }
                      className='w-full px-3 py-2 rounded-lg bg-secondary/50 border border-border text-foreground text-sm'
                    >
                      <option value='LOW'>Low</option>
                      <option value='MEDIUM'>Medium</option>
                      <option value='HIGH'>High</option>
                      <option value='URGENT'>Urgent</option>
                    </select>
                  </div>
                </div>

                <div className='grid grid-cols-2 gap-4'>
                  <div className='space-y-2'>
                    <Label htmlFor='assignee'>Assignee</Label>
                    <select
                      id='assignee'
                      value={formData.assigneeId}
                      onChange={(e) =>
                        setFormData({ ...formData, assigneeId: e.target.value })
                      }
                      className='w-full px-3 py-2 rounded-lg bg-secondary/50 border border-border text-foreground text-sm'
                    >
                      <option value=''>Select assignee</option>
                      {members.map((member) => (
                        <option key={member.userId} value={member.userId}>
                          {member.user.name}
                        </option>
                      ))}
                    </select>
                  </div>

                  <div className='space-y-2'>
                    <Label htmlFor='due_date'>Due Date</Label>
                    <Input
                      id='due_date'
                      type='date'
                      value={formData.due_date}
                      onChange={(e) =>
                        setFormData({ ...formData, due_date: e.target.value })
                      }
                      className='bg-secondary/50'
                    />
                  </div>
                </div>

                <div className='grid grid-cols-2 gap-4'>
                  <div className='space-y-2'>
                    <Label htmlFor='due_time'>Time (optional)</Label>
                    <Input
                      id='due_time'
                      type='time'
                      value={formData.due_time}
                      onChange={(e) =>
                        setFormData({ ...formData, due_time: e.target.value })
                      }
                      className='bg-secondary/50'
                      placeholder='Set a specific time'
                    />
                  </div>

                  <div className='space-y-2'>
                    <Label className='flex items-center gap-1.5'>
                      <Repeat className='w-3.5 h-3.5' />
                      Repeat
                    </Label>
                    <RecurrenceSelector
                      value={recurrenceRule}
                      onChange={setRecurrenceRule}
                      startDate={formData.due_date}
                    />
                  </div>
                </div>

                {recurrenceRule && (
                  <div className='p-3 rounded-lg bg-primary/10 border border-primary/20'>
                    <div className='flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-primary'>
                      <Repeat className='w-4 h-4' />
                      <span className='font-medium'>Recurring Task</span>
                    </div>
                    <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1'>
                      {getRecurrenceDescription(recurrenceRule)}
                    </p>
                  </div>
                )}

                <div className='flex justify-end gap-3 pt-4'>
                  <Button
                    type='button'
                    variant='outline'
                    onClick={() => onOpenChange(false)}
                  >
                    Cancel
                  </Button>
                  <Button
                    type='submit'
                    className='bg-primary hover:bg-primary/90'
                  >
                    Create Task
                  </Button>
                </div>
              </form>
            </div>
          </motion.div>
        </>
      )}
    </AnimatePresence>
  );
}

import { useState } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import { X, User, Bell, Palette, Save, Camera } from 'lucide-react';
import { useWorkspaceStore } from '@/store/workspaceStore';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Label } from '@/components/ui/label';
import { Switch } from '@/components/ui/switch';
import { Tabs, TabsContent, TabsList, TabsTrigger } from '@/components/ui/tabs';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { toast } from 'sonner';

interface SettingsModalProps {
  open: boolean;
  onOpenChange: (open: boolean) => void;
}

export default function SettingsModal({
  open,
  onOpenChange,
}: SettingsModalProps) {
  const { currentUser, theme, toggleTheme } = useWorkspaceStore();

  // Profile state
  const [name, setName] = useState(currentUser?.name || '');
  const [email, setEmail] = useState(currentUser?.email || '');

  // Notification preferences
  const [notifications, setNotifications] = useState({
    taskAssigned: true,
    mentions: true,
    statusChanges: true,
    dueDateReminders: true,
    projectInvites: true,
    emailDigest: false,
  });

  // Appearance
  const [accentColor, setAccentColor] = useState('blue');

  const handleSaveProfile = () => {
    toast.success('Profile updated', {
      description: 'Your profile settings have been saved.',
    });
  };

  const handleSaveNotifications = () => {
    toast.success('Notifications updated', {
      description: 'Your notification preferences have been saved.',
    });
  };

  const accentColors = [
    { name: 'blue', class: 'bg-blue-500' },
    { name: 'purple', class: 'bg-purple-500' },
    { name: 'green', class: 'bg-green-500' },
    { name: 'orange', class: 'bg-orange-500' },
    { name: 'pink', class: 'bg-pink-500' },
    { name: 'cyan', class: 'bg-cyan-500' },
  ];

  if (!open) return null;

  return (
    <AnimatePresence>
      {open && (
        <>

            initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
            className='fixed inset-0 bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-sm z-50'
            onClick={() => onOpenChange(false)}
          />

            initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95, y: 20 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1, y: 0 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95, y: 20 }}
            className='fixed left-1/2 top-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 z-50 w-full max-w-2xl mx-4'

            <div className='bg-card border border-border rounded-xl shadow-2xl overflow-hidden'>
              {/* Header */}
              <div className='flex items-center justify-between p-6 border-b border-border'>
                <h2 className='text-xl font-semibold text-foreground'>
                  Settings
                </h2>
                <button
                  onClick={() => onOpenChange(false)}
                  className='p-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-accent transition-colors'
                >
                  <X className='w-5 h-5 text-muted-foreground' />
                </button>
              </div>

              {/* Content */}
              <Tabs defaultValue='profile' className='w-full'>
                <div className='border-b border-border px-6'>
                  <TabsList className='h-12 bg-transparent gap-4'>
                    <TabsTrigger
                      value='profile'
                      className='data-[state=active]:bg-transparent data-[state=active]:border-b-2 data-[state=active]:border-primary rounded-none px-1'
                    >
                      <User className='w-4 h-4 mr-2' />
                      Profile
                    </TabsTrigger>
                    <TabsTrigger
                      value='notifications'
                      className='data-[state=active]:bg-transparent data-[state=active]:border-b-2 data-[state=active]:border-primary rounded-none px-1'
                    >
                      <Bell className='w-4 h-4 mr-2' />
                      Notifications
                    </TabsTrigger>
                    <TabsTrigger
                      value='appearance'
                      className='data-[state=active]:bg-transparent data-[state=active]:border-b-2 data-[state=active]:border-primary rounded-none px-1'
                    >
                      <Palette className='w-4 h-4 mr-2' />
                      Appearance
                    </TabsTrigger>
                  </TabsList>
                </div>

                {/* Profile Tab */}
                <TabsContent value='profile' className='p-6 space-y-6'>
                  {/* Avatar */}
                  <div className='flex items-center gap-4'>
                    <div className='relative'>
                      <div className='w-20 h-20 rounded-full bg-gradient-to-br from-primary to-cyan-400 flex items-center justify-center text-primary-foreground text-2xl font-semibold'>
                        {name?.charAt(0) || 'U'}
                      </div>
                      <button className='absolute bottom-0 right-0 p-1.5 bg-primary rounded-full text-primary-foreground hover:bg-primary/90 transition-colors'>
                        <Camera className='w-3.5 h-3.5' />
                      </button>
                    </div>
                    <div>
                      <p className='font-medium text-foreground'>
                        {name || 'User'}
                      </p>
                      <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>
                        {email || 'user@example.com'}
                      </p>
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  {/* Form */}
                  <div className='grid gap-4'>
                    <div className='grid gap-2'>
                      <Label htmlFor='name'>Full Name</Label>
                      <Input
                        id='name'
                        value={name}
                        onChange={(e) => setName(e.target.value)}
                        placeholder='Enter your name'
                      />
                    </div>
                    <div className='grid gap-2'>
                      <Label htmlFor='email'>Email Address</Label>
                      <Input
                        id='email'
                        type='email'
                        value={email}
                        onChange={(e) => setEmail(e.target.value)}
                        placeholder='Enter your email'
                      />
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  <Button
                    onClick={handleSaveProfile}
                    className='w-full sm:w-auto'
                  >
                    <Save className='w-4 h-4 mr-2' />
                    Save Changes
                  </Button>
                </TabsContent>

                {/* Notifications Tab */}
                <TabsContent value='notifications' className='p-6 space-y-6'>
                  <div className='space-y-4'>
                    <div className='flex items-center justify-between py-3 border-b border-border'>
                      <div>
                        <p className='font-medium text-foreground'>
                          Task Assigned
                        </p>
                        <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>
                          Get notified when a task is assigned to you
                        </p>
                      </div>
                      <Switch
                        checked={notifications.taskAssigned}
                        onCheckedChange={(checked) =>
                          setNotifications((prev) => ({
                            ...prev,
                            taskAssigned: checked,
                          }))
                        }
                      />
                    </div>

                    <div className='flex items-center justify-between py-3 border-b border-border'>
                      <div>
                        <p className='font-medium text-foreground'>Mentions</p>
                        <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>
                          Get notified when someone mentions you in a comment
                        </p>
                      </div>
                      <Switch
                        checked={notifications.mentions}
                        onCheckedChange={(checked) =>
                          setNotifications((prev) => ({
                            ...prev,
                            mentions: checked,
                          }))
                        }
                      />
                    </div>

                    <div className='flex items-center justify-between py-3 border-b border-border'>
                      <div>
                        <p className='font-medium text-foreground'>
                          Status Changes
                        </p>
                        <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>
                          Get notified when task status changes
                        </p>
                      </div>
                      <Switch
                        checked={notifications.statusChanges}
                        onCheckedChange={(checked) =>
                          setNotifications((prev) => ({
                            ...prev,
                            statusChanges: checked,
                          }))
                        }
                      />
                    </div>

                    <div className='flex items-center justify-between py-3 border-b border-border'>
                      <div>
                        <p className='font-medium text-foreground'>
                          Due Date Reminders
                        </p>
                        <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>
                          Receive reminders before task due dates
                        </p>
                      </div>
                      <Switch
                        checked={notifications.dueDateReminders}
                        onCheckedChange={(checked) =>
                          setNotifications((prev) => ({
                            ...prev,
                            dueDateReminders: checked,
                          }))
                        }
                      />
                    </div>

                    <div className='flex items-center justify-between py-3 border-b border-border'>
                      <div>
                        <p className='font-medium text-foreground'>
                          Project Invites
                        </p>
                        <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>
                          Get notified about project invitations
                        </p>
                      </div>
                      <Switch
                        checked={notifications.projectInvites}
                        onCheckedChange={(checked) =>
                          setNotifications((prev) => ({
                            ...prev,
                            projectInvites: checked,
                          }))
                        }
                      />
                    </div>

                    <div className='flex items-center justify-between py-3'>
                      <div>
                        <p className='font-medium text-foreground'>
                          Email Digest
                        </p>
                        <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>
                          Receive a daily email summary of activity
                        </p>
                      </div>
                      <Switch
                        checked={notifications.emailDigest}
                        onCheckedChange={(checked) =>
                          setNotifications((prev) => ({
                            ...prev,
                            emailDigest: checked,
                          }))
                        }
                      />
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  <Button
                    onClick={handleSaveNotifications}
                    className='w-full sm:w-auto'
                  >
                    <Save className='w-4 h-4 mr-2' />
                    Save Preferences
                  </Button>
                </TabsContent>

                {/* Appearance Tab */}
                <TabsContent value='appearance' className='p-6 space-y-6'>
                  {/* Theme */}
                  <div className='space-y-3'>
                    <Label>Theme</Label>
                    <div className='grid grid-cols-2 gap-3'>
                      <button
                        onClick={() => theme === 'dark' && toggleTheme()}
                        className={cn(
                          'p-4 rounded-lg border-2 transition-all flex flex-col items-center gap-2',
                          theme === 'light'
                            ? 'border-primary bg-primary/5'
                            : 'border-border hover:border-muted-foreground',
                        )}
                      >
                        <div className='w-full h-16 rounded bg-white border border-gray-200 flex items-center justify-center'>
                          <div className='w-8 h-8 rounded bg-gray-100' />
                        </div>
                        <span className='text-sm font-medium'>Light</span>
                      </button>
                      <button
                        onClick={() => theme === 'light' && toggleTheme()}
                        className={cn(
                          'p-4 rounded-lg border-2 transition-all flex flex-col items-center gap-2',
                          theme === 'dark'
                            ? 'border-primary bg-primary/5'
                            : 'border-border hover:border-muted-foreground',
                        )}
                      >
                        <div className='w-full h-16 rounded bg-gray-900 border border-gray-700 flex items-center justify-center'>
                          <div className='w-8 h-8 rounded bg-gray-800' />
                        </div>
                        <span className='text-sm font-medium'>Dark</span>
                      </button>
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  {/* Accent Color */}
                  <div className='space-y-3'>
                    <Label>Accent Color</Label>
                    <div className='flex gap-3'>
                      {accentColors.map((color) => (
                        <button
                          key={color.name}
                          onClick={() => setAccentColor(color.name)}
                          className={cn(
                            'w-10 h-10 rounded-full transition-all',
                            color.class,
                            accentColor === color.name
                              ? 'ring-2 ring-offset-2 ring-offset-background ring-primary scale-110'
                              : 'hover:scale-105',
                          )}
                        />
                      ))}
                    </div>
                    <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                      Accent color customization coming soon
                    </p>
                  </div>

                  {/* Compact Mode */}
                  <div className='flex items-center justify-between py-3 border-t border-border'>
                    <div>
                      <p className='font-medium text-foreground'>
                        Compact Mode
                      </p>
                      <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>
                        Reduce spacing for a denser layout
                      </p>
                    </div>
                    <Switch />
                  </div>

                  {/* Animations */}
                  <div className='flex items-center justify-between py-3 border-t border-border'>
                    <div>
                      <p className='font-medium text-foreground'>
                        Reduce Animations
                      </p>
                      <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>
                        Minimize motion for accessibility
                      </p>
                    </div>
                    <Switch />
                  </div>
                </TabsContent>
              </Tabs>
            </div>
          </motion.div>
        </>
      )}
    </AnimatePresence>
  );
}
