import { useState, useMemo, useRef } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import {
  X,
  Calendar,
  User,
  Tag,
  AlertCircle,
  CheckCircle2,
  Clock,
  Edit3,
  Save,
  MessageSquare,
  Activity,
  CheckSquare,
  Plus,
  Send,
  AtSign,
  Link2,
  ArrowRight,
  Search,
  XCircle,
  Network,
} from 'lucide-react';
import {
  useWorkspaceStore,
  type CommentType,
  type Task,
  type User as UserType,
} from '@/store/workspaceStore';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Textarea } from '@/components/ui/textarea';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import {
  format,
  isValid,
  parseISO,
  isBefore,
  formatDistanceToNow,
} from 'date-fns';
import DependencyGraph from '@/components/calendar/DependencyGraph';

interface TaskDetailModalProps {
  task: Task;
  projectId: string;
  isOpen: boolean;
  onClose: () => void;
}

const statusOptions: { value: Task['status']; label: string; color: string }[] =
  [
    {
      value: 'TODO',
      label: 'To Do',
      color: 'bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground',
    },
    {
      value: 'IN_PROGRESS',
      label: 'In Progress',
      color: 'bg-warning/20 text-warning',
    },
    { value: 'REVIEW', label: 'Review', color: 'bg-primary/20 text-primary' },
    { value: 'DONE', label: 'Done', color: 'bg-success/20 text-success' },
  ];

const priorityOptions: {
  value: Task['priority'];
  label: string;
  color: string;
}[] = [
  { value: 'LOW', label: 'Low', color: 'bg-muted text-muted-foreground' },
  { value: 'MEDIUM', label: 'Medium', color: 'bg-warning/20 text-warning' },
  { value: 'HIGH', label: 'High', color: 'bg-destructive/20 text-destructive' },
  {
    value: 'URGENT',
    label: 'Urgent',
    color: 'bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground',
  },
];

const typeOptions: { value: Task['type']; label: string; color: string }[] = [
  { value: 'TASK', label: 'Task', color: 'bg-success/10 text-success' },
  { value: 'BUG', label: 'Bug', color: 'bg-destructive/10 text-destructive' },
  { value: 'FEATURE', label: 'Feature', color: 'bg-primary/10 text-primary' },
  {
    value: 'IMPROVEMENT',
    label: 'Improvement',
    color: 'bg-violet-500/10 text-violet-500',
  },
  { value: 'OTHER', label: 'Other', color: 'bg-warning/10 text-warning' },
];

const safeParseDate = (dateString: string | undefined | null): Date | null => {
  if (!dateString) return null;
  const date = parseISO(dateString);
  return isValid(date) ? date : null;
};

// Helper to render comment content with highlighted mentions
const renderCommentContent = (
  content: string,
  members: { userId: string; user: UserType }[],
) => {
  const mentionRegex = /@(\w+(?:\s\w+)?)/g;
  const parts = content.split(mentionRegex);

  return parts.map((part, index) => {
    const mentionedUser = members.find(
      (m) => m.user.name.toLowerCase() === part.toLowerCase(),
    );
    if (mentionedUser) {
      return (
        <span
          key={index}
          className='text-primary font-medium bg-primary/10 px-1 rounded'
        >
          @{mentionedUser.user.name}
        </span>
      );
    }
    return part;
  });
};

export default function TaskDetailModal({
  task,
  projectId,
  isOpen,
  onClose,
}: TaskDetailModalProps) {
  const {
    currentWorkspace,
    currentUser,
    updateTask,
    addSubtask,
    toggleSubtask,
    addComment,
  } = useWorkspaceStore();
  const project = currentWorkspace?.projects.find((p) => p.id === projectId);
  const members = project?.members || [];

  // Get all tasks from the project for dependency selection
  const allProjectTasks = project?.tasks || [];

  const [isEditing, setIsEditing] = useState(false);
  const [editedTask, setEditedTask] = useState<Task>(task);
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState<
    'details' | 'dependencies' | 'comments' | 'subtasks' | 'activity'
  >('details');
  const [newSubtask, setNewSubtask] = useState('');

  // Comments state
  const [commentText, setCommentText] = useState('');
  const [showMentions, setShowMentions] = useState(false);
  const [mentionSearch, setMentionSearch] = useState('');
  const [cursorPosition, setCursorPosition] = useState(0);
  const commentInputRef = useRef<HTMLTextAreaElement>(null);

  // Dependencies state
  const [dependencySearch, setDependencySearch] = useState('');
  const [showBlockerDropdown, setShowBlockerDropdown] = useState(false);
  const [showBlockingDropdown, setShowBlockingDropdown] = useState(false);
  const [showDependencyGraph, setShowDependencyGraph] = useState(false);

  // Filter tasks for dependency dropdowns (exclude current task and already linked tasks)
  const availableBlockerTasks = useMemo(() => {
    const currentBlockers = task.blockedBy || [];
    return allProjectTasks.filter(
      (t) =>
        t.id !== task.id &&
        !currentBlockers.includes(t.id) &&
        t.title.toLowerCase().includes(dependencySearch.toLowerCase()),
    );
  }, [allProjectTasks, task.id, task.blockedBy, dependencySearch]);

  const availableBlockingTasks = useMemo(() => {
    const currentBlocking = task.blocking || [];
    return allProjectTasks.filter(
      (t) =>
        t.id !== task.id &&
        !currentBlocking.includes(t.id) &&
        t.title.toLowerCase().includes(dependencySearch.toLowerCase()),
    );
  }, [allProjectTasks, task.id, task.blocking, dependencySearch]);

  // Get task details by ID
  const getTaskById = (taskId: string) =>
    allProjectTasks.find((t) => t.id === taskId);

  // Add a blocker (this task is blocked by another)
  const addBlocker = (blockerId: string) => {
    const blockerTask = getTaskById(blockerId);
    if (!blockerTask) return;

    const updatedTask = {
      ...task,
      blockedBy: [...(task.blockedBy || []), blockerId],
      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    };

    // Also update the blocker task to include this task in its blocking array
    const updatedBlocker = {
      ...blockerTask,
      blocking: [...(blockerTask.blocking || []), task.id],
      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    };

    updateTask(updatedTask);
    updateTask(updatedBlocker);
    setDependencySearch('');
    setShowBlockerDropdown(false);
  };

  // Remove a blocker
  const removeBlocker = (blockerId: string) => {
    const blockerTask = getTaskById(blockerId);

    const updatedTask = {
      ...task,
      blockedBy: (task.blockedBy || []).filter((id) => id !== blockerId),
      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    };

    updateTask(updatedTask);

    // Also remove this task from the blocker's blocking array
    if (blockerTask) {
      const updatedBlocker = {
        ...blockerTask,
        blocking: (blockerTask.blocking || []).filter((id) => id !== task.id),
        updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      };
      updateTask(updatedBlocker);
    }
  };

  // Add a task that this task blocks
  const addBlocking = (blockedId: string) => {
    const blockedTask = getTaskById(blockedId);
    if (!blockedTask) return;

    const updatedTask = {
      ...task,
      blocking: [...(task.blocking || []), blockedId],
      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    };

    // Also update the blocked task
    const updatedBlocked = {
      ...blockedTask,
      blockedBy: [...(blockedTask.blockedBy || []), task.id],
      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    };

    updateTask(updatedTask);
    updateTask(updatedBlocked);
    setDependencySearch('');
    setShowBlockingDropdown(false);
  };

  // Remove a task that this task blocks
  const removeBlocking = (blockedId: string) => {
    const blockedTask = getTaskById(blockedId);

    const updatedTask = {
      ...task,
      blocking: (task.blocking || []).filter((id) => id !== blockedId),
      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    };

    updateTask(updatedTask);

    if (blockedTask) {
      const updatedBlocked = {
        ...blockedTask,
        blockedBy: (blockedTask.blockedBy || []).filter((id) => id !== task.id),
        updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      };
      updateTask(updatedBlocked);
    }
  };

  // Filter members for mention dropdown
  const filteredMembers = useMemo(() => {
    if (!mentionSearch) return members;
    return members.filter((m) =>
      m.user.name.toLowerCase().includes(mentionSearch.toLowerCase()),
    );
  }, [members, mentionSearch]);

  // Handle comment input changes and detect @mentions
  const handleCommentChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLTextAreaElement>) => {
    const value = e.target.value;
    const position = e.target.selectionStart || 0;
    setCommentText(value);
    setCursorPosition(position);

    // Check if we're typing a mention
    const textBeforeCursor = value.slice(0, position);
    const mentionMatch = textBeforeCursor.match(/@(\w*)$/);

    if (mentionMatch) {
      setShowMentions(true);
      setMentionSearch(mentionMatch[1]);
    } else {
      setShowMentions(false);
      setMentionSearch('');
    }
  };

  // Insert mention into comment
  const insertMention = (member: { userId: string; user: UserType }) => {
    const textBeforeCursor = commentText.slice(0, cursorPosition);
    const textAfterCursor = commentText.slice(cursorPosition);
    const mentionStart = textBeforeCursor.lastIndexOf('@');

    const newText =
      textBeforeCursor.slice(0, mentionStart) +
      `@${member.user.name} ` +
      textAfterCursor;

    setCommentText(newText);
    setShowMentions(false);
    setMentionSearch('');

    // Focus back on input
    setTimeout(() => {
      commentInputRef.current?.focus();
    }, 0);
  };

  // Submit comment
  const handleSubmitComment = () => {
    if (!commentText.trim() || !currentUser) return;

    // Extract mentions from comment
    const mentionRegex = /@(\w+(?:\s\w+)?)/g;
    const mentions: string[] = [];
    let match;

    while ((match = mentionRegex.exec(commentText)) !== null) {
      const mentionedUser = members.find(
        (m) => m.user.name.toLowerCase() === match[1].toLowerCase(),
      );
      if (mentionedUser) {
        mentions.push(mentionedUser.userId);
      }
    }

    const newComment: Comment = {
      id: `comment-${Date.now()}`,
      taskId: task.id,
      content: commentText.trim(),
      user: currentUser,
      mentions,
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    };

    addComment(task.id, projectId, newComment);
    setCommentText('');
  };

  const dueDate = safeParseDate(task.due_date);
  const isOverdue =
    dueDate && isBefore(dueDate, new Date()) && task.status !== 'DONE';

  const handleSave = () => {
    updateTask({ ...editedTask, updatedAt: new Date().toISOString() });
    setIsEditing(false);
  };

  const handleAddSubtask = () => {
    if (!newSubtask.trim()) return;
    addSubtask(task.id, projectId, {
      id: `subtask-${Date.now()}`,
      title: newSubtask.trim(),
      completed: false,
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    });
    setNewSubtask('');
  };

  const handleToggleSubtask = (subtaskId: string) => {
    toggleSubtask(task.id, projectId, subtaskId);
  };

  const completedSubtasks =
    task.subtasks?.filter((s) => s.completed).length || 0;
  const totalSubtasks = task.subtasks?.length || 0;

  if (!isOpen) return null;

  return (
    <AnimatePresence>
      {isOpen && (
        <>
          {/* Backdrop */}
          <motion.div
            initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
            className='fixed inset-0 bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-sm z-50'
            onClick={onClose}
          />

          {/* Modal */}
          <motion.div
            initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95, y: 20 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1, y: 0 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95, y: 20 }}
            transition={{ duration: 0.2 }}
            className='fixed inset-4 md:inset-auto md:left-1/2 md:top-1/2 md:-translate-x-1/2 md:-translate-y-1/2 md:w-full md:max-w-2xl md:max-h-[85vh] bg-card border border-border rounded-xl shadow-2xl z-50 overflow-hidden flex flex-col'
          >
            {/* Header */}
            <div className='flex items-center justify-between p-4 border-b border-border'>
              <div className='flex items-center gap-3'>
                <span
                  className={cn(
                    'px-2 py-1 rounded text-xs font-medium',
                    typeOptions.find((t) => t.value === task.type)?.color,
                  )}
                >
                  {task.type}
                </span>
                <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                  Created {format(parseISO(task.createdAt), 'MMM d, yyyy')}
                </span>
              </div>
              <div className='flex items-center gap-2'>
                {isEditing ? (
                  <Button size='sm' onClick={handleSave} className='gap-1'>
                    <Save className='w-3 h-3' />
                    Save
                  </Button>
                ) : (
                  <Button
                    size='sm'
                    variant='ghost'
                    onClick={() => setIsEditing(true)}
                    className='gap-1'
                  >
                    <Edit3 className='w-3 h-3' />
                    Edit
                  </Button>
                )}
                <button
                  onClick={onClose}
                  className='p-2 hover:bg-secondary rounded-lg transition-colors'
                >
                  <X className='w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground' />
                </button>
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Content */}
            <div className='flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-4 space-y-6'>
              {/* Title */}
              {isEditing ? (
                <Input
                  value={editedTask.title}
                  onChange={(e) =>
                    setEditedTask({ ...editedTask, title: e.target.value })
                  }
                  className='text-xl font-semibold'
                  placeholder='Task title'
                />
              ) : (
                <h2 className='text-xl font-semibold text-foreground'>
                  {task.title}
                </h2>
              )}

              {/* Tabs */}
              <div className='flex items-center gap-1 p-1 bg-secondary/50 rounded-lg w-fit overflow-x-auto'>
                {[
                  { id: 'details', label: 'Details', icon: Tag },
                  {
                    id: 'dependencies',
                    label: `Dependencies (${(task.blockedBy?.length || 0) + (task.blocking?.length || 0)})`,
                    icon: Link2,
                  },
                  {
                    id: 'comments',
                    label: `Comments (${task.comments?.length || 0})`,
                    icon: MessageSquare,
                  },
                  {
                    id: 'subtasks',
                    label: `Subtasks (${completedSubtasks}/${totalSubtasks})`,
                    icon: CheckSquare,
                  },
                  { id: 'activity', label: 'Activity', icon: Activity },
                ].map((tab) => (
                  <button
                    key={tab.id}
                    onClick={() => setActiveTab(tab.id as any)}
                    className={cn(
                      'flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all whitespace-nowrap',
                      activeTab === tab.id
                        ? 'bg-background text-foreground shadow-sm'
                        : 'text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground',
                    )}
                  >
                    <tab.icon className='w-3 h-3' />
                    {tab.label}
                  </button>
                ))}
              </div>

              {/* Details Tab */}
              {activeTab === 'details' && (
                <div className='space-y-4'>
                  {/* Description */}
                  <div>
                    <label className='text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground mb-2 block'>
                      Description
                    </label>
                    {isEditing ? (
                      <Textarea
                        value={editedTask.description}
                        onChange={(e) =>
                          setEditedTask({
                            ...editedTask,
                            description: e.target.value,
                          })
                        }
                        rows={3}
                        placeholder='Add a description...'
                      />
                    ) : (
                      <p className='text-foreground'>
                        {task.description || 'No description'}
                      </p>
                    )}
                  </div>

                  {/* Grid of properties */}
                  <div className='grid grid-cols-2 gap-4'>
                    {/* Status */}
                    <div>
                      <label className='text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground mb-2 flex items-center gap-2'>
                        <Clock className='w-3 h-3' />
                        Status
                      </label>
                      {isEditing ? (
                        <select
                          value={editedTask.status}
                          onChange={(e) =>
                            setEditedTask({
                              ...editedTask,
                              status: e.target.value as Task['status'],
                            })
                          }
                          className='w-full px-3 py-2 rounded-lg bg-secondary/50 border border-border text-sm'
                        >
                          {statusOptions.map((opt) => (
                            <option key={opt.value} value={opt.value}>
                              {opt.label}
                            </option>
                          ))}
                        </select>
                      ) : (
                        <span
                          className={cn(
                            'inline-flex px-3 py-1 rounded text-sm font-medium',
                            statusOptions.find((s) => s.value === task.status)
                              ?.color,
                          )}
                        >
                          {
                            statusOptions.find((s) => s.value === task.status)
                              ?.label
                          }
                        </span>
                      )}
                    </div>

                    {/* Priority */}
                    <div>
                      <label className='text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground mb-2 flex items-center gap-2'>
                        <AlertCircle className='w-3 h-3' />
                        Priority
                      </label>
                      {isEditing ? (
                        <select
                          value={editedTask.priority}
                          onChange={(e) =>
                            setEditedTask({
                              ...editedTask,
                              priority: e.target.value as Task['priority'],
                            })
                          }
                          className='w-full px-3 py-2 rounded-lg bg-secondary/50 border border-border text-sm'
                        >
                          {priorityOptions.map((opt) => (
                            <option key={opt.value} value={opt.value}>
                              {opt.label}
                            </option>
                          ))}
                        </select>
                      ) : (
                        <span
                          className={cn(
                            'inline-flex px-3 py-1 rounded text-sm font-medium',
                            priorityOptions.find(
                              (p) => p.value === task.priority,
                            )?.color,
                          )}
                        >
                          {
                            priorityOptions.find(
                              (p) => p.value === task.priority,
                            )?.label
                          }
                        </span>
                      )}
                    </div>

                    {/* Type */}
                    <div>
                      <label className='text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground mb-2 flex items-center gap-2'>
                        <Tag className='w-3 h-3' />
                        Type
                      </label>
                      {isEditing ? (
                        <select
                          value={editedTask.type}
                          onChange={(e) =>
                            setEditedTask({
                              ...editedTask,
                              type: e.target.value as Task['type'],
                            })
                          }
                          className='w-full px-3 py-2 rounded-lg bg-secondary/50 border border-border text-sm'
                        >
                          {typeOptions.map((opt) => (
                            <option key={opt.value} value={opt.value}>
                              {opt.label}
                            </option>
                          ))}
                        </select>
                      ) : (
                        <span
                          className={cn(
                            'inline-flex px-3 py-1 rounded text-sm font-medium',
                            typeOptions.find((t) => t.value === task.type)
                              ?.color,
                          )}
                        >
                          {
                            typeOptions.find((t) => t.value === task.type)
                              ?.label
                          }
                        </span>
                      )}
                    </div>

                    {/* Due Date */}
                    <div>
                      <label className='text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground mb-2 flex items-center gap-2'>
                        <Calendar className='w-3 h-3' />
                        Due Date
                      </label>
                      {isEditing ? (
                        <Input
                          type='date'
                          value={
                            editedTask.due_date
                              ? format(
                                  parseISO(editedTask.due_date),
                                  'yyyy-MM-dd',
                                )
                              : ''
                          }
                          onChange={(e) =>
                            setEditedTask({
                              ...editedTask,
                              due_date: new Date(e.target.value).toISOString(),
                            })
                          }
                        />
                      ) : (
                        <span
                          className={cn(
                            'inline-flex items-center gap-2 text-sm',
                            isOverdue ? 'text-destructive' : 'text-foreground',
                          )}
                        >
                          <Calendar className='w-4 h-4' />
                          {dueDate
                            ? format(dueDate, 'MMM d, yyyy')
                            : 'No due date'}
                          {isOverdue && (
                            <span className='text-destructive text-xs'>
                              (Overdue)
                            </span>
                          )}
                        </span>
                      )}
                    </div>

                    {/* Due Time */}
                    <div>
                      <label className='text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground mb-2 flex items-center gap-2'>
                        <Clock className='w-3 h-3' />
                        Time
                      </label>
                      {isEditing ? (
                        <Input
                          type='time'
                          value={editedTask.due_time || ''}
                          onChange={(e) =>
                            setEditedTask({
                              ...editedTask,
                              due_time: e.target.value,
                            })
                          }
                        />
                      ) : (
                        <span className='inline-flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-foreground'>
                          <Clock className='w-4 h-4' />
                          {task.due_time
                            ? format(
                                parseISO(`2000-01-01T${task.due_time}`),
                                'h:mm a',
                              )
                            : 'No time set'}
                        </span>
                      )}
                    </div>

                    {/* Assignee */}
                    <div className='col-span-2'>
                      <label className='text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground mb-2 flex items-center gap-2'>
                        <User className='w-3 h-3' />
                        Assignee
                      </label>
                      {isEditing ? (
                        <select
                          value={editedTask.assigneeId}
                          onChange={(e) => {
                            const member = members.find(
                              (m) => m.userId === e.target.value,
                            );
                            if (member) {
                              setEditedTask({
                                ...editedTask,
                                assigneeId: member.userId,
                                assignee: member.user,
                              });
                            }
                          }}
                          className='w-full px-3 py-2 rounded-lg bg-secondary/50 border border-border text-sm'
                        >
                          {members.map((member) => (
                            <option key={member.userId} value={member.userId}>
                              {member.user.name}
                            </option>
                          ))}
                        </select>
                      ) : (
                        <div className='flex items-center gap-3'>
                          <div className='w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-gradient-to-br from-primary to-cyan-400 flex items-center justify-center text-xs font-medium text-primary-foreground'>
                            {task.assignee?.name?.charAt(0) || '?'}
                          </div>
                          <div>
                            <p className='text-sm font-medium text-foreground'>
                              {task.assignee?.name}
                            </p>
                            <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                              {task.assignee?.email}
                            </p>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}

              {/* Dependencies Tab */}
              {activeTab === 'dependencies' && (
                <div className='space-y-6'>
                  {/* Blocked By Section */}
                  <div className='space-y-3'>
                    <div className='flex items-center justify-between'>
                      <label className='text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground flex items-center gap-2'>
                        <AlertCircle className='w-4 h-4 text-destructive' />
                        Blocked By
                        <span className='text-xs bg-destructive/20 text-destructive px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded'>
                          {task.blockedBy?.length || 0}
                        </span>
                      </label>
                    </div>

                    {/* Current Blockers */}
                    <div className='space-y-2'>
                      {!task.blockedBy || task.blockedBy.length === 0 ? (
                        <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground italic'>
                          No blocking tasks
                        </p>
                      ) : (
                        task.blockedBy.map((blockerId) => {
                          const blockerTask = getTaskById(blockerId);
                          if (!blockerTask) return null;
                          return (
                            <motion.div
                              key={blockerId}
                              initial={{ opacity: 0, x: -10 }}
                              animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
                              className='flex items-center justify-between p-3 bg-destructive/10 border border-destructive/20 rounded-lg group'
                            >
                              <div className='flex items-center gap-3'>
                                <div
                                  className={cn(
                                    'w-2 h-2 rounded-full',
                                    blockerTask.status === 'DONE'
                                      ? 'bg-success'
                                      : 'bg-destructive',
                                  )}
                                />
                                <div>
                                  <p
                                    className={cn(
                                      'text-sm font-medium',
                                      blockerTask.status === 'DONE' &&
                                        'line-through text-muted-foreground',
                                    )}
                                  >
                                    {blockerTask.title}
                                  </p>
                                  <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                                    {blockerTask.status.replace('_', ' ')} •{' '}
                                    {blockerTask.priority}
                                  </p>
                                </div>
                              </div>
                              <button
                                onClick={() => removeBlocker(blockerId)}
                                className='opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 p-1 hover:bg-destructive/20 rounded transition-all'
                              >
                                <XCircle className='w-4 h-4 text-destructive' />
                              </button>
                            </motion.div>
                          );
                        })
                      )}
                    </div>

                    {/* Add Blocker Dropdown */}
                    <div className='relative'>
                      <div className='flex gap-2'>
                        <div className='relative flex-1'>
                          <Search className='absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground' />
                          <input
                            type='text'
                            value={dependencySearch}
                            onChange={(e) => {
                              setDependencySearch(e.target.value);
                              setShowBlockerDropdown(true);
                              setShowBlockingDropdown(false);
                            }}
                            onFocus={() => {
                              setShowBlockerDropdown(true);
                              setShowBlockingDropdown(false);
                            }}
                            placeholder='Search tasks to add as blocker...'
                            className='w-full pl-9 pr-3 py-2 rounded-lg bg-secondary/50 border border-border text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-primary/50'
                          />
                        </div>
                      </div>

                      {/* Blocker Dropdown */}
                      <AnimatePresence>
                        {showBlockerDropdown &&
                          availableBlockerTasks.length > 0 && (
                            <motion.div
                              initial={{ opacity: 0, y: -10 }}
                              animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                              exit={{ opacity: 0, y: -10 }}
                              className='absolute left-0 right-0 top-full mt-1 bg-card border border-border rounded-lg shadow-xl z-50 max-h-48 overflow-y-auto'
                            >
                              <div className='p-1'>
                                {availableBlockerTasks.slice(0, 10).map((t) => (
                                  <button
                                    key={t.id}
                                    onClick={() => addBlocker(t.id)}
                                    className='w-full flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2 hover:bg-secondary rounded-md transition-colors text-left'
                                  >
                                    <div
                                      className={cn(
                                        'w-2 h-2 rounded-full flex-shrink-0',
                                        t.status === 'DONE'
                                          ? 'bg-success'
                                          : t.status === 'IN_PROGRESS'
                                            ? 'bg-warning'
                                            : 'bg-muted-foreground',
                                      )}
                                    />
                                    <div className='flex-1 min-w-0'>
                                      <p className='text-sm font-medium truncate'>
                                        {t.title}
                                      </p>
                                      <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                                        {t.status.replace('_', ' ')} •{' '}
                                        {t.assignee?.name}
                                      </p>
                                    </div>
                                    <Plus className='w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground flex-shrink-0' />
                                  </button>
                                ))}
                              </div>
                            </motion.div>
                          )}
                      </AnimatePresence>
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  {/* Divider */}
                  <div className='border-t border-border' />

                  {/* Blocking Section */}
                  <div className='space-y-3'>
                    <div className='flex items-center justify-between'>
                      <label className='text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground flex items-center gap-2'>
                        <ArrowRight className='w-4 h-4 text-primary' />
                        Blocking
                        <span className='text-xs bg-primary/20 text-primary px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded'>
                          {task.blocking?.length || 0}
                        </span>
                      </label>
                    </div>

                    {/* Current Blocking Tasks */}
                    <div className='space-y-2'>
                      {!task.blocking || task.blocking.length === 0 ? (
                        <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground italic'>
                          Not blocking any tasks
                        </p>
                      ) : (
                        task.blocking.map((blockedId) => {
                          const blockedTask = getTaskById(blockedId);
                          if (!blockedTask) return null;
                          return (
                            <motion.div
                              key={blockedId}
                              initial={{ opacity: 0, x: -10 }}
                              animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
                              className='flex items-center justify-between p-3 bg-primary/10 border border-primary/20 rounded-lg group'
                            >
                              <div className='flex items-center gap-3'>
                                <div
                                  className={cn(
                                    'w-2 h-2 rounded-full',
                                    blockedTask.status === 'DONE'
                                      ? 'bg-success'
                                      : 'bg-primary',
                                  )}
                                />
                                <div>
                                  <p
                                    className={cn(
                                      'text-sm font-medium',
                                      blockedTask.status === 'DONE' &&
                                        'line-through text-muted-foreground',
                                    )}
                                  >
                                    {blockedTask.title}
                                  </p>
                                  <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                                    {blockedTask.status.replace('_', ' ')} •{' '}
                                    {blockedTask.priority}
                                  </p>
                                </div>
                              </div>
                              <button
                                onClick={() => removeBlocking(blockedId)}
                                className='opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 p-1 hover:bg-primary/20 rounded transition-all'
                              >
                                <XCircle className='w-4 h-4 text-primary' />
                              </button>
                            </motion.div>
                          );
                        })
                      )}
                    </div>

                    {/* Add Blocking Dropdown */}
                    <div className='relative'>
                      <div className='flex gap-2'>
                        <div className='relative flex-1'>
                          <Search className='absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground' />
                          <input
                            type='text'
                            value={dependencySearch}
                            onChange={(e) => {
                              setDependencySearch(e.target.value);
                              setShowBlockingDropdown(true);
                              setShowBlockerDropdown(false);
                            }}
                            onFocus={() => {
                              setShowBlockingDropdown(true);
                              setShowBlockerDropdown(false);
                            }}
                            placeholder='Search tasks this blocks...'
                            className='w-full pl-9 pr-3 py-2 rounded-lg bg-secondary/50 border border-border text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-primary/50'
                          />
                        </div>
                      </div>

                      {/* Blocking Dropdown */}
                      <AnimatePresence>
                        {showBlockingDropdown &&
                          availableBlockingTasks.length > 0 && (
                            <motion.div
                              initial={{ opacity: 0, y: -10 }}
                              animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                              exit={{ opacity: 0, y: -10 }}
                              className='absolute left-0 right-0 top-full mt-1 bg-card border border-border rounded-lg shadow-xl z-50 max-h-48 overflow-y-auto'
                            >
                              <div className='p-1'>
                                {availableBlockingTasks
                                  .slice(0, 10)
                                  .map((t) => (
                                    <button
                                      key={t.id}
                                      onClick={() => addBlocking(t.id)}
                                      className='w-full flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2 hover:bg-secondary rounded-md transition-colors text-left'
                                    >
                                      <div
                                        className={cn(
                                          'w-2 h-2 rounded-full flex-shrink-0',
                                          t.status === 'DONE'
                                            ? 'bg-success'
                                            : t.status === 'IN_PROGRESS'
                                              ? 'bg-warning'
                                              : 'bg-muted-foreground',
                                        )}
                                      />
                                      <div className='flex-1 min-w-0'>
                                        <p className='text-sm font-medium truncate'>
                                          {t.title}
                                        </p>
                                        <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                                          {t.status.replace('_', ' ')} •{' '}
                                          {t.assignee?.name}
                                        </p>
                                      </div>
                                      <Plus className='w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground flex-shrink-0' />
                                    </button>
                                  ))}
                              </div>
                            </motion.div>
                          )}
                      </AnimatePresence>
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  {/* Dependency Summary & Graph Button */}
                  <div className='p-4 bg-secondary/30 rounded-lg border border-border'>
                    <div className='flex items-center justify-between mb-3'>
                      <div className='flex items-center gap-2'>
                        <Link2 className='w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground' />
                        <span className='text-sm font-medium text-foreground'>
                          Dependency Summary
                        </span>
                      </div>
                      <Button
                        variant='outline'
                        size='sm'
                        className='gap-1.5'
                        onClick={() => setShowDependencyGraph(true)}
                      >
                        <Network className='w-3.5 h-3.5' />
                        View Graph
                      </Button>
                    </div>
                    <div className='grid grid-cols-2 gap-4 text-sm'>
                      <div>
                        <span className='text-muted-foreground'>
                          Waiting on:{' '}
                        </span>
                        <span className='font-medium text-destructive'>
                          {task.blockedBy?.length || 0} task(s)
                        </span>
                      </div>
                      <div>
                        <span className='text-muted-foreground'>
                          Blocking:{' '}
                        </span>
                        <span className='font-medium text-primary'>
                          {task.blocking?.length || 0} task(s)
                        </span>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}

              {/* Dependency Graph Modal */}
              <AnimatePresence>
                {showDependencyGraph && (
                  <motion.div
                    initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
                    animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
                    exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
                    className='fixed inset-0 z-[60] bg-background/95 backdrop-blur-sm'
                  >
                    <div className='absolute inset-4'>
                      <div className='h-full'>
                        <div className='flex items-center justify-between mb-4'>
                          <div>
                            <h2 className='text-lg font-semibold text-foreground'>
                              Dependency Graph
                            </h2>
                            <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>
                              Visualizing task dependencies for {project?.name}
                            </p>
                          </div>
                          <Button
                            variant='outline'
                            size='sm'
                            onClick={() => setShowDependencyGraph(false)}
                            className='gap-1.5'
                          >
                            <X className='w-4 h-4' />
                            Close
                          </Button>
                        </div>
                        <div className='h-[calc(100%-60px)]'>
                          <DependencyGraph
                            tasks={allProjectTasks}
                            selectedTaskId={task.id}
                            onTaskClick={(clickedTask) => {
                              // Could navigate to clicked task
                              onClose();
                              // Optionally open the clicked task's modal
                            }}
                            onClose={() => setShowDependencyGraph(false)}
                          />
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </motion.div>
                )}
              </AnimatePresence>

              {/* Comments Tab */}
              {activeTab === 'comments' && (
                <div className='space-y-4'>
                  {/* Comment Input */}
                  <div className='relative'>
                    <div className='flex items-start gap-3'>
                      <div className='w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-gradient-to-br from-primary to-cyan-400 flex items-center justify-center text-xs font-medium text-primary-foreground flex-shrink-0'>
                        {currentUser?.name?.charAt(0) || '?'}
                      </div>
                      <div className='flex-1 relative'>
                        <Textarea
                          ref={commentInputRef}
                          value={commentText}
                          onChange={handleCommentChange}
                          placeholder='Add a comment... Use @ to mention someone'
                          rows={3}
                          className='resize-none pr-10'
                          onKeyDown={(e) => {
                            if (e.key === 'Enter' && (e.metaKey || e.ctrlKey)) {
                              e.preventDefault();
                              handleSubmitComment();
                            }
                          }}
                        />
                        <Button
                          size='icon'
                          className='absolute right-2 bottom-2 h-7 w-7'
                          onClick={handleSubmitComment}
                          disabled={!commentText.trim()}
                        >
                          <Send className='w-3 h-3' />
                        </Button>

                        {/* Mentions Dropdown */}
                        <AnimatePresence>
                          {showMentions && filteredMembers.length > 0 && (
                            <motion.div
                              initial={{ opacity: 0, y: -10 }}
                              animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                              exit={{ opacity: 0, y: -10 }}
                              className='absolute left-0 right-0 top-full mt-1 bg-card border border-border rounded-lg shadow-lg z-10 max-h-40 overflow-y-auto'
                            >
                              <div className='p-1'>
                                <div className='px-2 py-1 text-xs text-muted-foreground flex items-center gap-1'>
                                  <AtSign className='w-3 h-3' />
                                  Mention someone
                                </div>
                                {filteredMembers.map((member) => (
                                  <button
                                    key={member.userId}
                                    onClick={() => insertMention(member)}
                                    className='w-full flex items-center gap-2 px-2 py-2 hover:bg-secondary rounded-md transition-colors'
                                  >
                                    <div className='w-6 h-6 rounded-full bg-gradient-to-br from-primary to-cyan-400 flex items-center justify-center text-[10px] font-medium text-primary-foreground'>
                                      {member.user.name.charAt(0)}
                                    </div>
                                    <div className='text-left'>
                                      <p className='text-sm font-medium text-foreground'>
                                        {member.user.name}
                                      </p>
                                      <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                                        {member.user.email}
                                      </p>
                                    </div>
                                  </button>
                                ))}
                              </div>
                            </motion.div>
                          )}
                        </AnimatePresence>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-2 ml-11'>
                      Press ⌘+Enter to submit
                    </p>
                  </div>

                  {/* Comments List */}
                  <div className='space-y-4 pt-4 border-t border-border'>
                    {!task.comments || task.comments.length === 0 ? (
                      <div className='text-center py-8'>
                        <MessageSquare className='w-8 h-8 text-muted-foreground mx-auto mb-2' />
                        <p className='text-muted-foreground text-sm'>
                          No comments yet
                        </p>
                        <p className='text-muted-foreground text-xs'>
                          Be the first to comment!
                        </p>
                      </div>
                    ) : (
                      task.comments.map((comment) => (
                        <motion.div
                          key={comment.id}
                          initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
                          animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                          className='flex gap-3'
                        >
                          <div className='w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-gradient-to-br from-primary to-cyan-400 flex items-center justify-center text-xs font-medium text-primary-foreground flex-shrink-0'>
                            {comment.user?.name?.charAt(0) || '?'}
                          </div>
                          <div className='flex-1'>
                            <div className='flex items-center gap-2 mb-1'>
                              <span className='font-medium text-sm text-foreground'>
                                {comment.user?.name}
                              </span>
                              <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                                {formatDistanceToNow(
                                  parseISO(comment.createdAt),
                                  { addSuffix: true },
                                )}
                              </span>
                            </div>
                            <p className='text-sm text-foreground/90 whitespace-pre-wrap'>
                              {renderCommentContent(comment.content, members)}
                            </p>
                            {comment.mentions &&
                              comment.mentions.length > 0 && (
                                <div className='flex items-center gap-1 mt-2'>
                                  <AtSign className='w-3 h-3 text-muted-foreground' />
                                  <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                                    Mentioned {comment.mentions.length}{' '}
                                    {comment.mentions.length === 1
                                      ? 'person'
                                      : 'people'}
                                  </span>
                                </div>
                              )}
                          </div>
                        </motion.div>
                      ))
                    )}
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}

              {/* Subtasks Tab */}
              {activeTab === 'subtasks' && (
                <div className='space-y-4'>
                  {/* Add Subtask */}
                  <div className='flex gap-2'>
                    <Input
                      value={newSubtask}
                      onChange={(e) => setNewSubtask(e.target.value)}
                      placeholder='Add a subtask...'
                      onKeyDown={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && handleAddSubtask()}
                    />
                    <Button onClick={handleAddSubtask} size='icon'>
                      <Plus className='w-4 h-4' />
                    </Button>
                  </div>

                  {/* Subtask List */}
                  <div className='space-y-2'>
                    {task.subtasks?.length === 0 ? (
                      <p className='text-muted-foreground text-sm text-center py-8'>
                        No subtasks yet
                      </p>
                    ) : (
                      task.subtasks?.map((subtask) => (
                        <div
                          key={subtask.id}
                          className='flex items-center gap-3 p-3 bg-secondary/30 rounded-lg group'
                        >
                          <button
                            onClick={() => handleToggleSubtask(subtask.id)}
                            className={cn(
                              'w-5 h-5 rounded border-2 flex items-center justify-center transition-colors',
                              subtask.completed
                                ? 'bg-success border-success text-success-foreground'
                                : 'border-muted-foreground hover:border-primary',
                            )}
                          >
                            {subtask.completed && (
                              <CheckCircle2 className='w-3 h-3' />
                            )}
                          </button>
                          <span
                            className={cn(
                              'flex-1 text-sm',
                              subtask.completed &&
                                'line-through text-muted-foreground',
                            )}
                          >
                            {subtask.title}
                          </span>
                        </div>
                      ))
                    )}
                  </div>

                  {/* Progress */}
                  {totalSubtasks > 0 && (
                    <div className='pt-4 border-t border-border'>
                      <div className='flex items-center justify-between text-sm mb-2'>
                        <span className='text-muted-foreground'>Progress</span>
                        <span className='font-medium text-foreground'>
                          {completedSubtasks}/{totalSubtasks} completed
                        </span>
                      </div>
                      <div className='h-2 bg-secondary rounded-full overflow-hidden'>
                        <div
                          className='h-full bg-success transition-all duration-300'
                          style={{
                            width: `${(completedSubtasks / totalSubtasks) * 100}%`,
                          }}
                        />
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>
              )}

              {/* Activity Tab */}
              {activeTab === 'activity' && (
                <div className='space-y-4'>
                  {task.activities?.length === 0 ? (
                    <p className='text-muted-foreground text-sm text-center py-8'>
                      No activity yet
                    </p>
                  ) : (
                    <div className='space-y-4'>
                      {task.activities?.map((activity) => (
                        <div key={activity.id} className='flex gap-3'>
                          <div className='w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-gradient-to-br from-primary to-cyan-400 flex items-center justify-center text-xs font-medium text-primary-foreground flex-shrink-0'>
                            {activity.user?.name?.charAt(0) || '?'}
                          </div>
                          <div>
                            <p className='text-sm text-foreground'>
                              <span className='font-medium'>
                                {activity.user?.name}
                              </span>{' '}
                              {activity.type === 'created' &&
                                'created this task'}
                              {activity.type === 'status_change' && (
                                <>
                                  changed status from{' '}
                                  <span className='font-medium'>
                                    {activity.previousValue}
                                  </span>{' '}
                                  to{' '}
                                  <span className='font-medium'>
                                    {activity.newValue}
                                  </span>
                                </>
                              )}
                              {activity.type === 'priority_change' && (
                                <>
                                  changed priority to{' '}
                                  <span className='font-medium'>
                                    {activity.newValue}
                                  </span>
                                </>
                              )}
                              {activity.type === 'assignee_change' && (
                                <>
                                  assigned to{' '}
                                  <span className='font-medium'>
                                    {activity.newValue}
                                  </span>
                                </>
                              )}
                            </p>
                            <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                              {format(
                                parseISO(activity.createdAt),
                                'MMM d, yyyy h:mm a',
                              )}
                            </p>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      ))}
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </motion.div>
        </>
      )}
    </AnimatePresence>
  );
}

import { useState, useMemo } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import {
  DndContext,
  DragOverlay,
  closestCenter,
  KeyboardSensor,
  PointerSensor,
  useSensor,
  useSensors,
  type DragStartEvent,
  type DragEndEvent,
  type DragOverEvent,
  useDroppable,
} from '@dnd-kit/core';
import {
  SortableContext,
  sortableKeyboardCoordinates,
  verticalListSortingStrategy,
  useSortable,
} from '@dnd-kit/sortable';
import { CSS } from '@dnd-kit/utilities';
import { Calendar, GripVertical } from 'lucide-react';
import { useWorkspaceStore, type Task } from '@/store/workspaceStore';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { format, isValid, parseISO, isBefore } from 'date-fns';

interface KanbanBoardProps {
  projectId: string;
  onTaskClick?: (task: Task) => void;
}

const statusColors: Record<string, string> = {
  TODO: 'border-t-muted-foreground',
  IN_PROGRESS: 'border-t-warning',
  REVIEW: 'border-t-primary',
  DONE: 'border-t-success',
};

const priorityDots: Record<string, string> = {
  LOW: 'bg-muted-foreground',
  MEDIUM: 'bg-warning',
  HIGH: 'bg-destructive',
  URGENT: 'bg-destructive animate-pulse',
};

// Helper to safely parse dates
const safeParseDate = (dateString: string | undefined | null): Date | null => {
  if (!dateString) return null;
  const date = parseISO(dateString);
  return isValid(date) ? date : null;
};

function TaskCard({
  task,
  onTaskClick,
}: {
  task: Task;
  onTaskClick?: (task: Task) => void;
}) {
  const {
    attributes,
    listeners,
    setNodeRef,
    transform,
    transition,
    isDragging,
  } = useSortable({ id: task.id });

  const style = {
    transform: CSS.Transform.toString(transform),
    transition,
  };

  const dueDate = safeParseDate(task.due_date);
  const isOverdue =
    dueDate && isBefore(dueDate, new Date()) && task.status !== 'DONE';

  return (
    <div
      ref={setNodeRef}
      style={style}
      className={cn(
        'glass-card p-3 cursor-pointer group transition-all touch-none',
        isDragging && 'opacity-50 scale-105 shadow-xl z-50',
      )}
      onClick={() => !isDragging && onTaskClick?.(task)}
    >
      <div className='flex items-start gap-2'>
        <div
          {...attributes}
          {...listeners}
          className='p-1 opacity-50 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity cursor-grab active:cursor-grabbing touch-none'
        >
          <GripVertical className='w-3 h-3 text-muted-foreground' />
        </div>
        <div className='flex-1 min-w-0'>
          <div className='flex items-center gap-2 mb-1'>
            <span
              className={cn(
                'w-2 h-2 rounded-full flex-shrink-0',
                priorityDots[task.priority],
              )}
            />
            <span className='text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded bg-secondary text-muted-foreground'>
              {task.type}
            </span>
          </div>
          <h4 className='font-medium text-sm text-foreground line-clamp-2'>
            {task.title}
          </h4>
          <div className='flex items-center justify-between mt-2'>
            {dueDate ? (
              <span
                className={cn(
                  'text-[10px] flex items-center gap-1',
                  isOverdue ? 'text-destructive' : 'text-muted-foreground',
                )}
              >
                <Calendar className='w-3 h-3' />
                {format(dueDate, 'MMM d')}
              </span>
            ) : (
              <span className='text-[10px] text-muted-foreground'>
                No due date
              </span>
            )}
            <div
              className='w-6 h-6 rounded-full bg-gradient-to-br from-primary to-cyan-400 flex items-center justify-center text-[10px] font-medium text-primary-foreground'
              title={task.assignee?.name}
            >
              {task.assignee?.name?.charAt(0) || '?'}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function DroppableColumn({
  status,
  title,
  tasks,
  onTaskClick,
  isOver,
}: {
  status: Task['status'];
  title: string;
  tasks: Task[];
  onTaskClick?: (task: Task) => void;
  isOver: boolean;
}) {
  const { setNodeRef } = useDroppable({
    id: `column-${status}`,
    data: { status },
  });

  return (
    <div
      ref={setNodeRef}
      className={cn(
        'flex-1 min-w-[280px] max-w-[320px] bg-secondary/30 rounded-xl border-t-2 transition-all',
        statusColors[status],
        isOver && 'ring-2 ring-primary ring-offset-2 ring-offset-background',
      )}
    >
      <div className='p-3 border-b border-border'>
        <div className='flex items-center justify-between'>
          <h3 className='font-medium text-foreground'>{title}</h3>
          <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground bg-secondary px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full'>
            {tasks.length}
          </span>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div className='p-2 space-y-2 min-h-[200px] max-h-[calc(100vh-400px)] overflow-y-auto'>
        <SortableContext
          items={tasks.map((t) => t.id)}
          strategy={verticalListSortingStrategy}
        >
          <AnimatePresence mode='popLayout'>
            {tasks.length === 0 ? (
              <motion.div
                initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
                animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
                className={cn(
                  'flex items-center justify-center h-24 border-2 border-dashed rounded-lg transition-colors',
                  isOver ? 'border-primary bg-primary/10' : 'border-border',
                )}
              >
                <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                  {isOver ? 'Drop here' : 'No tasks'}
                </span>
              </motion.div>
            ) : (
              tasks.map((task) => (
                <motion.div
                  key={task.id}
                  layout
                  initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
                  animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                  exit={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.9 }}
                  transition={{ duration: 0.2 }}
                >
                  <TaskCard task={task} onTaskClick={onTaskClick} />
                </motion.div>
              ))
            )}
          </AnimatePresence>
        </SortableContext>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export default function KanbanBoard({
  projectId,
  onTaskClick,
}: KanbanBoardProps) {
  const { currentWorkspace, updateTaskStatus } = useWorkspaceStore();
  const project = currentWorkspace?.projects.find((p) => p.id === projectId);
  const tasks = project?.tasks || [];

  const [activeTask, setActiveTask] = useState<Task | null>(null);
  const [overColumnId, setOverColumnId] = useState<string | null>(null);

  const sensors = useSensors(
    useSensor(PointerSensor, {
      activationConstraint: {
        distance: 8,
      },
    }),
    useSensor(KeyboardSensor, {
      coordinateGetter: sortableKeyboardCoordinates,
    }),
  );

  const columns: { status: Task['status']; title: string }[] = [
    { status: 'TODO', title: 'To Do' },
    { status: 'IN_PROGRESS', title: 'In Progress' },
    { status: 'REVIEW', title: 'Review' },
    { status: 'DONE', title: 'Done' },
  ];

  const tasksByStatus = useMemo(() => {
    return columns.reduce(
      (acc, col) => {
        acc[col.status] = tasks
          .filter((t) => t.status === col.status)
          .sort((a, b) => (a.order || 0) - (b.order || 0));
        return acc;
      },
      {} as Record<string, Task[]>,
    );
  }, [tasks]);

  const handleDragStart = (event: DragStartEvent) => {
    const task = tasks.find((t) => t.id === event.active.id);
    setActiveTask(task || null);
  };

  const handleDragOver = (event: DragOverEvent) => {
    const { over } = event;
    if (!over) {
      setOverColumnId(null);
      return;
    }

    // Check if hovering over a column
    if (String(over.id).startsWith('column-')) {
      setOverColumnId(String(over.id));
      return;
    }

    // Check if hovering over a task - find its column
    const overTask = tasks.find((t) => t.id === over.id);
    if (overTask) {
      setOverColumnId(`column-${overTask.status}`);
    }
  };

  const handleDragEnd = (event: DragEndEvent) => {
    const { active, over } = event;
    setActiveTask(null);
    setOverColumnId(null);

    if (!over) return;

    const activeTaskData = tasks.find((t) => t.id === active.id);
    if (!activeTaskData) return;

    let newStatus: Task['status'] | null = null;

    // Dropped on a column
    if (String(over.id).startsWith('column-')) {
      const columnStatus = String(over.id).replace(
        'column-',
        '',
      ) as Task['status'];
      newStatus = columnStatus;
    } else {
      // Dropped on a task - use that task's status
      const overTask = tasks.find((t) => t.id === over.id);
      if (overTask) {
        newStatus = overTask.status;
      }
    }

    if (newStatus && activeTaskData.status !== newStatus) {
      updateTaskStatus(activeTaskData.id, projectId, newStatus);
    }
  };

  const handleDragCancel = () => {
    setActiveTask(null);
    setOverColumnId(null);
  };

  return (
    <DndContext
      sensors={sensors}
      collisionDetection={closestCenter}
      onDragStart={handleDragStart}
      onDragOver={handleDragOver}
      onDragEnd={handleDragEnd}
      onDragCancel={handleDragCancel}
    >
      <div className='flex gap-4 overflow-x-auto pb-4'>
        {columns.map((col) => (
          <DroppableColumn
            key={col.status}
            status={col.status}
            title={col.title}
            tasks={tasksByStatus[col.status] || []}
            onTaskClick={onTaskClick}
            isOver={overColumnId === `column-${col.status}`}
          />
        ))}
      </div>
      <DragOverlay>
        {activeTask && (
          <div className='glass-card p-3 shadow-2xl rotate-2 scale-105 w-[280px]'>
            <div className='flex items-center gap-2 mb-1'>
              <span
                className={cn(
                  'w-2 h-2 rounded-full',
                  priorityDots[activeTask.priority],
                )}
              />
              <span className='text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded bg-secondary text-muted-foreground'>
                {activeTask.type}
              </span>
            </div>
            <h4 className='font-medium text-sm text-foreground'>
              {activeTask.title}
            </h4>
          </div>
        )}
      </DragOverlay>
    </DndContext>
  );
}

                ⌘K

              size='icon'
              className='sm:hidden bg-primary hover:bg-primary/90 text-primary-foreground'
            >
              <Plus className='w-4 h-4' />
            </Button>

                >

                      {currentUser?.name || 'User'}
                    </p>
                    <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                      {currentWorkspace?.name}
                    </p>
                  </div>
                  <div className='w-9 h-9 rounded-full bg-gradient-to-br from-primary to-cyan-400 flex items-center justify-center text-primary-foreground font-medium'>
                    {currentUser?.name?.charAt(0) || 'U'}
                  </div>
                  <ChevronDown className='w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground hidden sm:block' />
                </motion.button>
              </DropdownMenuTrigger>
              <DropdownMenuContent align='end' className='w-56'>
                <DropdownMenuLabel className='font-normal'>
                  <div className='flex flex-col space-y-1'>
                    <p className='text-sm font-medium'>
                      {currentUser?.name || 'User'}

                      {currentUser?.email || 'user@example.com'}
                    </p>
                  </div>
                </DropdownMenuLabel>
                <DropdownMenuSeparator />

                  onClick={() => setShowSettings(true)}
                  className='cursor-pointer'
                >
                  <User className='mr-2 h-4 w-4' />
                  Profile
                </DropdownMenuItem>
                <DropdownMenuItem
                  onClick={() => setShowSettings(true)}
                  className='cursor-pointer'
                >
                  <Settings className='mr-2 h-4 w-4' />
                  Settings
                </DropdownMenuItem>
                <DropdownMenuItem
                  onClick={toggleTheme}
                  className='cursor-pointer'
                >
                  {theme === 'dark' ? (
                    <>
                      <Sun className='mr-2 h-4 w-4' />
                      Light Mode
                    </>
                  ) : (
                    <>
                      <Moon className='mr-2 h-4 w-4' />
                      Dark Mode
                    </>
                  )}
                </DropdownMenuItem>
                <DropdownMenuSeparator />
                <DropdownMenuItem
                  onClick={handleLogout}
                  className='cursor-pointer text-destructive focus:text-destructive'
                >
                  <LogOut className='mr-2 h-4 w-4' />
                  Log out
                </DropdownMenuItem>
              </DropdownMenuContent>
            </DropdownMenu>
          </div>
        </div>
      </header>

      <CreateProjectDialog
        open={showCreateProject}
        onOpenChange={setShowCreateProject}
      />

      <SettingsModal open={showSettings} onOpenChange={setShowSettings} />
    </>
  );
}

  return (

        className={cn(
          'flex-1 flex flex-col min-h-screen transition-all duration-300',
          sidebarOpen ? 'lg:ml-0' : 'lg:ml-0',

          <div className='max-w-7xl mx-auto'>
            <Outlet />
          </div>
        </main>

      {/* Global Command Palette */}

  );

import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import {
  LayoutDashboard,
  FolderKanban,
  Users,
  ChevronLeft,
  ChevronDown,
  Building2,
  Moon,
  Sun,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { NavLink, useLocation } from 'react-router-dom';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { useWorkspaceStore } from '@/store/workspaceStore';
import { useState } from 'react';
import { useTheme } from 'next-themes';

const navItems = [
  { icon: LayoutDashboard, label: 'Dashboard', path: '/' },
  { icon: FolderKanban, label: 'Projects', path: '/projects' },
  { icon: Users, label: 'Team', path: '/team' },
];

export default function Sidebar() {

  const {
    sidebarOpen,
    toggleSidebar,
    currentWorkspace,
    workspaces,
    setCurrentWorkspace,
  } = useWorkspaceStore();

  const [workspaceDropdownOpen, setWorkspaceDropdownOpen] = useState(false);

  return (
