            initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
            className='fixed inset-0 bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-sm z-40 lg:hidden'
            onClick={toggleSidebar}
          />
        )}
      </AnimatePresence>

      {/* Sidebar */}
      <motion.aside
        initial={false}
        animate={{
          width: sidebarOpen ? 280 : 72,
          x: 0,
        }}
        className={cn(
          'fixed lg:relative z-50 h-screen flex flex-col',
          'bg-sidebar border-r border-sidebar-border',
          'transition-all duration-300 ease-out',
          !sidebarOpen && 'max-lg:translate-x-[-100%]',
        )}
      >
        {/* Header */}
        <div className='flex items-center justify-between p-4 border-b border-sidebar-border'>
          <AnimatePresence mode='wait'>
            {sidebarOpen && (
              <motion.div
                initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
                animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
                exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
                className='flex items-center gap-3'
              >
                <div className='w-8 h-8 rounded-lg bg-gradient-to-br from-primary to-cyan-400 flex items-center justify-center'>
                  <Building2 className='w-4 h-4 text-primary-foreground' />
                </div>
                <span className='font-semibold text-foreground'>Workspace</span>
              </motion.div>
            )}
          </AnimatePresence>

          <button
            onClick={toggleSidebar}
            className='p-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-sidebar-accent text-sidebar-foreground transition-colors'
          >
            <ChevronLeft
              className={cn(
                'w-4 h-4 transition-transform duration-300',
                !sidebarOpen && 'rotate-180',
              )}
            />
          </button>
        </div>

        {/* Workspace Selector */}
        <div className='p-3'>
          <div className='relative'>
            <button
              onClick={() =>
                sidebarOpen && setWorkspaceDropdownOpen(!workspaceDropdownOpen)
              }
              className={cn(
                'w-full flex items-center gap-3 p-3 rounded-xl',
                'bg-sidebar-accent/50 hover:bg-sidebar-accent transition-colors',
                'text-left',
              )}
            >
              <div className='w-8 h-8 rounded-lg bg-gradient-to-br from-primary/20 to-cyan-400/20 border border-primary/30 flex items-center justify-center flex-shrink-0'>
                <span className='text-sm font-medium text-primary'>
                  {currentWorkspace?.name.charAt(0) || 'W'}
                </span>
              </div>
              {sidebarOpen && (
                <>
                  <div className='flex-1 min-w-0'>
                    <p className='text-sm font-medium text-foreground truncate'>
                      {currentWorkspace?.name || 'Select Workspace'}
                    </p>
                    <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate'>
                      {currentWorkspace?.projects.length || 0} projects
                    </p>
                  </div>
                  <ChevronDown
                    className={cn(
                      'w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground transition-transform',
                      workspaceDropdownOpen && 'rotate-180',
                    )}
                  />
                </>
              )}
            </button>

            {/* Workspace Dropdown */}
            <AnimatePresence>
              {workspaceDropdownOpen && sidebarOpen && (
                <motion.div
                  initial={{ opacity: 0, y: -10 }}
                  animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                  exit={{ opacity: 0, y: -10 }}
                  className='absolute top-full left-0 right-0 mt-2 p-2 rounded-xl bg-popover border border-border shadow-lg z-50'
                >
                  {workspaces.map((workspace) => (
                    <button
                      key={workspace.id}
                      onClick={() => {
                        setCurrentWorkspace(workspace.id);
                        setWorkspaceDropdownOpen(false);
                      }}
                      className={cn(
                        'w-full flex items-center gap-3 p-2 rounded-lg transition-colors',
                        workspace.id === currentWorkspace?.id
                          ? 'bg-primary/10 text-primary'
                          : 'hover:bg-accent text-foreground',
                      )}
                    >
                      <div className='w-6 h-6 rounded bg-primary/20 flex items-center justify-center text-xs font-medium'>
                        {workspace.name.charAt(0)}
                      </div>
                      <span className='text-sm truncate'>{workspace.name}</span>
                    </button>
                  ))}
                </motion.div>
              )}
            </AnimatePresence>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Navigation */}
        <nav className='flex-1 p-3 space-y-1'>
          {navItems.map((item) => {
            const isActive = location.pathname === item.path;

            return (
              <NavLink
                key={item.path}
                to={item.path}
                className={cn(
                  'flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2.5 rounded-xl transition-all duration-200',
                  isActive
                    ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground shadow-md shadow-primary/20'
                    : 'text-sidebar-foreground hover:bg-sidebar-accent',
                )}
              >
                <item.icon className='w-5 h-5 flex-shrink-0' />
                <AnimatePresence mode='wait'>
                  {sidebarOpen && (
                    <motion.span
                      initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
                      animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
                      exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
                      className='text-sm font-medium'
                    >
                      {item.label}
                    </motion.span>
                  )}
                </AnimatePresence>
              </NavLink>
            );
          })}
        </nav>

        {/* Footer */}
        <div className='p-3 border-t border-sidebar-border space-y-2'>
          {/* Theme Toggle */}
          <button
            onClick={() => setTheme(theme === 'dark' ? 'light' : 'dark')}
            className={cn(
              'w-full flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2.5 rounded-xl transition-colors',
              'text-sidebar-foreground hover:bg-sidebar-accent',
            )}
          >
            {theme === 'dark' ? (
              <Sun className='w-5 h-5 flex-shrink-0' />
            ) : (
              <Moon className='w-5 h-5 flex-shrink-0' />
            )}
            {sidebarOpen && (
              <span className='text-sm font-medium'>
                {theme === 'dark' ? 'Light Mode' : 'Dark Mode'}
              </span>
            )}
          </button>
        </div>
      </motion.aside>
    </>
  );
}

import { NavLink as RouterNavLink, NavLinkProps } from 'react-router-dom';
import { forwardRef } from 'react';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';

interface NavLinkCompatProps extends Omit<NavLinkProps, 'className'> {
  className?: string;
  activeClassName?: string;
  pendingClassName?: string;
}

const NavLink = forwardRef<HTMLAnchorElement, NavLinkCompatProps>(
  ({ className, activeClassName, pendingClassName, to, ...props }, ref) => {
    return (
      <RouterNavLink
        ref={ref}
        to={to}
        className={({ isActive, isPending }) =>
          cn(
            className,
            isActive && activeClassName,
            isPending && pendingClassName,
          )
        }
        {...props}
      />
    );
  },
);

NavLink.displayName = 'NavLink';

export { NavLink };

import { useState } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import {
  Bell,
  Check,
  CheckCheck,
  Trash2,
  MessageSquare,
  UserPlus,
  GitBranch,
  Clock,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { useWorkspaceStore, type Notification } from '@/store/workspaceStore';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { formatDistanceToNow } from 'date-fns';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';

const notificationIcons: Record<Notification['type'], typeof Bell> = {
  task_assigned: UserPlus,
  comment_mention: MessageSquare,
  status_change: GitBranch,
  project_invite: UserPlus,
  due_reminder: Clock,
};

export default function NotificationPanel() {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const {
    notifications,
    markNotificationRead,
    markAllNotificationsRead,
    clearNotifications,
  } = useWorkspaceStore();
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false);

  const unreadCount = notifications.filter((n) => !n.read).length;

  const handleNotificationClick = (notification: Notification) => {
    markNotificationRead(notification.id);
    if (notification.link) {
      navigate(notification.link);
      setIsOpen(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className='relative'>
      <button
        onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)}
        className='relative p-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-accent transition-colors'
      >
        <Bell className='w-5 h-5 text-muted-foreground' />
        {unreadCount > 0 && (
          <span className='absolute -top-0.5 -right-0.5 w-5 h-5 rounded-full bg-primary text-primary-foreground text-[10px] font-bold flex items-center justify-center animate-pulse'>
            {unreadCount > 9 ? '9+' : unreadCount}
          </span>
        )}
      </button>

      <AnimatePresence>
        {isOpen && (
          <>
            <motion.div
              initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
              animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
              exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
              className='fixed inset-0 z-40'
              onClick={() => setIsOpen(false)}
            />
            <motion.div
              initial={{ opacity: 0, y: -10, scale: 0.95 }}
              animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0, scale: 1 }}
              exit={{ opacity: 0, y: -10, scale: 0.95 }}
              className='absolute right-0 top-full mt-2 w-80 sm:w-96 glass-card overflow-hidden z-50'
            >
              {/* Header */}
              <div className='p-4 border-b border-border flex items-center justify-between'>
                <h3 className='font-semibold text-foreground'>Notifications</h3>
                <div className='flex items-center gap-2'>
                  {unreadCount > 0 && (
                    <button
                      onClick={markAllNotificationsRead}
                      className='p-1.5 rounded hover:bg-accent transition-colors'
                      title='Mark all as read'
                    >
                      <CheckCheck className='w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground' />
                    </button>
                  )}
                  <button
                    onClick={clearNotifications}
                    className='p-1.5 rounded hover:bg-accent transition-colors'
                    title='Clear all'
                  >
                    <Trash2 className='w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground' />
                  </button>
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* Notifications List */}
              <div className='max-h-[400px] overflow-y-auto'>
                {notifications.length === 0 ? (
                  <div className='p-8 text-center'>
                    <Bell className='w-10 h-10 text-muted-foreground mx-auto mb-3' />
                    <p className='text-muted-foreground'>
                      No notifications yet
                    </p>
                  </div>
                ) : (
                  notifications.map((notification) => {
                    const Icon = notificationIcons[notification.type];
                    return (
                      <motion.div
                        key={notification.id}
                        initial={{ opacity: 0, x: -20 }}
                        animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
                        className={cn(
                          'p-4 border-b border-border cursor-pointer hover:bg-accent/50 transition-colors',
                          !notification.read && 'bg-primary/5',
                        )}
                        onClick={() => handleNotificationClick(notification)}
                      >
                        <div className='flex gap-3'>
                          <div
                            className={cn(
                              'w-8 h-8 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center flex-shrink-0',
                              notification.read
                                ? 'bg-secondary'
                                : 'bg-primary/20',
                            )}
                          >
                            <Icon
                              className={cn(
                                'w-4 h-4',
                                notification.read
                                  ? 'text-muted-foreground'
                                  : 'text-primary',
                              )}
                            />
                          </div>
                          <div className='flex-1 min-w-0'>
                            <p
                              className={cn(
                                'text-sm',
                                notification.read
                                  ? 'text-muted-foreground'
                                  : 'text-foreground font-medium',
                              )}
                            >
                              {notification.title}
                            </p>
                            <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-0.5 line-clamp-2'>
                              {notification.message}
                            </p>
                            <p className='text-[10px] text-muted-foreground mt-1'>
                              {formatDistanceToNow(
                                new Date(notification.createdAt),
                                { addSuffix: true },
                              )}
                            </p>
                          </div>
                          {!notification.read && (
                            <div className='w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-primary flex-shrink-0 mt-2' />
                          )}
                        </div>
                      </motion.div>
                    );
                  })
                )}
              </div>
            </motion.div>
          </>
        )}
      </AnimatePresence>
    </div>
  );
}

==============================

import * as React from "react"

const MOBILE_BREAKPOINT = 768

export function useIsMobile() {
  const [isMobile, setIsMobile] = React.useState<boolean | undefined>(undefined)

  React.useEffect(() => {
    const mql = window.matchMedia(`(max-width: ${MOBILE_BREAKPOINT - 1}px)`)
    const onChange = () => {
      setIsMobile(window.innerWidth < MOBILE_BREAKPOINT)
    }
    mql.addEventListener("change", onChange)
    setIsMobile(window.innerWidth < MOBILE_BREAKPOINT)
    return () => mql.removeEventListener("change", onChange)
  }, [])

  return !!isMobile
}

FILE: E:\My Projects\Project-Management\sprintly-frontend\src\hooks\useKeyboardShortcuts.ts
==============================

/**
 * Keyboard shortcuts hook for calendar navigation and task management
 */

import { useEffect, useCallback, useState } from 'react';

export interface KeyboardShortcut {
  key: string;
  description: string;
  category: string;
  modifiers?: {
    ctrl?: boolean;
    meta?: boolean;
    shift?: boolean;
    alt?: boolean;
  };
}

// Define all available shortcuts
export const KEYBOARD_SHORTCUTS: KeyboardShortcut[] = [
  // Task actions
  { key: 'n', description: 'Create new task', category: 'Tasks' },
  { key: 'e', description: 'Edit selected task', category: 'Tasks' },
  { key: 'Delete', description: 'Delete selected task', category: 'Tasks' },
  { key: 'Backspace', description: 'Delete selected task', category: 'Tasks' },
  { key: 'Escape', description: 'Deselect / Close modal', category: 'Tasks' },

  // View switching
  { key: '1', description: 'Switch to Month view', category: 'Views' },
  { key: '2', description: 'Switch to Week view', category: 'Views' },
  { key: '3', description: 'Switch to Day view', category: 'Views' },
  { key: '4', description: 'Switch to Gantt view', category: 'Views' },

  // Navigation
  { key: 'ArrowLeft', description: 'Previous period', category: 'Navigation' },
  { key: 'ArrowRight', description: 'Next period', category: 'Navigation' },
  { key: 'ArrowUp', description: 'Previous task', category: 'Navigation' },
  { key: 'ArrowDown', description: 'Next task', category: 'Navigation' },
  { key: 't', description: 'Go to today', category: 'Navigation' },

  // Filters & Search
  {
    key: 'f',
    description: 'Focus filters',
    category: 'Filters',
    modifiers: { ctrl: true },
  },
  {
    key: 'f',
    description: 'Focus filters (Mac)',
    category: 'Filters',
    modifiers: { meta: true },
  },

  // Help
  { key: '?', description: 'Show keyboard shortcuts', category: 'Help' },
];

export type ViewMode = 'month' | 'week' | 'day' | 'gantt';

export interface UseKeyboardShortcutsOptions {
  onCreateTask?: () => void;
  onEditTask?: () => void;
  onDeleteTask?: () => void;
  onNavigatePrev?: () => void;
  onNavigateNext?: () => void;
  onGoToToday?: () => void;
  onViewChange?: (view: ViewMode) => void;
  onFocusFilters?: () => void;
  onShowHelp?: () => void;
  onEscape?: () => void;
  onNavigateTaskUp?: () => void;
  onNavigateTaskDown?: () => void;
  enabled?: boolean;
}

export function useKeyboardShortcuts(options: UseKeyboardShortcutsOptions) {
  const {
    onCreateTask,
    onEditTask,
    onDeleteTask,
    onNavigatePrev,
    onNavigateNext,
    onGoToToday,
    onViewChange,
    onFocusFilters,
    onShowHelp,
    onEscape,
    onNavigateTaskUp,
    onNavigateTaskDown,
    enabled = true,
  } = options;

  const [showHelpModal, setShowHelpModal] = useState(false);

  const handleKeyDown = useCallback(
    (event: KeyboardEvent) => {
      if (!enabled) return;

      // Ignore if user is typing in an input
      const target = event.target as HTMLElement;
      const isInputField =
        target.tagName === 'INPUT' ||
        target.tagName === 'TEXTAREA' ||
        target.tagName === 'SELECT' ||
        target.isContentEditable;

      // Allow Escape even in input fields
      if (event.key === 'Escape') {
        if (showHelpModal) {
          setShowHelpModal(false);
          event.preventDefault();
          return;
        }
        onEscape?.();
        return;
      }

      // Skip other shortcuts if in input field
      if (isInputField) return;

      const isCtrl = event.ctrlKey;
      const isMeta = event.metaKey;
      const isShift = event.shiftKey;

      // Handle Ctrl/Cmd + F for filters
      if ((isCtrl || isMeta) && event.key.toLowerCase() === 'f') {
        event.preventDefault();
        onFocusFilters?.();
        return;
      }

      // Skip if any modifier is pressed (except for specific shortcuts)
      if (isCtrl || isMeta || isShift) return;

      switch (event.key) {
        case 'n':
        case 'N':
          event.preventDefault();
          onCreateTask?.();
          break;

        case 'e':
        case 'E':
          event.preventDefault();
          onEditTask?.();
          break;

        case 'Delete':
        case 'Backspace':
          event.preventDefault();
          onDeleteTask?.();
          break;

        case '1':
          event.preventDefault();
          onViewChange?.('month');
          break;

        case '2':
          event.preventDefault();
          onViewChange?.('week');
          break;

        case '3':
          event.preventDefault();
          onViewChange?.('day');
          break;

        case '4':
          event.preventDefault();
          onViewChange?.('gantt');
          break;

        case 'ArrowLeft':
          event.preventDefault();
          onNavigatePrev?.();
          break;

        case 'ArrowRight':
          event.preventDefault();
          onNavigateNext?.();
          break;

        case 'ArrowUp':
          event.preventDefault();
          onNavigateTaskUp?.();
          break;

        case 'ArrowDown':
          event.preventDefault();
          onNavigateTaskDown?.();
          break;

        case 't':
        case 'T':
          event.preventDefault();
          onGoToToday?.();
          break;

        case '?':
          event.preventDefault();
          setShowHelpModal(true);
          onShowHelp?.();
          break;
      }
    },
    [
      enabled,
      showHelpModal,
      onCreateTask,
      onEditTask,
      onDeleteTask,
      onNavigatePrev,
      onNavigateNext,
      onGoToToday,
      onViewChange,
      onFocusFilters,
      onShowHelp,
      onEscape,
      onNavigateTaskUp,
      onNavigateTaskDown,
    ],
  );

  useEffect(() => {
    window.addEventListener('keydown', handleKeyDown);
    return () => window.removeEventListener('keydown', handleKeyDown);
  }, [handleKeyDown]);

  return {
    showHelpModal,
    setShowHelpModal,
  };
}

/**
 * Format a shortcut key for display
 */
export function formatShortcutKey(shortcut: KeyboardShortcut): string {
  const parts: string[] = [];

  if (shortcut.modifiers?.ctrl) {
    parts.push('Ctrl');
  }
  if (shortcut.modifiers?.meta) {
    parts.push('⌘');
  }
  if (shortcut.modifiers?.shift) {
    parts.push('Shift');
  }
  if (shortcut.modifiers?.alt) {
    parts.push('Alt');
  }

  // Format special keys
  let keyDisplay = shortcut.key;
  switch (shortcut.key) {
    case 'ArrowLeft':
      keyDisplay = '←';
      break;
    case 'ArrowRight':
      keyDisplay = '→';
      break;
    case 'ArrowUp':
      keyDisplay = '↑';
      break;
    case 'ArrowDown':
      keyDisplay = '↓';
      break;
    case 'Delete':
    case 'Backspace':
      keyDisplay = '⌫';
      break;
    case 'Escape':
      keyDisplay = 'Esc';
      break;
  }

  parts.push(keyDisplay);
  return parts.join(' + ');
}

/**
 * Get shortcuts grouped by category
 */
export function getShortcutsByCategory(): Record<string, KeyboardShortcut[]> {
  const grouped: Record<string, KeyboardShortcut[]> = {};

  KEYBOARD_SHORTCUTS.forEach((shortcut) => {
    if (!grouped[shortcut.category]) {
      grouped[shortcut.category] = [];
    }
    grouped[shortcut.category].push(shortcut);
  });

  return grouped;
}

/**
 * iCal (.ics) export utilities
 * Generates RFC 5545 compliant iCalendar files for task export
 * Compatible with Google Calendar, Outlook, Apple Calendar
 */

import { format, parseISO, isValid } from 'date-fns';
import { type Task } from '@/store/workspaceStore';
import { type RecurrenceRule, type RecurringTaskData } from './recurrence';

// Priority mapping: Task priority -> iCal priority (1-9, 1 being highest)
const PRIORITY_MAP: Record<string, number> = {
  URGENT: 1,
  HIGH: 3,
  MEDIUM: 5,
  LOW: 7,
};

// Status mapping: Task status -> iCal status
const STATUS_MAP: Record<string, string> = {
  TODO: 'NEEDS-ACTION',
  IN_PROGRESS: 'IN-PROCESS',
  REVIEW: 'IN-PROCESS',
  DONE: 'COMPLETED',
};

/**
 * Escape special characters for iCal format
 */
function escapeICalText(text: string): string {
  return text
    .replace(/\\/g, '\\\\')
    .replace(/;/g, '\\;')
    .replace(/,/g, '\\,')
    .replace(/\n/g, '\\n');
}

/**
 * Format a date for iCal (YYYYMMDD format)
 */
function formatICalDate(date: Date): string {
  return format(date, "yyyyMMdd");
}

/**
 * Format a datetime for iCal (YYYYMMDDTHHMMSS format)
 */
function formatICalDateTime(date: Date): string {
  return format(date, "yyyyMMdd'T'HHmmss");
}

/**
 * Generate a unique UID for an iCal event
 */
function generateUID(taskId: string): string {
  return `${taskId}@lovable-calendar`;
}

/**
 * Fold long lines according to RFC 5545 (max 75 chars per line)
 */
function foldLine(line: string): string {
  const maxLength = 75;
  if (line.length <= maxLength) return line;

  const result: string[] = [];
  let remaining = line;

  while (remaining.length > maxLength) {
    result.push(remaining.substring(0, maxLength));
    remaining = ' ' + remaining.substring(maxLength);
  }
  result.push(remaining);

  return result.join('\r\n');
}

/**
 * Convert recurrence rule to RRULE format
 */
function recurrenceToRRule(rule: RecurrenceRule): string | null {
  if (!rule) return null;

  const parts: string[] = [];

  // Frequency
  const freqMap: Record<string, string> = {
    daily: 'DAILY',
    weekly: 'WEEKLY',
    monthly: 'MONTHLY',
    yearly: 'YEARLY',
    custom: 'DAILY',
  };
  parts.push(`FREQ=${freqMap[rule.frequency]}`);

  // Interval
  if (rule.interval > 1) {
    parts.push(`INTERVAL=${rule.interval}`);
  }

  // Days of week (for weekly)
  if (rule.frequency === 'weekly' && rule.daysOfWeek && rule.daysOfWeek.length > 0) {
    const dayMap = ['SU', 'MO', 'TU', 'WE', 'TH', 'FR', 'SA'];
    const days = rule.daysOfWeek.map((d) => dayMap[d]).join(',');
    parts.push(`BYDAY=${days}`);
  }

  // Day of month (for monthly)
  if (rule.frequency === 'monthly' && rule.dayOfMonth) {
    parts.push(`BYMONTHDAY=${rule.dayOfMonth}`);
  }

  // End conditions
  if (rule.endType === 'after' && rule.endAfterOccurrences) {
    parts.push(`COUNT=${rule.endAfterOccurrences}`);
  } else if (rule.endType === 'on_date' && rule.endDate) {
    const endDate = parseISO(rule.endDate);
    if (isValid(endDate)) {
      parts.push(`UNTIL=${formatICalDate(endDate)}`);
    }
  }

  return parts.length > 0 ? `RRULE:${parts.join(';')}` : null;
}

/**
 * Generate a single VTODO component for a task
 */
function generateVTODO(task: Task & { recurring?: RecurringTaskData }): string {
  const lines: string[] = [];
  
  lines.push('BEGIN:VTODO');
  lines.push(`UID:${generateUID(task.id)}`);
  lines.push(`DTSTAMP:${formatICalDateTime(new Date())}`);

  // Summary (title)
  lines.push(`SUMMARY:${escapeICalText(task.title)}`);

  // Description
  if (task.description) {
    lines.push(`DESCRIPTION:${escapeICalText(task.description)}`);
  }

  // Due date
  if (task.due_date) {
    const dueDate = parseISO(task.due_date);
    if (isValid(dueDate)) {
      if (task.due_time) {
        // Has specific time
        const [hours, minutes] = task.due_time.split(':').map(Number);
        dueDate.setHours(hours, minutes, 0, 0);
        lines.push(`DUE:${formatICalDateTime(dueDate)}`);
      } else {
        // All-day task
        lines.push(`DUE;VALUE=DATE:${formatICalDate(dueDate)}`);
      }
    }
  }

  // Created
  if (task.createdAt) {
    const created = parseISO(task.createdAt);
    if (isValid(created)) {
      lines.push(`CREATED:${formatICalDateTime(created)}`);
    }
  }

  // Last modified
  if (task.updatedAt) {
    const modified = parseISO(task.updatedAt);
    if (isValid(modified)) {
      lines.push(`LAST-MODIFIED:${formatICalDateTime(modified)}`);
    }
  }

  // Priority
  if (task.priority) {
    lines.push(`PRIORITY:${PRIORITY_MAP[task.priority] || 5}`);
  }

  // Status
  if (task.status) {
    lines.push(`STATUS:${STATUS_MAP[task.status] || 'NEEDS-ACTION'}`);
  }

  // Categories (type)
  if (task.type) {
    lines.push(`CATEGORIES:${task.type}`);
  }

  // Percent complete (based on status)
  const percentMap: Record<string, number> = {
    TODO: 0,
    IN_PROGRESS: 50,
    REVIEW: 75,
    DONE: 100,
  };
  lines.push(`PERCENT-COMPLETE:${percentMap[task.status] || 0}`);

  // Recurrence rule
  if (task.recurring?.isRecurring && task.recurring.recurrenceRule) {
    const rrule = recurrenceToRRule(task.recurring.recurrenceRule);
    if (rrule) {
      lines.push(rrule);
    }
  }

  // Subtasks as description appendix
  if (task.subtasks && task.subtasks.length > 0) {
    const subtaskList = task.subtasks
      .map((st) => `${st.completed ? '✓' : '○'} ${st.title}`)
      .join('\\n');
    const existingDesc = task.description ? `${escapeICalText(task.description)}\\n\\n` : '';
    lines.push(`DESCRIPTION:${existingDesc}Subtasks:\\n${subtaskList}`);
  }

  lines.push('END:VTODO');

  return lines.map(foldLine).join('\r\n');
}

/**
 * Generate a VEVENT component for calendar display
 * (Some calendar apps better support VEVENT than VTODO)
 */
function generateVEVENT(task: Task & { recurring?: RecurringTaskData }): string {
  const lines: string[] = [];
  
  lines.push('BEGIN:VEVENT');
  lines.push(`UID:${generateUID(task.id)}`);
  lines.push(`DTSTAMP:${formatICalDateTime(new Date())}`);

  // Summary (title)
  const statusPrefix = task.status === 'DONE' ? '✓ ' : '';
  lines.push(`SUMMARY:${escapeICalText(statusPrefix + task.title)}`);

  // Description
  let description = task.description || '';
  if (task.priority) {
    description = `Priority: ${task.priority}\n${description}`;
  }
  if (task.status) {
    description = `Status: ${task.status.replace('_', ' ')}\n${description}`;
  }
  if (description) {
    lines.push(`DESCRIPTION:${escapeICalText(description)}`);
  }

  // Date/Time
  if (task.due_date) {
    const dueDate = parseISO(task.due_date);
    if (isValid(dueDate)) {
      if (task.due_time) {
        // Has specific time - create 1 hour event
        const [hours, minutes] = task.due_time.split(':').map(Number);
        const startDate = new Date(dueDate);
        startDate.setHours(hours, minutes, 0, 0);
        const endDate = new Date(startDate);
        endDate.setHours(endDate.getHours() + 1);
        
        lines.push(`DTSTART:${formatICalDateTime(startDate)}`);
        lines.push(`DTEND:${formatICalDateTime(endDate)}`);
      } else {
        // All-day event
        lines.push(`DTSTART;VALUE=DATE:${formatICalDate(dueDate)}`);
        lines.push(`DTEND;VALUE=DATE:${formatICalDate(dueDate)}`);
      }
    }
  }

  // Created
  if (task.createdAt) {
    const created = parseISO(task.createdAt);
    if (isValid(created)) {
      lines.push(`CREATED:${formatICalDateTime(created)}`);
    }
  }

  // Categories
  const categories: string[] = [task.type];
  if (task.priority) categories.push(task.priority);
  if (task.status) categories.push(task.status);
  lines.push(`CATEGORIES:${categories.join(',')}`);

  // Recurrence rule
  if (task.recurring?.isRecurring && task.recurring.recurrenceRule) {
    const rrule = recurrenceToRRule(task.recurring.recurrenceRule);
    if (rrule) {
      lines.push(rrule);
    }
  }

  // Color hint based on priority
  const colorMap: Record<string, string> = {
    URGENT: '10',  // Red
    HIGH: '11',    // Orange
    MEDIUM: '5',   // Yellow
    LOW: '8',      // Gray
  };
  if (task.priority && colorMap[task.priority]) {
    lines.push(`X-APPLE-CALENDAR-COLOR:${colorMap[task.priority]}`);
  }

  lines.push('END:VEVENT');

  return lines.map(foldLine).join('\r\n');
}

/**
 * Generate a complete iCal file from tasks
 */
export function generateICalendar(
  tasks: (Task & { recurring?: RecurringTaskData })[],
  options: {
    productId?: string;
    calendarName?: string;
    useEvents?: boolean; // Use VEVENT instead of VTODO for better compatibility
  } = {}
): string {
  const {
    productId = '-//Lovable Calendar//Task Export//EN',
    calendarName = 'Lovable Tasks',
    useEvents = true, // Default to events for better compatibility
  } = options;

  const lines: string[] = [];

  // Calendar header
  lines.push('BEGIN:VCALENDAR');
  lines.push('VERSION:2.0');
  lines.push(`PRODID:${productId}`);
  lines.push('CALSCALE:GREGORIAN');
  lines.push('METHOD:PUBLISH');
  lines.push(`X-WR-CALNAME:${calendarName}`);
  lines.push('X-WR-TIMEZONE:UTC');

  // Generate components for each task
  tasks.forEach((task) => {
    if (useEvents) {
      lines.push(generateVEVENT(task));
    } else {
      lines.push(generateVTODO(task));
    }
  });

  // Calendar footer
  lines.push('END:VCALENDAR');

  return lines.join('\r\n');
}

/**
 * Export tasks to an .ics file and trigger download
 */
export function exportToICS(
  tasks: (Task & { recurring?: RecurringTaskData })[],
  filename: string = 'tasks.ics',
  options?: {
    productId?: string;
    calendarName?: string;
    useEvents?: boolean;
  }
): void {
  const icsContent = generateICalendar(tasks, options);
  
  // Create blob
  const blob = new Blob([icsContent], { type: 'text/calendar;charset=utf-8' });
  
  // Create download link
  const link = document.createElement('a');
  link.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  link.download = filename.endsWith('.ics') ? filename : `${filename}.ics`;
  
  // Trigger download
  document.body.appendChild(link);
  link.click();
  document.body.removeChild(link);
  
  // Cleanup
  URL.revokeObjectURL(link.href);
}

/**
 * Export a single task to .ics
 */
export function exportSingleTaskToICS(
  task: Task & { recurring?: RecurringTaskData },
  filename?: string
): void {
  const sanitizedTitle = task.title.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g, '_').substring(0, 50);
  const defaultFilename = `task_${sanitizedTitle}.ics`;
  exportToICS([task], filename || defaultFilename);
}

/**
 * Export filtered tasks to .ics
 */
export function exportFilteredTasksToICS(
  tasks: (Task & { recurring?: RecurringTaskData })[],
  filterName: string = 'filtered_tasks'
): void {
  const filename = `${filterName.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g, '_')}_${format(new Date(), 'yyyy-MM-dd')}.ics`;
  exportToICS(tasks, filename, {
    calendarName: `Lovable Tasks - ${filterName}`,
  });
}

FILE: E:\My Projects\Project-Management\sprintly-frontend\src\lib\recurrence.ts
==============================

/**
 * Recurrence utilities for recurring tasks
 * Handles recurrence rule generation, parsing, and date expansion
 */

import {
  addDays,
  addWeeks,
  addMonths,
  addYears,
  format,
  parseISO,
  isBefore,
  isAfter,
  startOfDay,
  endOfDay,
  getDay,
  setDay,
} from 'date-fns';

// Recurrence frequency types
export type RecurrenceFrequency =
  | 'daily'
  | 'weekly'
  | 'monthly'
  | 'yearly'
  | 'custom';

// Days of the week for weekly recurrence
export type DayOfWeek = 0 | 1 | 2 | 3 | 4 | 5 | 6; // Sun = 0, Sat = 6

// End condition types
export type RecurrenceEndType = 'never' | 'after' | 'on_date';

// Recurrence rule interface
export interface RecurrenceRule {
  frequency: RecurrenceFrequency;
  interval: number; // Every N days/weeks/months
  daysOfWeek?: DayOfWeek[]; // For weekly: which days
  dayOfMonth?: number; // For monthly: which day (1-31)
  monthOfYear?: number; // For yearly: which month (1-12)
  endType: RecurrenceEndType;
  endAfterOccurrences?: number; // If endType is 'after'
  endDate?: string; // If endType is 'on_date' (ISO string)
}

// Recurring task extension
export interface RecurringTaskData {
  isRecurring: boolean;
  recurrenceRule?: RecurrenceRule;
  parentTaskId?: string; // For instances, points to the original task
  instanceDate?: string; // The specific date this instance represents
  seriesId?: string; // Unique ID for the entire series
  excludedDates?: string[]; // Dates excluded from recurrence (when deleting single)
  modifiedInstances?: Record<string, Partial<ModifiedInstance>>; // Date key -> modifications
}

export interface ModifiedInstance {
  title?: string;
  description?: string;
  due_time?: string;
  status?: string;
  priority?: string;
}

// Day of week labels
export const DAY_LABELS = [
  'Sun',
  'Mon',
  'Tue',
  'Wed',
  'Thu',
  'Fri',
  'Sat',
] as const;

// Default recurrence presets
export const RECURRENCE_PRESETS = {
  daily: {
    label: 'Daily',
    rule: {
      frequency: 'daily' as const,
      interval: 1,
      endType: 'never' as const,
    },
  },
  weekdays: {
    label: 'Every Weekday',
    rule: {
      frequency: 'weekly' as const,
      interval: 1,
      daysOfWeek: [1, 2, 3, 4, 5] as DayOfWeek[],
      endType: 'never' as const,
    },
  },
  weekly: {
    label: 'Weekly',
    rule: {
      frequency: 'weekly' as const,
      interval: 1,
      endType: 'never' as const,
    },
  },
  biweekly: {
    label: 'Every 2 Weeks',
    rule: {
      frequency: 'weekly' as const,
      interval: 2,
      endType: 'never' as const,
    },
  },
  monthly: {
    label: 'Monthly',
    rule: {
      frequency: 'monthly' as const,
      interval: 1,
      endType: 'never' as const,
    },
  },
  yearly: {
    label: 'Yearly',
    rule: {
      frequency: 'yearly' as const,
      interval: 1,
      endType: 'never' as const,
    },
  },
};

/**
 * Generate a human-readable description of a recurrence rule
 */
export function getRecurrenceDescription(rule: RecurrenceRule): string {
  let desc = '';

  switch (rule.frequency) {
    case 'daily':
      desc = rule.interval === 1 ? 'Daily' : `Every ${rule.interval} days`;
      break;
    case 'weekly':
      if (rule.daysOfWeek && rule.daysOfWeek.length > 0) {
        const days = rule.daysOfWeek.map((d) => DAY_LABELS[d]).join(', ');
        desc =
          rule.interval === 1
            ? `Weekly on ${days}`
            : `Every ${rule.interval} weeks on ${days}`;
      } else {
        desc = rule.interval === 1 ? 'Weekly' : `Every ${rule.interval} weeks`;
      }
      break;
    case 'monthly':
      desc = rule.interval === 1 ? 'Monthly' : `Every ${rule.interval} months`;
      if (rule.dayOfMonth) {
        desc += ` on day ${rule.dayOfMonth}`;
      }
      break;
    case 'yearly':
      desc = rule.interval === 1 ? 'Yearly' : `Every ${rule.interval} years`;
      break;
    case 'custom':
      desc = 'Custom schedule';
      break;
  }

  // Add end condition
  switch (rule.endType) {
    case 'after':
      desc += `, ${rule.endAfterOccurrences} times`;
      break;
    case 'on_date':
      if (rule.endDate) {
        desc += `, until ${format(parseISO(rule.endDate), 'MMM d, yyyy')}`;
      }
      break;
    case 'never':
    default:
      break;
  }

  return desc;
}

/**
 * Generate occurrence dates for a recurring task within a date range
 */
export function generateOccurrences(
  startDate: Date,
  rule: RecurrenceRule,
  rangeStart: Date,
  rangeEnd: Date,
  excludedDates: string[] = [],
  maxOccurrences: number = 100,
): Date[] {
  const occurrences: Date[] = [];
  let currentDate = startOfDay(startDate);
  let occurrenceCount = 0;

  // Determine the effective end based on rule
  let effectiveEnd = rangeEnd;
  if (rule.endType === 'on_date' && rule.endDate) {
    const ruleEndDate = parseISO(rule.endDate);
    if (isBefore(ruleEndDate, effectiveEnd)) {
      effectiveEnd = ruleEndDate;
    }
  }

  const maxCount =
    rule.endType === 'after' && rule.endAfterOccurrences
      ? Math.min(rule.endAfterOccurrences, maxOccurrences)
      : maxOccurrences;

  const excludedSet = new Set(excludedDates);

  while (occurrences.length < maxCount && !isAfter(currentDate, effectiveEnd)) {
    // Check if within range and not excluded
    if (!isBefore(currentDate, rangeStart) && !isAfter(currentDate, rangeEnd)) {
      const dateKey = format(currentDate, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
      if (!excludedSet.has(dateKey)) {
        // For weekly with specific days, check if current day matches
        if (
          rule.frequency === 'weekly' &&
          rule.daysOfWeek &&
          rule.daysOfWeek.length > 0
        ) {
          if (rule.daysOfWeek.includes(getDay(currentDate) as DayOfWeek)) {
            occurrences.push(new Date(currentDate));
            occurrenceCount++;
          }
        } else {
          occurrences.push(new Date(currentDate));
          occurrenceCount++;
        }
      }
    }

    // Move to next occurrence
    currentDate = getNextOccurrence(currentDate, rule);

    // Safety check for end conditions
    if (rule.endType === 'after' && occurrenceCount >= maxCount) {
      break;
    }
  }

  return occurrences;
}

/**
 * Get the next occurrence date based on the recurrence rule
 */
function getNextOccurrence(currentDate: Date, rule: RecurrenceRule): Date {
  switch (rule.frequency) {
    case 'daily':
      return addDays(currentDate, rule.interval);

    case 'weekly':
      if (rule.daysOfWeek && rule.daysOfWeek.length > 0) {
        // Find next matching day of week
        let nextDate = addDays(currentDate, 1);
        let weeksToAdd = 0;
        let daysChecked = 0;

        while (daysChecked < 7 * rule.interval) {
          if (rule.daysOfWeek.includes(getDay(nextDate) as DayOfWeek)) {
            // Check if we've completed an interval
            const daysDiff = Math.floor(
              (nextDate.getTime() - currentDate.getTime()) /
                (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24),
            );
            if (daysDiff >= rule.interval * 7 || daysChecked < 7) {
              return nextDate;
            }
          }
          nextDate = addDays(nextDate, 1);
          daysChecked++;
        }
        return addWeeks(currentDate, rule.interval);
      }
      return addWeeks(currentDate, rule.interval);

    case 'monthly':
      return addMonths(currentDate, rule.interval);

    case 'yearly':
      return addYears(currentDate, rule.interval);

    case 'custom':
    default:
      return addDays(currentDate, rule.interval);
  }
}

/**
 * Create a default recurrence rule
 */
export function createDefaultRecurrenceRule(): RecurrenceRule {
  return {
    frequency: 'weekly',
    interval: 1,
    endType: 'never',
  };
}

/**
 * Validate a recurrence rule
 */
export function validateRecurrenceRule(rule: RecurrenceRule): string[] {
  const errors: string[] = [];

  if (rule.interval < 1) {
    errors.push('Interval must be at least 1');
  }

  if (rule.interval > 365) {
    errors.push('Interval cannot exceed 365');
  }

  if (rule.frequency === 'weekly' && rule.daysOfWeek) {
    if (rule.daysOfWeek.some((d) => d < 0 || d > 6)) {
      errors.push('Invalid day of week');
    }
  }

  if (rule.frequency === 'monthly' && rule.dayOfMonth) {
    if (rule.dayOfMonth < 1 || rule.dayOfMonth > 31) {
      errors.push('Day of month must be between 1 and 31');
    }
  }

  if (
    rule.endType === 'after' &&
    (!rule.endAfterOccurrences || rule.endAfterOccurrences < 1)
  ) {
    errors.push('Number of occurrences must be at least 1');
  }

  if (rule.endType === 'on_date' && !rule.endDate) {
    errors.push('End date is required');
  }

  return errors;
}

/**
 * Generate a unique series ID
 */
export function generateSeriesId(): string {
  return `series_${Date.now()}_${Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9)}`;
}

import { clsx, type ClassValue } from "clsx"
import { twMerge } from "tailwind-merge"

export function cn(...inputs: ClassValue[]) {
  return twMerge(clsx(inputs))
}

import { useState } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import {
  Mail,
  Lock,
  User,
  ArrowRight,
  Loader2,
  Eye,
  EyeOff,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { useWorkspaceStore } from '@/store/workspaceStore';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Label } from '@/components/ui/label';

import { z } from 'zod';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { toast } from 'sonner';

const loginSchema = z.object({
  email: z
    .string()
    .trim()
    .email({ message: 'Please enter a valid email address' }),
  password: z
    .string()
    .min(6, { message: 'Password must be at least 6 characters' }),
});

const signupSchema = z
  .object({
    name: z
      .string()
      .trim()
      .min(2, { message: 'Name must be at least 2 characters' })
      .max(50, { message: 'Name must be less than 50 characters' }),
    email: z
      .string()
      .trim()
      .email({ message: 'Please enter a valid email address' }),
    password: z
      .string()
      .min(6, { message: 'Password must be at least 6 characters' }),
    confirmPassword: z.string(),
  })
  .refine((data) => data.password === data.confirmPassword, {
    message: "Passwords don't match",
    path: ['confirmPassword'],
  });

type LoginFormData = z.infer<typeof loginSchema>;
type SignupFormData = z.infer<typeof signupSchema>;

export default function Auth() {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const { login, signup, auth } = useWorkspaceStore();
  const [isLogin, setIsLogin] = useState(true);
  const [showPassword, setShowPassword] = useState(false);
  const [errors, setErrors] = useState<Record<string, string>>({});

  // Login form state
  const [loginData, setLoginData] = useState<LoginFormData>({
    email: '',
    password: '',
  });

  // Signup form state
  const [signupData, setSignupData] = useState<SignupFormData>({
    name: '',
    email: '',
    password: '',
    confirmPassword: '',
  });

  const handleLogin = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setErrors({});

    const result = loginSchema.safeParse(loginData);
    if (!result.success) {
      const fieldErrors: Record<string, string> = {};
      result.error.errors.forEach((err) => {
        if (err.path[0]) {
          fieldErrors[err.path[0].toString()] = err.message;
        }
      });
      setErrors(fieldErrors);
      return;
    }

    try {
      const success = await login(loginData.email, loginData.password);
      if (success) {
        toast.success('Welcome back!', {
          description: 'You have successfully logged in.',
        });
        navigate('/');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      toast.error('Login failed', {
        description: 'Please check your credentials and try again.',
      });
    }
  };

  const handleSignup = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setErrors({});

    const result = signupSchema.safeParse(signupData);
    if (!result.success) {
      const fieldErrors: Record<string, string> = {};
      result.error.errors.forEach((err) => {
        if (err.path[0]) {
          fieldErrors[err.path[0].toString()] = err.message;
        }
      });
      setErrors(fieldErrors);
      return;
    }

    try {
      const success = await signup(
        signupData.name,
        signupData.email,
        signupData.password,
      );
      if (success) {
        toast({
          title: 'Account created!',
          description: 'Welcome to sprintly.',
        });
        navigate('/');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      toast({
        title: 'Signup failed',
        description: 'Please try again later.',
        variant: 'destructive',
      });
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className='min-h-screen flex bg-background'>
      {/* Left Side - Branding */}
      <div className='hidden lg:flex lg:w-1/2 bg-gradient-to-br from-primary/20 via-primary/10 to-background p-12 flex-col justify-between relative overflow-hidden'>
        <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[url('data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20width%3D%2260%22%20height%3D%2260%22%20viewBox%3D%220%200%2060%2060%22%20xmlns%3D%22http%3A%2F%2Fwww.w3.org%2F2000%2Fsvg%22%3E%3Cg%20fill%3D%22none%22%20fill-rule%3D%22evenodd%22%3E%3Cg%20fill%3D%22%239C92AC%22%20fill-opacity%3D%220.05%22%3E%3Cpath%20d%3D%22M36%2034v-4h-2v4h-4v2h4v4h2v-4h4v-2h-4zm0-30V0h-2v4h-4v2h4v4h2V6h4V4h-4zM6%2034v-4H4v4H0v2h4v4h2v-4h4v-2H6zM6%204V0H4v4H0v2h4v4h2V6h4V4H6z%22%2F%3E%3C%2Fg%3E%3C%2Fg%3E%3C%2Fsvg%3E')] opacity-50" />

        <div className='relative z-10'>
          <motion.div
            initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
            transition={{ delay: 0.2 }}
          >
            <h1 className='text-4xl font-bold text-foreground mb-2'>
              sprintly
            </h1>
            <p className='text-muted-foreground'>Modern Project Management</p>
          </motion.div>
        </div>

        <motion.div
          initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
          animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
          transition={{ delay: 0.4 }}
          className='relative z-10 space-y-8'
        >
          <div className='space-y-4'>
            <FeatureItem

            />

              title='Gantt Charts'

        <motion.p
          initial={{ opacity: 0 }}

          className='relative z-10 text-sm text-muted-foreground'
        >
          © 2024 sprintly. All rights reserved.
        </motion.p>
      </div>

      {/* Right Side - Auth Form */}
      <div className='flex-1 flex items-center justify-center p-8'>
        <motion.div
          initial={{ opacity: 0, x: 20 }}

          className='w-full max-w-md'
        >
          {/* Mobile Logo */}
          <div className='lg:hidden mb-8 text-center'>
            <h1 className='text-3xl font-bold text-foreground'>sprintly</h1>
            <p className='text-muted-foreground'>Modern Project Management</p>
          </div>

          {/* Tab Switcher */}
          <div className='flex gap-1 p-1 bg-secondary/50 rounded-lg mb-8'>
            <button
              onClick={() => setIsLogin(true)}
              className={cn(
                'flex-1 py-2.5 px-4 rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all',

            >
              Sign In

            <button

              className={cn(
                'flex-1 py-2.5 px-4 rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all',
                !isLogin
                  ? 'bg-background text-foreground shadow-sm'
                  : 'text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground',
              )}
            >
              Sign Up

          </div>

          <AnimatePresence mode='wait'>
            {isLogin ? (

                initial={{ opacity: 0, x: -20 }}
                animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
                exit={{ opacity: 0, x: 20 }}
                onSubmit={handleLogin}

                        value={loginData.email}

                          setLoginData({ ...loginData, email: e.target.value })

                        className={cn(

                    {errors.confirmPassword && (
                      <p className='text-xs text-destructive'>
                        {errors.confirmPassword}
                      </p>
                    )}
                  </div>
                </div>

                <Button
                  type='submit'
                  className='w-full'
                  disabled={auth.isLoading}
                >
                  {auth.isLoading ? (
                    <Loader2 className='w-4 h-4 mr-2 animate-spin' />
                  ) : (
                    <ArrowRight className='w-4 h-4 mr-2' />
                  )}
                  Create Account
                </Button>

                <p className='text-center text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                  By signing up, you agree to our{' '}
                  <button
                    type='button'
                    className='text-primary hover:underline'
                  >
                    Terms of Service
                  </button>{' '}
                  and{' '}
                  <button
                    type='button'
                    className='text-primary hover:underline'
                  >
                    Privacy Policy
                  </button>
                </p>
              </motion.form>
            )}
          </AnimatePresence>
        </motion.div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function FeatureItem({
  title,
  description,
}: {
  title: string;
  description: string;
}) {
  return (
    <div className='flex items-start gap-3'>
      <div className='w-8 h-8 rounded-lg bg-primary/20 flex items-center justify-center flex-shrink-0 mt-0.5'>
        <ArrowRight className='w-4 h-4 text-primary' />
      </div>
      <div>
        <h3 className='font-medium text-foreground'>{title}</h3>
        <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>{description}</p>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import { useLocation } from 'react-router-dom';
import { useEffect } from 'react';

const NotFound = () => {
  const location = useLocation();

  useEffect(() => {
    console.error(
      '404 Error: User attempted to access non-existent route:',
      location.pathname,
    );
  }, [location.pathname]);

  return (
    <div className='flex min-h-screen items-center justify-center bg-muted'>
      <div className='text-center'>
        <h1 className='mb-4 text-4xl font-bold'>404</h1>
        <p className='mb-4 text-xl text-muted-foreground'>
          Oops! Page not found
        </p>
        <a href='/' className='text-primary underline hover:text-primary/90'>
          Return to Home
        </a>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default NotFound;


==============================
FILE: E:\My Projects\Project-Management\sprintly-frontend\src\pages\ProjectDetails.tsx
==============================

import { useState, useMemo } from 'react';
import { useParams, useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { motion } from 'framer-motion';
import {
  ArrowLeft,
  Plus,
  BarChart3,
  Calendar,
  List,
  Settings,
  Clock,
  CheckCircle2,
  AlertTriangle,
  LayoutGrid,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { type Task, useWorkspaceStore } from '@/store/workspaceStore';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import CreateTaskDialog from '@/components/dialogs/CreateTaskDialog';
import KanbanBoard from '@/components/kanban/KanbanBoard';
import TaskDetailModal from '@/components/dialogs/TaskDetailModal';
import TaskCalendar from '@/components/calendar/TaskCalendar';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { format, isBefore, isValid, parseISO } from 'date-fns';

// Helper to safely parse and validate dates
const safeParseDate = (dateString: string | undefined | null): Date | null => {
  if (!dateString) return null;
  const date = parseISO(dateString);
  return isValid(date) ? date : null;
};

const statusColors: Record<string, string> = {
  TODO: 'bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground',
  IN_PROGRESS: 'bg-warning/20 text-warning',
  REVIEW: 'bg-primary/20 text-primary',
  DONE: 'bg-success/20 text-success',
};

const priorityColors: Record<string, string> = {
  LOW: 'border-l-muted-foreground',
  MEDIUM: 'border-l-warning',
  HIGH: 'border-l-destructive',
  URGENT: 'border-l-destructive',
};

const typeColors: Record<string, string> = {
  BUG: 'bg-destructive/10 text-destructive',
  FEATURE: 'bg-primary/10 text-primary',
  TASK: 'bg-success/10 text-success',
  IMPROVEMENT: 'bg-violet-500/10 text-violet-500',
  OTHER: 'bg-warning/10 text-warning',
};

type TabType = 'tasks' | 'analytics' | 'calendar' | 'settings';
type TaskViewType = 'list' | 'board';

export default function ProjectDetails() {
  const { id } = useParams();
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const { currentWorkspace, updateTask } = useWorkspaceStore();

  const project = currentWorkspace?.projects.find((p) => p.id === id);
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState<TabType>('tasks');
  const [taskView, setTaskView] = useState<TaskViewType>('board');
  const [showCreateTask, setShowCreateTask] = useState(false);
  const [selectedTask, setSelectedTask] = useState<Task | null>(null);
  const [statusFilter, setStatusFilter] = useState<string>('');
  const [typeFilter, setTypeFilter] = useState<string>('');

  const tasks = project?.tasks || [];
  const now = new Date();

  const filteredTasks = useMemo(() => {
    return tasks.filter((task) => {
      const matchesStatus = !statusFilter || task.status === statusFilter;
      const matchesType = !typeFilter || task.type === typeFilter;
      return matchesStatus && matchesType;
    });
  }, [tasks, statusFilter, typeFilter]);

  const stats = useMemo(
    () => ({
      total: tasks.length,
      completed: tasks.filter((t) => t.status === 'DONE').length,
      inProgress: tasks.filter((t) => t.status === 'IN_PROGRESS').length,
      todo: tasks.filter((t) => t.status === 'TODO').length,
      overdue: tasks.filter((t) => {
        const dueDate = safeParseDate(t.due_date);
        return dueDate && isBefore(dueDate, now) && t.status !== 'DONE';
      }).length,
    }),
    [tasks],
  );

  const handleStatusChange = (
    taskId: string,
    newStatus: 'TODO' | 'IN_PROGRESS' | 'DONE',
  ) => {
    const task = tasks.find((t) => t.id === taskId);
    if (task) {
      updateTask({
        ...task,
        status: newStatus,
        updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      });
    }
  };

  if (!project) {
    return (
      <div className='text-center py-16'>
        <p className='text-muted-foreground mb-4'>Project not found</p>
        <Button onClick={() => navigate('/projects')}>Back to Projects</Button>
      </div>
    );
  }

  const tabs: { id: TabType; label: string; icon: typeof List }[] = [
    { id: 'tasks', label: 'Tasks', icon: List },
    { id: 'analytics', label: 'Analytics', icon: BarChart3 },
    { id: 'calendar', label: 'Calendar', icon: Calendar },
    { id: 'settings', label: 'Settings', icon: Settings },
  ];

  return (
    <div className='space-y-6'>
      {/* Header */}
      <motion.div
        initial={{ opacity: 0, y: -20 }}
        animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
        className='flex flex-col gap-4'
      >
        <button
          onClick={() => navigate('/projects')}
          className='flex items-center gap-2 text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground transition-colors w-fit'
        >
          <ArrowLeft className='w-4 h-4' />
          Back to Projects
        </button>

        <div className='flex flex-col sm:flex-row sm:items-start sm:justify-between gap-4'>
          <div>
            <h1 className='text-2xl md:text-3xl font-bold text-foreground'>
              {project.name}
            </h1>
            <p className='text-muted-foreground mt-1 max-w-2xl'>
              {project.description}
            </p>
          </div>
          <Button
            onClick={() => setShowCreateTask(true)}
            className='bg-primary hover:bg-primary/90 text-primary-foreground'
          >
            <Plus className='w-4 h-4 mr-2' />
            Add Task
          </Button>
        </div>
      </motion.div>

      {/* Quick Stats */}
      <motion.div
        initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
        animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
        transition={{ delay: 0.1 }}
        className='grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-4 gap-4'
      >
        {[
          {
            label: 'Completed',
            value: stats.completed,
            icon: CheckCircle2,
            color: 'text-success',
          },
          {
            label: 'In Progress',
            value: stats.inProgress,
            icon: Clock,
            color: 'text-warning',
          },
          {
            label: 'To Do',
            value: stats.todo,
            icon: List,
            color: 'text-primary',
          },
          {
            label: 'Overdue',
            value: stats.overdue,
            icon: AlertTriangle,
            color: 'text-destructive',
          },
        ].map((stat) => (
          <div key={stat.label} className='glass-card p-4'>
            <div className='flex items-center gap-3'>
              <stat.icon className={cn('w-5 h-5', stat.color)} />
              <div>
                <p className='text-2xl font-bold text-foreground'>
                  {stat.value}
                </p>
                <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>{stat.label}</p>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </motion.div>

      {/* Tabs */}
      <motion.div
        initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
        animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
        transition={{ delay: 0.2 }}
        className='flex items-center gap-2 border-b border-border pb-4 overflow-x-auto'
      >
        {tabs.map((tab) => (
          <button
            key={tab.id}
            onClick={() => setActiveTab(tab.id)}
            className={cn(
              'flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm font-medium transition-all',
              activeTab === tab.id
                ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground'
                : 'text-muted-foreground hover:bg-secondary hover:text-foreground',
            )}
          >
            <tab.icon className='w-4 h-4' />
            {tab.label}
          </button>
        ))}
      </motion.div>

      {/* Tab Content */}
      {activeTab === 'tasks' && (
        <motion.div
          initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
          animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
          className='space-y-4'
        >
          {/* View Toggle & Filters */}
          <div className='flex flex-wrap items-center justify-between gap-3'>
            <div className='flex flex-wrap gap-3'>
              <select
                value={statusFilter}
                onChange={(e) => setStatusFilter(e.target.value)}
                className='px-3 py-2 rounded-lg bg-secondary/50 border border-border text-sm'
              >
                <option value=''>All Status</option>
                <option value='TODO'>To Do</option>
                <option value='IN_PROGRESS'>In Progress</option>
                <option value='REVIEW'>Review</option>
                <option value='DONE'>Done</option>
              </select>
              <select
                value={typeFilter}
                onChange={(e) => setTypeFilter(e.target.value)}
                className='px-3 py-2 rounded-lg bg-secondary/50 border border-border text-sm'
              >
                <option value=''>All Types</option>
                <option value='TASK'>Task</option>
                <option value='BUG'>Bug</option>
                <option value='FEATURE'>Feature</option>
                <option value='IMPROVEMENT'>Improvement</option>
              </select>
            </div>

            {/* View Toggle */}
            <div className='flex items-center gap-1 p-1 bg-secondary/50 rounded-lg'>
              <button
                onClick={() => setTaskView('list')}
                className={cn(
                  'flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all',
                  taskView === 'list'
                    ? 'bg-background text-foreground shadow-sm'
                    : 'text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground',
                )}
              >
                <List className='w-4 h-4' />
                List
              </button>
              <button
                onClick={() => setTaskView('board')}
                className={cn(
                  'flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all',
                  taskView === 'board'
                    ? 'bg-background text-foreground shadow-sm'
                    : 'text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground',
                )}
              >
                <LayoutGrid className='w-4 h-4' />
                Board
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Kanban Board View */}
          {taskView === 'board' && (
            <KanbanBoard
              projectId={project.id}
              onTaskClick={(task) => setSelectedTask(task)}
            />
          )}

          {/* List View */}
          {taskView === 'list' && (
            <>
              {filteredTasks.length === 0 ? (
                <div className='text-center py-16'>
                  <p className='text-muted-foreground mb-4'>No tasks found</p>
                  <Button onClick={() => setShowCreateTask(true)}>
                    Create your first task
                  </Button>
                </div>
              ) : (
                <div className='space-y-3'>
                  {filteredTasks.map((task, index) => {
                    const dueDate = safeParseDate(task.due_date);
                    const isOverdue =
                      dueDate &&
                      isBefore(dueDate, now) &&
                      task.status !== 'DONE';

                    return (
                      <motion.div
                        key={task.id}
                        initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
                        animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                        transition={{ delay: index * 0.03 }}
                        onClick={() => setSelectedTask(task)}
                        className={cn(
                          'glass-card p-4 border-l-2 transition-all hover:shadow-lg cursor-pointer',
                          priorityColors[task.priority],
                        )}
                      >
                        <div className='flex flex-col sm:flex-row sm:items-center gap-4'>
                          <div className='flex-1 min-w-0'>
                            <div className='flex items-center gap-2 mb-1'>
                              <h3 className='font-medium text-foreground truncate'>
                                {task.title}
                              </h3>
                              <span
                                className={cn(
                                  'px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-[10px] font-medium',
                                  typeColors[task.type],
                                )}
                              >
                                {task.type}
                              </span>
                            </div>
                            <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground line-clamp-1'>
                              {task.description}
                            </p>
                          </div>

                          <div className='flex items-center gap-3 flex-shrink-0'>
                            {/* Assignee */}
                            <div
                              className='w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-gradient-to-br from-primary to-cyan-400 flex items-center justify-center text-xs font-medium text-primary-foreground'
                              title={task.assignee?.name}
                            >
                              {task.assignee?.name?.charAt(0) || '?'}
                            </div>

                            {/* Due Date */}
                            {dueDate && (
                              <span
                                className={cn(
                                  'text-xs flex items-center gap-1',
                                  isOverdue
                                    ? 'text-destructive'
                                    : 'text-muted-foreground',
                                )}
                              >
                                <Calendar className='w-3.5 h-3.5' />
                                {format(dueDate, 'MMM d')}
                              </span>
                            )}

                            {/* Status Dropdown */}
                            <select
                              value={task.status}
                              onChange={(e) =>
                                handleStatusChange(
                                  task.id,
                                  e.target.value as any,
                                )
                              }
                              className={cn(
                                'px-2 py-1 rounded text-xs font-medium border-0 cursor-pointer',
                                statusColors[task.status],
                              )}
                            >
                              <option value='TODO'>To Do</option>
                              <option value='IN_PROGRESS'>In Progress</option>
                              <option value='REVIEW'>Review</option>
                              <option value='DONE'>Done</option>
                            </select>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      </motion.div>
                    );
                  })}
                </div>
              )}
            </>
          )}
        </motion.div>
      )}

      {activeTab === 'analytics' && (
        <motion.div
          initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
          animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
          className='grid md:grid-cols-2 gap-6'
        >
          {/* Completion Rate */}
          <div className='glass-card p-6'>
            <h3 className='font-medium text-foreground mb-4'>
              Completion Rate
            </h3>
            <div className='text-center'>
              <div className='text-5xl font-bold text-primary mb-2'>
                {stats.total > 0
                  ? Math.round((stats.completed / stats.total) * 100)
                  : 0}
                %
              </div>
              <p className='text-muted-foreground'>
                {stats.completed} of {stats.total} tasks completed
              </p>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Team */}
          <div className='glass-card p-6'>
            <h3 className='font-medium text-foreground mb-4'>Team Members</h3>
            <div className='space-y-3'>
              {project.members.map((member) => (
                <div key={member.id} className='flex items-center gap-3'>
                  <div className='w-10 h-10 rounded-full bg-gradient-to-br from-primary to-cyan-400 flex items-center justify-center text-sm font-medium text-primary-foreground'>
                    {member.user.name.charAt(0)}
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    <p className='font-medium text-foreground'>
                      {member.user.name}
                    </p>
                    <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>
                      {member.user.email}
                    </p>
                  </div>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        </motion.div>
      )}

      {activeTab === 'calendar' && (
        <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }}>
          <TaskCalendar
            tasks={tasks}
            onTaskClick={(task) => setSelectedTask(task)}
          />
        </motion.div>
      )}

      {activeTab === 'settings' && (
        <motion.div
          initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
          animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
          className='glass-card p-6'
        >
          <h3 className='font-medium text-foreground mb-4'>Project Settings</h3>
          <div className='space-y-4'>
            <div>
              <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>Project Name</p>
              <p className='text-foreground'>{project.name}</p>
            </div>
            <div>
              <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>Status</p>
              <p className='text-foreground'>{project.status}</p>
            </div>
            <div>
              <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>Priority</p>
              <p className='text-foreground'>{project.priority}</p>
            </div>
            <div>
              <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>Created</p>
              <p className='text-foreground'>
                {format(new Date(project.createdAt), 'MMMM d, yyyy')}
              </p>
            </div>
          </div>
        </motion.div>
      )}

      <CreateTaskDialog
        open={showCreateTask}
        onOpenChange={setShowCreateTask}
        projectId={project.id}
      />

      {selectedTask && (
        <TaskDetailModal
          task={selectedTask}
          projectId={project.id}
          isOpen={!!selectedTask}
          onClose={() => setSelectedTask(null)}
        />
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

FILE: E:\My Projects\Project-Management\sprintly-frontend\src\pages\Projects.tsx
